41006012	They went out and preached that people should repent .
41006013	They drove out many demons and anointed many sick people with oil and healed them .
41006014	King Herod heard about this , for Jesus' name had become well known . Some were saying , " John the Baptist has been raised from the dead , and that is why miraculous powers are at work in him . "
41006015	Others said , " He is Elijah . " And still others claimed , " He is a prophet , like one of the prophets of long ago . "
41006016	But when Herod heard this , he said , " John , whom I beheaded , has been raised from the dead ! "
41006017	For Herod himself had given orders to have John arrested , and he had him bound and put in prison . He did this because of Herodias , his brother Philip's wife , whom he had married .
41006018	For John had been saying to Herod , " It is not lawful for you to have your brother's wife . "
41006019	So Herodias nursed a grudge against John and wanted to kill him . But she was not able to ,
41006020	because Herod feared John and protected him , knowing him to be a righteous and holy man . When Herod heard John , he was greatly puzzled ; yet he liked to listen to him .
41006021	Finally the opportune time came . On his birthday Herod gave a banquet for his high officials and military commanders and the leading men of Galilee .
41006022	When the daughter of Herodias came in and danced , she pleased Herod and his dinner guests . The king said to the girl , " Ask me for anything you want , and I'll give it to you . "
41006023	And he promised her with an oath , " Whatever you ask I will give you , up to half my kingdom . "
41006024	She went out and said to her mother , " What shall I ask for ? " " The head of John the Baptist , " she answered .
41006025	At once the girl hurried in to the king with the request : " I want you to give me right now the head of John the Baptist on a platter . "
41006026	The king was greatly distressed , but because of his oaths and his dinner guests , he did not want to refuse her .
41006027	So he immediately sent an executioner with orders to bring John's head . The man went , beheaded John in the prison ,
41006028	and brought back his head on a platter . He presented it to the girl , and she gave it to her mother .
41006029	On hearing of this , John's disciples came and took his body and laid it in a tomb .
41006030	The apostles gathered around Jesus and reported to him all they had done and taught .
41006031	Then , because so many people were coming and going that they did not even have a chance to eat , he said to them , " Come with me by yourselves to a quiet place and get some rest . "
41006032	So they went away by themselves in a boat to a solitary place .
41006033	But many who saw them leaving recognized them and ran on foot from all the towns and got there ahead of them .
41006034	When Jesus landed and saw a large crowd , he had compassion on them , because they were like sheep without a shepherd . So he began teaching them many things .
41006035	By this time it was late in the day , so his disciples came to him . " This is a remote place , " they said , " and it's already very late .
41006036	Send the people away so that they can go to the surrounding countryside and villages and buy themselves something to eat . "
41006037	But he answered , " You give them something to eat . " They said to him , " That would take more than half a year's wages ! Are we to go and spend that much on bread and give it to them to eat ? "
41006038	" How many loaves do you have ? " he asked . " Go and see . " When they found out , they said , " Five — and two fish . "
41006039	Then Jesus directed them to have all the people sit down in groups on the green grass .
41006040	So they sat down in groups of hundreds and fifties .
41006041	Taking the five loaves and the two fish and looking up to heaven , he gave thanks and broke the loaves . Then he gave them to his disciples to distribute to the people . He also divided the two fish among them all .
41006042	They all ate and were satisfied ,
41006043	and the disciples picked up twelve basketfuls of broken pieces of bread and fish .
41006044	The number of the men who had eaten was five thousand .
41006045	Immediately Jesus made his disciples get into the boat and go on ahead of him to Bethsaida , while he dismissed the crowd .
41006046	After leaving them , he went up on a mountainside to pray .
41006047	Later that night , the boat was in the middle of the lake , and he was alone on land .
41006048	He saw the disciples straining at the oars , because the wind was against them . Shortly before dawn he went out to them , walking on the lake . He was about to pass by them ,
41006049	but when they saw him walking on the lake , they thought he was a ghost . They cried out ,
41006050	because they all saw him and were terrified . Immediately he spoke to them and said , " Take courage ! It is I . Don't be afraid . "
41006051	Then he climbed into the boat with them , and the wind died down . They were completely amazed ,
41006052	for they had not understood about the loaves ; their hearts were hardened .
41006053	When they had crossed over , they landed at Gennesaret and anchored there .
41006054	As soon as they got out of the boat , people recognized Jesus .
41006055	They ran throughout that whole region and carried the sick on mats to wherever they heard he was .
41006056	And wherever he went — into villages , towns or countryside — they placed the sick in the marketplaces . They begged him to let them touch even the edge of his cloak , and all who touched it were healed .
41007001	The Pharisees and some of the teachers of the law who had come from Jerusalem gathered around Jesus
41007002	and saw some of his disciples eating food with hands that were defiled , that is , unwashed .
41007003	( The Pharisees and all the Jews do not eat unless they give their hands a ceremonial washing , holding to the tradition of the elders .
41007004	When they come from the marketplace they do not eat unless they wash . And they observe many other traditions , such as the washing of cups , pitchers and kettles . )
41007005	So the Pharisees and teachers of the law asked Jesus , " Why don't your disciples live according to the tradition of the elders instead of eating their food with defiled hands ? "
41007006	He replied , " Isaiah was right when he prophesied about you hypocrites ; as it is written :
41007007	They worship me in vain ;
41007008	You have let go of the commands of God and are holding on to human traditions . "
41007009	And he continued , " You have a fine way of setting aside the commands of God in order to observe your own traditions !
41007010	For Moses said , ' Honor your father and mother , ' and , ' Anyone who curses their father or mother is to be put to death . '
41007011	But you say that if anyone declares that what might have been used to help their father or mother is Corban ( that is , devoted to God ) —
41007012	then you no longer let them do anything for their father or mother .
41007013	Thus you nullify the word of God by your tradition that you have handed down . And you do many things like that . "
41007014	Again Jesus called the crowd to him and said , " Listen to me , everyone , and understand this .
41007015	Nothing outside a person can defile them by going into them . Rather , it is what comes out of a person that defiles them . "
41007017	After he had left the crowd and entered the house , his disciples asked him about this parable .
41007018	" Are you so dull ? " he asked . " Don't you see that nothing that enters a person from the outside can defile them ?
41007019	For it doesn't go into their heart but into their stomach , and then out of the body . " ( In saying this , Jesus declared all foods clean . )
41007020	He went on : " What comes out of a person is what defiles them .
41007021	For it is from within , out of a person's heart , that evil thoughts come — sexual immorality , theft , murder ,
41007022	adultery , greed , malice , deceit , lewdness , envy , slander , arrogance and folly .
41007023	All these evils come from inside and defile a person . "
41007024	Jesus left that place and went to the vicinity of Tyre . He entered a house and did not want anyone to know it ; yet he could not keep his presence secret .
41007025	In fact , as soon as she heard about him , a woman whose little daughter was possessed by an impure spirit came and fell at his feet .
41007026	The woman was a Greek , born in Syrian Phoenicia . She begged Jesus to drive the demon out of her daughter .
41007027	" First let the children eat all they want , " he told her , " for it is not right to take the children's bread and toss it to the dogs . "
41007028	" Lord , " she replied , " even the dogs under the table eat the children's crumbs . "
41007029	Then he told her , " For such a reply , you may go ; the demon has left your daughter . "
41007030	She went home and found her child lying on the bed , and the demon gone .
41007031	Then Jesus left the vicinity of Tyre and went through Sidon , down to the Sea of Galilee and into the region of the Decapolis .
41007032	There some people brought to him a man who was deaf and could hardly talk , and they begged Jesus to place his hand on him .
41007033	After he took him aside , away from the crowd , Jesus put his fingers into the man's ears . Then he spit and touched the man's tongue .
41007034	He looked up to heaven and with a deep sigh said to him , " Ephphatha ! " ( which means " Be opened ! " ) .
41007035	At this , the man's ears were opened , his tongue was loosened and he began to speak plainly .
41007036	Jesus commanded them not to tell anyone . But the more he did so , the more they kept talking about it .
41007037	People were overwhelmed with amazement . " He has done everything well , " they said . " He even makes the deaf hear and the mute speak . "
41008001	During those days another large crowd gathered . Since they had nothing to eat , Jesus called his disciples to him and said ,
41008002	" I have compassion for these people ; they have already been with me three days and have nothing to eat .
41008003	If I send them home hungry , they will collapse on the way , because some of them have come a long distance . "
41008004	His disciples answered , " But where in this remote place can anyone get enough bread to feed them ? "
41008005	" How many loaves do you have ? " Jesus asked . " Seven , " they replied .
41008006	He told the crowd to sit down on the ground . When he had taken the seven loaves and given thanks , he broke them and gave them to his disciples to distribute to the people , and they did so .
41008007	They had a few small fish as well ; he gave thanks for them also and told the disciples to distribute them .
41008008	The people ate and were satisfied . Afterward the disciples picked up seven basketfuls of broken pieces that were left over .
41008009	About four thousand were present . After he had sent them away ,
41008010	he got into the boat with his disciples and went to the region of Dalmanutha .
41008011	The Pharisees came and began to question Jesus . To test him , they asked him for a sign from heaven .
41008012	He sighed deeply and said , " Why does this generation ask for a sign ? Truly I tell you , no sign will be given to it . "
41008013	Then he left them , got back into the boat and crossed to the other side .
41008014	The disciples had forgotten to bring bread , except for one loaf they had with them in the boat .
41008015	" Be careful , " Jesus warned them . " Watch out for the yeast of the Pharisees and that of Herod . "
41008016	They discussed this with one another and said , " It is because we have no bread . "
41008017	Aware of their discussion , Jesus asked them : " Why are you talking about having no bread ? Do you still not see or understand ? Are your hearts hardened ?
41008018	Do you have eyes but fail to see , and ears but fail to hear ? And don't you remember ?
41008019	When I broke the five loaves for the five thousand , how many basketfuls of pieces did you pick up ? " " Twelve , " they replied .
41008020	" And when I broke the seven loaves for the four thousand , how many basketfuls of pieces did you pick up ? " They answered , " Seven . "
41008021	He said to them , " Do you still not understand ? "
41008022	They came to Bethsaida , and some people brought a blind man and begged Jesus to touch him .
41008023	He took the blind man by the hand and led him outside the village . When he had spit on the man's eyes and put his hands on him , Jesus asked , " Do you see anything ? "
41008024	He looked up and said , " I see people ; they look like trees walking around . "
41008025	Once more Jesus put his hands on the man's eyes . Then his eyes were opened , his sight was restored , and he saw everything clearly .
41008026	Jesus sent him home , saying , " Don't even go into the village . "
41008027	Jesus and his disciples went on to the villages around Caesarea Philippi . On the way he asked them , " Who do people say I am ? "
41008028	They replied , " Some say John the Baptist ; others say Elijah ; and still others , one of the prophets . "
41008029	" But what about you ? " he asked . " Who do you say I am ? " Peter answered , " You are the Messiah . "
41008030	Jesus warned them not to tell anyone about him .
41008031	He then began to teach them that the Son of Man must suffer many things and be rejected by the elders , the chief priests and the teachers of the law , and that he must be killed and after three days rise again .
41008032	He spoke plainly about this , and Peter took him aside and began to rebuke him .
41008033	But when Jesus turned and looked at his disciples , he rebuked Peter . " Get behind me , Satan ! " he said . " You do not have in mind the concerns of God , but merely human concerns . "
41008034	Then he called the crowd to him along with his disciples and said : " Whoever wants to be my disciple must deny themselves and take up their cross and follow me .
41008035	For whoever wants to save their life will lose it , but whoever loses their life for me and for the gospel will save it .
41008036	What good is it for someone to gain the whole world , yet forfeit their soul ?
41008037	Or what can anyone give in exchange for their soul ?
41008038	If anyone is ashamed of me and my words in this adulterous and sinful generation , the Son of Man will be ashamed of them when he comes in his Father's glory with the holy angels . "
41009001	And he said to them , " Truly I tell you , some who are standing here will not taste death before they see that the kingdom of God has come with power . "
41009002	After six days Jesus took Peter , James and John with him and led them up a high mountain , where they were all alone . There he was transfigured before them .
41009003	His clothes became dazzling white , whiter than anyone in the world could bleach them .
41009004	And there appeared before them Elijah and Moses , who were talking with Jesus .
41009005	Peter said to Jesus , " Rabbi , it is good for us to be here . Let us put up three shelters — one for you , one for Moses and one for Elijah . "
41009006	( He did not know what to say , they were so frightened . )
41009007	Then a cloud appeared and covered them , and a voice came from the cloud : " This is my Son , whom I love . Listen to him ! "
41009008	Suddenly , when they looked around , they no longer saw anyone with them except Jesus .
41009009	As they were coming down the mountain , Jesus gave them orders not to tell anyone what they had seen until the Son of Man had risen from the dead .
41009010	They kept the matter to themselves , discussing what " rising from the dead " meant .
41009011	And they asked him , " Why do the teachers of the law say that Elijah must come first ? "
41009012	Jesus replied , " To be sure , Elijah does come first , and restores all things . Why then is it written that the Son of Man must suffer much and be rejected ?
41009013	But I tell you , Elijah has come , and they have done to him everything they wished , just as it is written about him . "
41009014	When they came to the other disciples , they saw a large crowd around them and the teachers of the law arguing with them .
41009015	As soon as all the people saw Jesus , they were overwhelmed with wonder and ran to greet him .
41009016	" What are you arguing with them about ? " he asked .
41009017	A man in the crowd answered , " Teacher , I brought you my son , who is possessed by a spirit that has robbed him of speech .
41009018	Whenever it seizes him , it throws him to the ground . He foams at the mouth , gnashes his teeth and becomes rigid . I asked your disciples to drive out the spirit , but they could not . "
41009019	" You unbelieving generation , " Jesus replied , " how long shall I stay with you ? How long shall I put up with you ? Bring the boy to me . "
41009020	So they brought him . When the spirit saw Jesus , it immediately threw the boy into a convulsion . He fell to the ground and rolled around , foaming at the mouth .
41009021	Jesus asked the boy's father , " How long has he been like this ? " " From childhood , " he answered .
41009022	" It has often thrown him into fire or water to kill him . But if you can do anything , take pity on us and help us . "
41009023	" ' If you can ' ? " said Jesus . " Everything is possible for one who believes . "
41009024	Immediately the boy's father exclaimed , " I do believe ; help me overcome my unbelief ! "
41009025	When Jesus saw that a crowd was running to the scene , he rebuked the impure spirit . " You deaf and mute spirit , " he said , " I command you , come out of him and never enter him again . "
41009026	The spirit shrieked , convulsed him violently and came out . The boy looked so much like a corpse that many said , " He's dead . "
41009027	But Jesus took him by the hand and lifted him to his feet , and he stood up .
41009028	After Jesus had gone indoors , his disciples asked him privately , " Why couldn't we drive it out ? "
41009029	He replied , " This kind can come out only by prayer . "
41009030	They left that place and passed through Galilee . Jesus did not want anyone to know where they were ,
41009031	because he was teaching his disciples . He said to them , " The Son of Man is going to be delivered into the hands of men . They will kill him , and after three days he will rise . "
41009032	But they did not understand what he meant and were afraid to ask him about it .
41009033	They came to Capernaum . When he was in the house , he asked them , " What were you arguing about on the road ? "
41009034	But they kept quiet because on the way they had argued about who was the greatest .
41009035	Sitting down , Jesus called the Twelve and said , " Anyone who wants to be first must be the very last , and the servant of all . "
41009036	He took a little child whom he placed among them . Taking the child in his arms , he said to them ,
41009037	" Whoever welcomes one of these little children in my name welcomes me ; and whoever welcomes me does not welcome me but the one who sent me . "
41009038	" Teacher , " said John , " we saw someone driving out demons in your name and we told him to stop , because he was not one of us . "
41009039	" Do not stop him , " Jesus said . " For no one who does a miracle in my name can in the next moment say anything bad about me ,
41009040	for whoever is not against us is for us .
41009041	Truly I tell you , anyone who gives you a cup of water in my name because you belong to the Messiah will certainly not lose their reward .
41009042	" If anyone causes one of these little ones — those who believe in me — to stumble , it would be better for them if a large millstone were hung around their neck and they were thrown into the sea .
41009043	If your hand causes you to stumble , cut it off . It is better for you to enter life maimed than with two hands to go into hell , where the fire never goes out .
41009045	And if your foot causes you to stumble , cut it off . It is better for you to enter life crippled than to have two feet and be thrown into hell .
41009047	And if your eye causes you to stumble , pluck it out . It is better for you to enter the kingdom of God with one eye than to have two eyes and be thrown into hell ,
41009048	where the worms that eat them do not die , and the fire is not quenched . '
41009049	Everyone will be salted with fire .
41009050	" Salt is good , but if it loses its saltiness , how can you make it salty again ? Have salt among yourselves , and be at peace with each other . "
41010001	Jesus then left that place and went into the region of Judea and across the Jordan . Again crowds of people came to him , and as was his custom , he taught them .
41010002	Some Pharisees came and tested him by asking , " Is it lawful for a man to divorce his wife ? "
41010003	" What did Moses command you ? " he replied .
41010004	They said , " Moses permitted a man to write a certificate of divorce and send her away . "
41010005	" It was because your hearts were hard that Moses wrote you this law , " Jesus replied .
41010006	" But at the beginning of creation God ' made them male and female . '
41010007	' For this reason a man will leave his father and mother and be united to his wife ,
41010008	and the two will become one flesh . ' So they are no longer two , but one flesh .
41010009	Therefore what God has joined together , let no one separate . "

41010020	" Teacher , " he declared , " all these I have kept since I was a boy . "

41011030	John's baptism — was it from heaven , or of human origin ? Tell me ! "
41011031	They discussed it among themselves and said , " If we say , ' From heaven , ' he will ask , ' Then why didn't you believe him ? '
41011032	But if we say , ' Of human origin ' . . . " ( They feared the people , for everyone held that John really was a prophet . )
41011033	So they answered Jesus , " We don't know . " Jesus said , " Neither will I tell you by what authority I am doing these things . "
41012001	Jesus then began to speak to them in parables : " A man planted a vineyard . He put a wall around it , dug a pit for the winepress and built a watchtower . Then he rented the vineyard to some farmers and moved to another place .
41012002	At harvest time he sent a servant to the tenants to collect from them some of the fruit of the vineyard .
41012003	But they seized him , beat him and sent him away empty-handed .
41012004	Then he sent another servant to them ; they struck this man on the head and treated him shamefully .
41012005	He sent still another , and that one they killed . He sent many others ; some of them they beat , others they killed .
41012006	" He had one left to send , a son , whom he loved . He sent him last of all , saying , ' They will respect my son . '
41012007	" But the tenants said to one another , ' This is the heir . Come , let's kill him , and the inheritance will be ours . '
41012008	So they took him and killed him , and threw him out of the vineyard .
41012009	" What then will the owner of the vineyard do ? He will come and kill those tenants and give the vineyard to others .
41012010	Haven't you read this passage of Scripture :
41012012	Then the chief priests , the teachers of the law and the elders looked for a way to arrest him because they knew he had spoken the parable against them . But they were afraid of the crowd ; so they left him and went away .
41012013	Later they sent some of the Pharisees and Herodians to Jesus to catch him in his words .
41012014	They came to him and said , " Teacher , we know that you are a man of integrity . You aren't swayed by others , because you pay no attention to who they are ; but you teach the way of God in accordance with the truth . Is it right to pay the imperial tax to Caesar or not ?
41012015	Should we pay or shouldn't we ? " But Jesus knew their hypocrisy . " Why are you trying to trap me ? " he asked . " Bring me a denarius and let me look at it . "
41012016	They brought the coin , and he asked them , " Whose image is this ? And whose inscription ? " " Caesar's , " they replied .
41012017	Then Jesus said to them , " Give back to Caesar what is Caesar's and to God what is God's . " And they were amazed at him .
41012018	Then the Sadducees , who say there is no resurrection , came to him with a question .
41012019	" Teacher , " they said , " Moses wrote for us that if a man's brother dies and leaves a wife but no children , the man must marry the widow and raise up offspring for his brother .
41012020	Now there were seven brothers . The first one married and died without leaving any children .
41012021	The second one married the widow , but he also died , leaving no child . It was the same with the third .
41012022	In fact , none of the seven left any children . Last of all , the woman died too .
41012023	At the resurrection whose wife will she be , since the seven were married to her ? "
41012024	Jesus replied , " Are you not in error because you do not know the Scriptures or the power of God ?
41012025	When the dead rise , they will neither marry nor be given in marriage ; they will be like the angels in heaven .
41012026	Now about the dead rising — have you not read in the Book of Moses , in the account of the burning bush , how God said to him , ' I am the God of Abraham , the God of Isaac , and the God of Jacob ' ?
41012027	He is not the God of the dead , but of the living . You are badly mistaken ! "
41012028	One of the teachers of the law came and heard them debating . Noticing that Jesus had given them a good answer , he asked him , " Of all the commandments , which is the most important ? "
41012029	" The most important one , " answered Jesus , " is this : ' Hear , O Israel : The Lord our God , the Lord is one .
41012030	Love the Lord your God with all your heart and with all your soul and with all your mind and with all your strength . '
41012031	The second is this : ' Love your neighbor as yourself . ' There is no commandment greater than these . "
41012032	" Well said , teacher , " the man replied . " You are right in saying that God is one and there is no other but him .
41012033	To love him with all your heart , with all your understanding and with all your strength , and to love your neighbor as yourself is more important than all burnt offerings and sacrifices . "
41012034	When Jesus saw that he had answered wisely , he said to him , " You are not far from the kingdom of God . " And from then on no one dared ask him any more questions .
41012035	While Jesus was teaching in the temple courts , he asked , " Why do the teachers of the law say that the Messiah is the son of David ?
41012036	David himself , speaking by the Holy Spirit , declared :
41012038	As he taught , Jesus said , " Watch out for the teachers of the law . They like to walk around in flowing robes and be greeted with respect in the marketplaces ,
41012039	and have the most important seats in the synagogues and the places of honor at banquets .
41012040	They devour widows' houses and for a show make lengthy prayers . These men will be punished most severely . "
41012041	Jesus sat down opposite the place where the offerings were put and watched the crowd putting their money into the temple treasury . Many rich people threw in large amounts .
41012042	But a poor widow came and put in two very small copper coins , worth only a few cents .
41012043	Calling his disciples to him , Jesus said , " Truly I tell you , this poor widow has put more into the treasury than all the others .
41012044	They all gave out of their wealth ; but she , out of her poverty , put in everything — all she had to live on . "
41013001	As Jesus was leaving the temple , one of his disciples said to him , " Look , Teacher ! What massive stones ! What magnificent buildings ! "
41013002	" Do you see all these great buildings ? " replied Jesus . " Not one stone here will be left on another ; every one will be thrown down . "
41013003	As Jesus was sitting on the Mount of Olives opposite the temple , Peter , James , John and Andrew asked him privately ,
41013004	" Tell us , when will these things happen ? And what will be the sign that they are all about to be fulfilled ? "
41013005	Jesus said to them : " Watch out that no one deceives you .
41013006	Many will come in my name , claiming , ' I am he , ' and will deceive many .
41013007	When you hear of wars and rumors of wars , do not be alarmed . Such things must happen , but the end is still to come .
41013008	Nation will rise against nation , and kingdom against kingdom . There will be earthquakes in various places , and famines . These are the beginning of birth pains .
41013009	" You must be on your guard . You will be handed over to the local councils and flogged in the synagogues . On account of me you will stand before governors and kings as witnesses to them .
41013010	And the gospel must first be preached to all nations .
41013011	Whenever you are arrested and brought to trial , do not worry beforehand about what to say . Just say whatever is given you at the time , for it is not you speaking , but the Holy Spirit .
41013012	" Brother will betray brother to death , and a father his child . Children will rebel against their parents and have them put to death .
41013013	Everyone will hate you because of me , but the one who stands firm to the end will be saved .
41013014	" When you see ' the abomination that causes desolation ' standing where it does not belong — let the reader understand — then let those who are in Judea flee to the mountains .
41013015	Let no one on the housetop go down or enter the house to take anything out .
41013016	Let no one in the field go back to get their cloak .
41013017	How dreadful it will be in those days for pregnant women and nursing mothers !
41013018	Pray that this will not take place in winter ,
41013019	because those will be days of distress unequaled from the beginning , when God created the world , until now — and never to be equaled again .
41013020	" If the Lord had not cut short those days , no one would survive . But for the sake of the elect , whom he has chosen , he has shortened them .
41013021	At that time if anyone says to you , ' Look , here is the Messiah ! ' or , ' Look , there he is ! ' do not believe it .
41013022	For false messiahs and false prophets will appear and perform signs and wonders to deceive , if possible , even the elect .
41013023	So be on your guard ; I have told you everything ahead of time .
41013024	" But in those days , following that distress ,
41013025	the stars will fall from the sky ,
41013026	" At that time people will see the Son of Man coming in clouds with great power and glory .
41013027	And he will send his angels and gather his elect from the four winds , from the ends of the earth to the ends of the heavens .
41013028	" Now learn this lesson from the fig tree : As soon as its twigs get tender and its leaves come out , you know that summer is near .
41013029	Even so , when you see these things happening , you know that it is near , right at the door .
41013030	Truly I tell you , this generation will certainly not pass away until all these things have happened .
41013031	Heaven and earth will pass away , but my words will never pass away .
41013032	" But about that day or hour no one knows , not even the angels in heaven , nor the Son , but only the Father .
41013033	Be on guard ! Be alert ! You do not know when that time will come .
41013034	It's like a man going away : He leaves his house and puts his servants in charge , each with their assigned task , and tells the one at the door to keep watch .
41013035	" Therefore keep watch because you do not know when the owner of the house will come back — whether in the evening , or at midnight , or when the rooster crows , or at dawn .
41013036	If he comes suddenly , do not let him find you sleeping .
41013037	What I say to you , I say to everyone : ' Watch ! ' "
41014001	Now the Passover and the Festival of Unleavened Bread were only two days away , and the chief priests and the teachers of the law were scheming to arrest Jesus secretly and kill him .
41014002	" But not during the festival , " they said , " or the people may riot . "
41014003	While he was in Bethany , reclining at the table in the home of Simon the Leper , a woman came with an alabaster jar of very expensive perfume , made of pure nard . She broke the jar and poured the perfume on his head .
41014004	Some of those present were saying indignantly to one another , " Why this waste of perfume ?
41014005	It could have been sold for more than a year's wages and the money given to the poor . " And they rebuked her harshly .
41014006	" Leave her alone , " said Jesus . " Why are you bothering her ? She has done a beautiful thing to me .

41015001	Very early in the morning , the chief priests , with the elders , the teachers of the law and the whole Sanhedrin , made their plans . So they bound Jesus , led him away and handed him over to Pilate .

41016020	Then the disciples went out and preached everywhere , and the Lord worked with them and confirmed his word by the signs that accompanied it .
43001001	In the beginning was the Word , and the Word was with God , and the Word was God .
43001002	He was with God in the beginning .
43001003	Through him all things were made ; without him nothing was made that has been made .
43001004	In him was life , and that life was the light of all mankind .
43001005	The light shines in the darkness , and the darkness has not overcome it .
43001006	There was a man sent from God whose name was John .
43001007	He came as a witness to testify concerning that light , so that through him all might believe .
43001008	He himself was not the light ; he came only as a witness to the light .
43001009	The true light that gives light to everyone was coming into the world .
43001010	He was in the world , and though the world was made through him , the world did not recognize him .
43001011	He came to that which was his own , but his own did not receive him .
43001012	Yet to all who did receive him , to those who believed in his name , he gave the right to become children of God —
43001013	children born not of natural descent , nor of human decision or a husband's will , but born of God .
43001014	The Word became flesh and made his dwelling among us . We have seen his glory , the glory of the one and only Son , who came from the Father , full of grace and truth .
43001015	( John testified concerning him . He cried out , saying , " This is the one I spoke about when I said , ' He who comes after me has surpassed me because he was before me . ' " )
43001016	Out of his fullness we have all received grace in place of grace already given .
43001017	For the law was given through Moses ; grace and truth came through Jesus Christ .
43001018	No one has ever seen God , but the one and only Son , who is himself God and is in closest relationship with the Father , has made him known .
43001019	Now this was John's testimony when the Jewish leaders in Jerusalem sent priests and Levites to ask him who he was .
43001020	He did not fail to confess , but confessed freely , " I am not the Messiah . "
43001021	They asked him , " Then who are you ? Are you Elijah ? " He said , " I am not . " " Are you the Prophet ? " He answered , " No . "
43001022	Finally they said , " Who are you ? Give us an answer to take back to those who sent us . What do you say about yourself ? "
43001023	John replied in the words of Isaiah the prophet , " I am the voice of one calling in the wilderness , ' Make straight the way for the Lord . ' "
43001024	Now the Pharisees who had been sent
43001025	questioned him , " Why then do you baptize if you are not the Messiah , nor Elijah , nor the Prophet ? "
43001026	" I baptize with water , " John replied , " but among you stands one you do not know .
43001027	He is the one who comes after me , the straps of whose sandals I am not worthy to untie . "
43001028	This all happened at Bethany on the other side of the Jordan , where John was baptizing .
43001029	The next day John saw Jesus coming toward him and said , " Look , the Lamb of God , who takes away the sin of the world !
43001030	This is the one I meant when I said , ' A man who comes after me has surpassed me because he was before me . '
43001031	I myself did not know him , but the reason I came baptizing with water was that he might be revealed to Israel . "
43001032	Then John gave this testimony : " I saw the Spirit come down from heaven as a dove and remain on him .
43001033	And I myself did not know him , but the one who sent me to baptize with water told me , ' The man on whom you see the Spirit come down and remain is the one who will baptize with the Holy Spirit . '
43001034	I have seen and I testify that this is God's Chosen One . "
43001035	The next day John was there again with two of his disciples .
43001036	When he saw Jesus passing by , he said , " Look , the Lamb of God ! "
43001037	When the two disciples heard him say this , they followed Jesus .
43001038	Turning around , Jesus saw them following and asked , " What do you want ? " They said , " Rabbi " ( which means " Teacher " ) , " where are you staying ? "
43001039	" Come , " he replied , " and you will see . " So they went and saw where he was staying , and they spent that day with him . It was about four in the afternoon .
43001040	Andrew , Simon Peter's brother , was one of the two who heard what John had said and who had followed Jesus .
43001041	The first thing Andrew did was to find his brother Simon and tell him , " We have found the Messiah " ( that is , the Christ ) .
43001042	And he brought him to Jesus . Jesus looked at him and said , " You are Simon son of John . You will be called Cephas " ( which , when translated , is Peter ) .
43001043	The next day Jesus decided to leave for Galilee . Finding Philip , he said to him , " Follow me . "
43001044	Philip , like Andrew and Peter , was from the town of Bethsaida .
43001045	Philip found Nathanael and told him , " We have found the one Moses wrote about in the Law , and about whom the prophets also wrote — Jesus of Nazareth , the son of Joseph . "
43001046	" Nazareth ! Can anything good come from there ? " Nathanael asked . " Come and see , " said Philip .
43001047	When Jesus saw Nathanael approaching , he said of him , " Here truly is an Israelite in whom there is no deceit . "
43001048	" How do you know me ? " Nathanael asked . Jesus answered , " I saw you while you were still under the fig tree before Philip called you . "
43001049	Then Nathanael declared , " Rabbi , you are the Son of God ; you are the king of Israel . "
43001050	Jesus said , " You believe because I told you I saw you under the fig tree . You will see greater things than that . "
43001051	He then added , " Very truly I tell you , you will see ' heaven open , and the angels of God ascending and descending on ' the Son of Man . "
43002001	On the third day a wedding took place at Cana in Galilee . Jesus' mother was there ,
43002002	and Jesus and his disciples had also been invited to the wedding .
43002003	When the wine was gone , Jesus' mother said to him , " They have no more wine . "
43002004	" Woman , why do you involve me ? " Jesus replied . " My hour has not yet come . "
43002005	His mother said to the servants , " Do whatever he tells you . "
43002006	Nearby stood six stone water jars , the kind used by the Jews for ceremonial washing , each holding from twenty to thirty gallons .
43002007	Jesus said to the servants , " Fill the jars with water " ; so they filled them to the brim .
43002008	Then he told them , " Now draw some out and take it to the master of the banquet . " They did so ,
43002009	and the master of the banquet tasted the water that had been turned into wine . He did not realize where it had come from , though the servants who had drawn the water knew . Then he called the bridegroom aside
43002010	and said , " Everyone brings out the choice wine first and then the cheaper wine after the guests have had too much to drink ; but you have saved the best till now . "
43002011	What Jesus did here in Cana of Galilee was the first of the signs through which he revealed his glory ; and his disciples believed in him .
43002012	After this he went down to Capernaum with his mother and brothers and his disciples . There they stayed for a few days .
43002013	When it was almost time for the Jewish Passover , Jesus went up to Jerusalem .
43002014	In the temple courts he found people selling cattle , sheep and doves , and others sitting at tables exchanging money .
43002015	So he made a whip out of cords , and drove all from the temple courts , both sheep and cattle ; he scattered the coins of the money changers and overturned their tables .
43002016	To those who sold doves he said , " Get these out of here ! Stop turning my Father's house into a market ! "
43002017	His disciples remembered that it is written : " Zeal for your house will consume me . "
43002018	The Jews then responded to him , " What sign can you show us to prove your authority to do all this ? "
43002019	Jesus answered them , " Destroy this temple , and I will raise it again in three days . "
43002020	They replied , " It has taken forty-six years to build this temple , and you are going to raise it in three days ? "
43002021	But the temple he had spoken of was his body .
43002022	After he was raised from the dead , his disciples recalled what he had said . Then they believed the scripture and the words that Jesus had spoken .
43002023	Now while he was in Jerusalem at the Passover Festival , many people saw the signs he was performing and believed in his name .
43002024	But Jesus would not entrust himself to them , for he knew all people .
43002025	He did not need any testimony about mankind , for he knew what was in each person .
43003001	Now there was a Pharisee , a man named Nicodemus who was a member of the Jewish ruling council .
43003002	He came to Jesus at night and said , " Rabbi , we know that you are a teacher who has come from God . For no one could perform the signs you are doing if God were not with him . "
43003003	Jesus replied , " Very truly I tell you , no one can see the kingdom of God unless they are born again . "
43003004	" How can someone be born when they are old ? " Nicodemus asked . " Surely they cannot enter a second time into their mother's womb to be born ! "
43003005	Jesus answered , " Very truly I tell you , no one can enter the kingdom of God unless they are born of water and the Spirit .
43003006	Flesh gives birth to flesh , but the Spirit gives birth to spirit .
43003007	You should not be surprised at my saying , ' You must be born again . '
43003008	The wind blows wherever it pleases . You hear its sound , but you cannot tell where it comes from or where it is going . So it is with everyone born of the Spirit . "
43003009	" How can this be ? " Nicodemus asked .
43003010	" You are Israel's teacher , " said Jesus , " and do you not understand these things ?
43003011	Very truly I tell you , we speak of what we know , and we testify to what we have seen , but still you people do not accept our testimony .
43003012	I have spoken to you of earthly things and you do not believe ; how then will you believe if I speak of heavenly things ?
43003013	No one has ever gone into heaven except the one who came from heaven — the Son of Man .
43003014	Just as Moses lifted up the snake in the wilderness , so the Son of Man must be lifted up ,
43003015	that everyone who believes may have eternal life in him . "
43003016	For God so loved the world that he gave his one and only Son , that whoever believes in him shall not perish but have eternal life .
43003017	For God did not send his Son into the world to condemn the world , but to save the world through him .
43003018	Whoever believes in him is not condemned , but whoever does not believe stands condemned already because they have not believed in the name of God's one and only Son .
43003019	This is the verdict : Light has come into the world , but people loved darkness instead of light because their deeds were evil .
43003020	Everyone who does evil hates the light , and will not come into the light for fear that their deeds will be exposed .
43003021	But whoever lives by the truth comes into the light , so that it may be seen plainly that what they have done has been done in the sight of God .
43003022	After this , Jesus and his disciples went out into the Judean countryside , where he spent some time with them , and baptized .
43003023	Now John also was baptizing at Aenon near Salim , because there was plenty of water , and people were coming and being baptized .
43003024	( This was before John was put in prison . )
43003025	An argument developed between some of John's disciples and a certain Jew over the matter of ceremonial washing .
43003026	They came to John and said to him , " Rabbi , that man who was with you on the other side of the Jordan — the one you testified about — look , he is baptizing , and everyone is going to him . "
43003027	To this John replied , " A person can receive only what is given them from heaven .
43003028	You yourselves can testify that I said , ' I am not the Messiah but am sent ahead of him . '
43003029	The bride belongs to the bridegroom . The friend who attends the bridegroom waits and listens for him , and is full of joy when he hears the bridegroom's voice . That joy is mine , and it is now complete .
43003030	He must become greater ; I must become less . "
43003031	The one who comes from above is above all ; the one who is from the earth belongs to the earth , and speaks as one from the earth . The one who comes from heaven is above all .
43003032	He testifies to what he has seen and heard , but no one accepts his testimony .
43003033	Whoever has accepted it has certified that God is truthful .
43003034	For the one whom God has sent speaks the words of God , for God gives the Spirit without limit .
43003035	The Father loves the Son and has placed everything in his hands .
43003036	Whoever believes in the Son has eternal life , but whoever rejects the Son will not see life , for God's wrath remains on them .
43004001	Now Jesus learned that the Pharisees had heard that he was gaining and baptizing more disciples than John —
43004002	although in fact it was not Jesus who baptized , but his disciples .
43004003	So he left Judea and went back once more to Galilee .
43004004	Now he had to go through Samaria .
43004005	So he came to a town in Samaria called Sychar , near the plot of ground Jacob had given to his son Joseph .
43004006	Jacob's well was there , and Jesus , tired as he was from the journey , sat down by the well . It was about noon .
43004007	When a Samaritan woman came to draw water , Jesus said to her , " Will you give me a drink ? "
43004008	( His disciples had gone into the town to buy food . )
43004009	The Samaritan woman said to him , " You are a Jew and I am a Samaritan woman . How can you ask me for a drink ? " ( For Jews do not associate with Samaritans . )
43004010	Jesus answered her , " If you knew the gift of God and who it is that asks you for a drink , you would have asked him and he would have given you living water . "
43004011	" Sir , " the woman said , " you have nothing to draw with and the well is deep . Where can you get this living water ?
43004012	Are you greater than our father Jacob , who gave us the well and drank from it himself , as did also his sons and his livestock ? "
43004013	Jesus answered , " Everyone who drinks this water will be thirsty again ,
43004014	but whoever drinks the water I give them will never thirst . Indeed , the water I give them will become in them a spring of water welling up to eternal life . "
43004015	The woman said to him , " Sir , give me this water so that I won't get thirsty and have to keep coming here to draw water . "
43004016	He told her , " Go , call your husband and come back . "
43004017	" I have no husband , " she replied . Jesus said to her , " You are right when you say you have no husband .
43004018	The fact is , you have had five husbands , and the man you now have is not your husband . What you have just said is quite true . "
43004019	" Sir , " the woman said , " I can see that you are a prophet .
43004020	Our ancestors worshiped on this mountain , but you Jews claim that the place where we must worship is in Jerusalem . "
43004021	" Woman , " Jesus replied , " believe me , a time is coming when you will worship the Father neither on this mountain nor in Jerusalem .
43004022	You Samaritans worship what you do not know ; we worship what we do know , for salvation is from the Jews .
43004023	Yet a time is coming and has now come when the true worshipers will worship the Father in the Spirit and in truth , for they are the kind of worshipers the Father seeks .
43004024	God is spirit , and his worshipers must worship in the Spirit and in truth . "
43004025	The woman said , " I know that Messiah " ( called Christ ) " is coming . When he comes , he will explain everything to us . "
43004026	Then Jesus declared , " I , the one speaking to you — I am he . "
43004027	Just then his disciples returned and were surprised to find him talking with a woman . But no one asked , " What do you want ? " or " Why are you talking with her ? "
43004028	Then , leaving her water jar , the woman went back to the town and said to the people ,
43004029	" Come , see a man who told me everything I ever did . Could this be the Messiah ? "
43004030	They came out of the town and made their way toward him .
43004031	Meanwhile his disciples urged him , " Rabbi , eat something . "
43004032	But he said to them , " I have food to eat that you know nothing about . "
43004033	Then his disciples said to each other , " Could someone have brought him food ? "
43004034	" My food , " said Jesus , " is to do the will of him who sent me and to finish his work .
43004035	Don't you have a saying , ' It's still four months until harvest ' ? I tell you , open your eyes and look at the fields ! They are ripe for harvest .
43004036	Even now the one who reaps draws a wage and harvests a crop for eternal life , so that the sower and the reaper may be glad together .
43004037	Thus the saying ' One sows and another reaps ' is true .
43004038	I sent you to reap what you have not worked for . Others have done the hard work , and you have reaped the benefits of their labor . "
43004039	Many of the Samaritans from that town believed in him because of the woman's testimony , " He told me everything I ever did . "
43004040	So when the Samaritans came to him , they urged him to stay with them , and he stayed two days .
43004041	And because of his words many more became believers .
43004042	They said to the woman , " We no longer believe just because of what you said ; now we have heard for ourselves , and we know that this man really is the Savior of the world . "
43004043	After the two days he left for Galilee .
43004044	( Now Jesus himself had pointed out that a prophet has no honor in his own country . )
43004045	When he arrived in Galilee , the Galileans welcomed him . They had seen all that he had done in Jerusalem at the Passover Festival , for they also had been there .
43004046	Once more he visited Cana in Galilee , where he had turned the water into wine . And there was a certain royal official whose son lay sick at Capernaum .
43004047	When this man heard that Jesus had arrived in Galilee from Judea , he went to him and begged him to come and heal his son , who was close to death .
43004048	" Unless you people see signs and wonders , " Jesus told him , " you will never believe . "
43004049	The royal official said , " Sir , come down before my child dies . "
43004050	" Go , " Jesus replied , " your son will live . " The man took Jesus at his word and departed .
43004051	While he was still on the way , his servants met him with the news that his boy was living .
43004052	When he inquired as to the time when his son got better , they said to him , " Yesterday , at one in the afternoon , the fever left him . "
43004053	Then the father realized that this was the exact time at which Jesus had said to him , " Your son will live . " So he and his whole household believed .
43004054	This was the second sign Jesus performed after coming from Judea to Galilee .
43005001	Some time later , Jesus went up to Jerusalem for one of the Jewish festivals .
43005002	Now there is in Jerusalem near the Sheep Gate a pool , which in Aramaic is called Bethesda and which is surrounded by five covered colonnades .
43005003	Here a great number of disabled people used to lie — the blind , the lame , the paralyzed .
43005005	One who was there had been an invalid for thirty-eight years .
43005006	When Jesus saw him lying there and learned that he had been in this condition for a long time , he asked him , " Do you want to get well ? "
43005007	" Sir , " the invalid replied , " I have no one to help me into the pool when the water is stirred . While I am trying to get in , someone else goes down ahead of me . "
43005008	Then Jesus said to him , " Get up ! Pick up your mat and walk . "
43005009	At once the man was cured ; he picked up his mat and walked . The day on which this took place was a Sabbath ,
43005010	and so the Jewish leaders said to the man who had been healed , " It is the Sabbath ; the law forbids you to carry your mat . "
43005011	But he replied , " The man who made me well said to me , ' Pick up your mat and walk . ' "
43005012	So they asked him , " Who is this fellow who told you to pick it up and walk ? "
43005013	The man who was healed had no idea who it was , for Jesus had slipped away into the crowd that was there .
43005014	Later Jesus found him at the temple and said to him , " See , you are well again . Stop sinning or something worse may happen to you . "
43005015	The man went away and told the Jewish leaders that it was Jesus who had made him well .
43005016	So , because Jesus was doing these things on the Sabbath , the Jewish leaders began to persecute him .
43005017	In his defense Jesus said to them , " My Father is always at his work to this very day , and I too am working . "
43005018	For this reason they tried all the more to kill him ; not only was he breaking the Sabbath , but he was even calling God his own Father , making himself equal with God .
43005019	Jesus gave them this answer : " Very truly I tell you , the Son can do nothing by himself ; he can do only what he sees his Father doing , because whatever the Father does the Son also does .
43005020	For the Father loves the Son and shows him all he does . Yes , and he will show him even greater works than these , so that you will be amazed .
43005021	For just as the Father raises the dead and gives them life , even so the Son gives life to whom he is pleased to give it .
43005022	Moreover , the Father judges no one , but has entrusted all judgment to the Son ,
43005023	that all may honor the Son just as they honor the Father . Whoever does not honor the Son does not honor the Father , who sent him .
43005024	" Very truly I tell you , whoever hears my word and believes him who sent me has eternal life and will not be judged but has crossed over from death to life .
43005025	Very truly I tell you , a time is coming and has now come when the dead will hear the voice of the Son of God and those who hear will live .
43005026	For as the Father has life in himself , so he has granted the Son also to have life in himself .
43005027	And he has given him authority to judge because he is the Son of Man .
43005028	" Do not be amazed at this , for a time is coming when all who are in their graves will hear his voice
43005029	and come out — those who have done what is good will rise to live , and those who have done what is evil will rise to be condemned .
43005030	By myself I can do nothing ; I judge only as I hear , and my judgment is just , for I seek not to please myself but him who sent me .
43005031	" If I testify about myself , my testimony is not true .
43005032	There is another who testifies in my favor , and I know that his testimony about me is true .
43005033	" You have sent to John and he has testified to the truth .
43005034	Not that I accept human testimony ; but I mention it that you may be saved .
43005035	John was a lamp that burned and gave light , and you chose for a time to enjoy his light .
43005036	" I have testimony weightier than that of John . For the works that the Father has given me to finish — the very works that I am doing — testify that the Father has sent me .
43005037	And the Father who sent me has himself testified concerning me . You have never heard his voice nor seen his form ,
43005038	nor does his word dwell in you , for you do not believe the one he sent .
43005039	You study the Scriptures diligently because you think that in them you have eternal life . These are the very Scriptures that testify about me ,
43005040	yet you refuse to come to me to have life .
43005041	" I do not accept glory from human beings ,
43005042	but I know you . I know that you do not have the love of God in your hearts .
43005043	I have come in my Father's name , and you do not accept me ; but if someone else comes in his own name , you will accept him .
43005044	How can you believe since you accept glory from one another but do not seek the glory that comes from the only God ?
43005045	" But do not think I will accuse you before the Father . Your accuser is Moses , on whom your hopes are set .
43005046	If you believed Moses , you would believe me , for he wrote about me .
43005047	But since you do not believe what he wrote , how are you going to believe what I say ? "
43006001	Some time after this , Jesus crossed to the far shore of the Sea of Galilee ( that is , the Sea of Tiberias ) ,
43006002	and a great crowd of people followed him because they saw the signs he had performed by healing the sick .
43006003	Then Jesus went up on a mountainside and sat down with his disciples .
43006004	The Jewish Passover Festival was near .
43006005	When Jesus looked up and saw a great crowd coming toward him , he said to Philip , " Where shall we buy bread for these people to eat ? "
43006006	He asked this only to test him , for he already had in mind what he was going to do .
43006007	Philip answered him , " It would take more than half a year's wages to buy enough bread for each one to have a bite ! "
43006008	Another of his disciples , Andrew , Simon Peter's brother , spoke up ,
43006009	" Here is a boy with five small barley loaves and two small fish , but how far will they go among so many ? "
43006010	Jesus said , " Have the people sit down . " There was plenty of grass in that place , and they sat down ( about five thousand men were there ) .
43006011	Jesus then took the loaves , gave thanks , and distributed to those who were seated as much as they wanted . He did the same with the fish .
43006012	When they had all had enough to eat , he said to his disciples , " Gather the pieces that are left over . Let nothing be wasted . "
43006013	So they gathered them and filled twelve baskets with the pieces of the five barley loaves left over by those who had eaten .
43006014	After the people saw the sign Jesus performed , they began to say , " Surely this is the Prophet who is to come into the world . "
43006015	Jesus , knowing that they intended to come and make him king by force , withdrew again to a mountain by himself .
43006016	When evening came , his disciples went down to the lake ,
43006017	where they got into a boat and set off across the lake for Capernaum . By now it was dark , and Jesus had not yet joined them .
43006018	A strong wind was blowing and the waters grew rough .
43006019	When they had rowed about three or four miles , they saw Jesus approaching the boat , walking on the water ; and they were frightened .
43006020	But he said to them , " It is I ; don't be afraid . "
43006021	Then they were willing to take him into the boat , and immediately the boat reached the shore where they were heading .
43006022	The next day the crowd that had stayed on the opposite shore of the lake realized that only one boat had been there , and that Jesus had not entered it with his disciples , but that they had gone away alone .
43006023	Then some boats from Tiberias landed near the place where the people had eaten the bread after the Lord had given thanks .
43006024	Once the crowd realized that neither Jesus nor his disciples were there , they got into the boats and went to Capernaum in search of Jesus .
43006025	When they found him on the other side of the lake , they asked him , " Rabbi , when did you get here ? "
43006026	Jesus answered , " Very truly I tell you , you are looking for me , not because you saw the signs I performed but because you ate the loaves and had your fill .
43006027	Do not work for food that spoils , but for food that endures to eternal life , which the Son of Man will give you . For on him God the Father has placed his seal of approval . "
43006028	Then they asked him , " What must we do to do the works God requires ? "
43006029	Jesus answered , " The work of God is this : to believe in the one he has sent . "
43006030	So they asked him , " What sign then will you give that we may see it and believe you ? What will you do ?
43006031	Our ancestors ate the manna in the wilderness ; as it is written : ' He gave them bread from heaven to eat . ' "
43006032	Jesus said to them , " Very truly I tell you , it is not Moses who has given you the bread from heaven , but it is my Father who gives you the true bread from heaven .
43006033	For the bread of God is the bread that comes down from heaven and gives life to the world . "
43006034	" Sir , " they said , " always give us this bread . "
43006035	Then Jesus declared , " I am the bread of life . Whoever comes to me will never go hungry , and whoever believes in me will never be thirsty .
43006036	But as I told you , you have seen me and still you do not believe .
43006037	All those the Father gives me will come to me , and whoever comes to me I will never drive away .
43006038	For I have come down from heaven not to do my will but to do the will of him who sent me .
43006039	And this is the will of him who sent me , that I shall lose none of all those he has given me , but raise them up at the last day .
43006040	For my Father's will is that everyone who looks to the Son and believes in him shall have eternal life , and I will raise them up at the last day . "
43006041	At this the Jews there began to grumble about him because he said , " I am the bread that came down from heaven . "
43006042	They said , " Is this not Jesus , the son of Joseph , whose father and mother we know ? How can he now say , ' I came down from heaven ' ? "
43006043	" Stop grumbling among yourselves , " Jesus answered .
43006044	" No one can come to me unless the Father who sent me draws them , and I will raise them up at the last day .
43006045	It is written in the Prophets : ' They will all be taught by God . ' Everyone who has heard the Father and learned from him comes to me .
43006046	No one has seen the Father except the one who is from God ; only he has seen the Father .
43006047	Very truly I tell you , the one who believes has eternal life .
43006048	I am the bread of life .
43006049	Your ancestors ate the manna in the wilderness , yet they died .
43006050	But here is the bread that comes down from heaven , which anyone may eat and not die .
43006051	I am the living bread that came down from heaven . Whoever eats this bread will live forever . This bread is my flesh , which I will give for the life of the world . "
43006052	Then the Jews began to argue sharply among themselves , " How can this man give us his flesh to eat ? "
43006053	Jesus said to them , " Very truly I tell you , unless you eat the flesh of the Son of Man and drink his blood , you have no life in you .
43006054	Whoever eats my flesh and drinks my blood has eternal life , and I will raise them up at the last day .
43006055	For my flesh is real food and my blood is real drink .
43006056	Whoever eats my flesh and drinks my blood remains in me , and I in them .
43006057	Just as the living Father sent me and I live because of the Father , so the one who feeds on me will live because of me .
43006058	This is the bread that came down from heaven . Your ancestors ate manna and died , but whoever feeds on this bread will live forever . "
43006059	He said this while teaching in the synagogue in Capernaum .
43006060	On hearing it , many of his disciples said , " This is a hard teaching . Who can accept it ? "
43006061	Aware that his disciples were grumbling about this , Jesus said to them , " Does this offend you ?
43006062	Then what if you see the Son of Man ascend to where he was before !
43006063	The Spirit gives life ; the flesh counts for nothing . The words I have spoken to you — they are full of the Spirit and life .
43006064	Yet there are some of you who do not believe . " For Jesus had known from the beginning which of them did not believe and who would betray him .
43006065	He went on to say , " This is why I told you that no one can come to me unless the Father has enabled them . "
43006066	From this time many of his disciples turned back and no longer followed him .
43006067	" You do not want to leave too , do you ? " Jesus asked the Twelve .
43006068	Simon Peter answered him , " Lord , to whom shall we go ? You have the words of eternal life .
43006069	We have come to believe and to know that you are the Holy One of God . "
43006070	Then Jesus replied , " Have I not chosen you , the Twelve ? Yet one of you is a devil ! "
43006071	( He meant Judas , the son of Simon Iscariot , who , though one of the Twelve , was later to betray him . )
43007001	After this , Jesus went around in Galilee . He did not want to go about in Judea because the Jewish leaders there were looking for a way to kill him .
43007002	But when the Jewish Festival of Tabernacles was near ,
43007003	Jesus' brothers said to him , " Leave Galilee and go to Judea , so that your disciples there may see the works you do .
43007004	No one who wants to become a public figure acts in secret . Since you are doing these things , show yourself to the world . "
43007005	For even his own brothers did not believe in him .
43007006	Therefore Jesus told them , " My time is not yet here ; for you any time will do .
43007007	The world cannot hate you , but it hates me because I testify that its works are evil .
43007008	You go to the festival . I am not going up to this festival , because my time has not yet fully come . "
43007009	After he had said this , he stayed in Galilee .
43007010	However , after his brothers had left for the festival , he went also , not publicly , but in secret .
43007011	Now at the festival the Jewish leaders were watching for Jesus and asking , " Where is he ? "
43007012	Among the crowds there was widespread whispering about him . Some said , " He is a good man . " Others replied , " No , he deceives the people . "
43007013	But no one would say anything publicly about him for fear of the leaders .
43007014	Not until halfway through the festival did Jesus go up to the temple courts and begin to teach .
43007015	The Jews there were amazed and asked , " How did this man get such learning without having been taught ? "
43007016	Jesus answered , " My teaching is not my own . It comes from the one who sent me .
43007017	Anyone who chooses to do the will of God will find out whether my teaching comes from God or whether I speak on my own .
43007018	Whoever speaks on their own does so to gain personal glory , but he who seeks the glory of the one who sent him is a man of truth ; there is nothing false about him .
43007019	Has not Moses given you the law ? Yet not one of you keeps the law . Why are you trying to kill me ? "
43007020	" You are demon-possessed , " the crowd answered . " Who is trying to kill you ? "
43007021	Jesus said to them , " I did one miracle , and you are all amazed .
43007022	Yet , because Moses gave you circumcision ( though actually it did not come from Moses , but from the patriarchs ) , you circumcise a boy on the Sabbath .
43007023	Now if a boy can be circumcised on the Sabbath so that the law of Moses may not be broken , why are you angry with me for healing a man's whole body on the Sabbath ?
43007024	Stop judging by mere appearances , but instead judge correctly . "
43007025	At that point some of the people of Jerusalem began to ask , " Isn't this the man they are trying to kill ?
43007026	Here he is , speaking publicly , and they are not saying a word to him . Have the authorities really concluded that he is the Messiah ?
43007027	But we know where this man is from ; when the Messiah comes , no one will know where he is from . "
43007028	Then Jesus , still teaching in the temple courts , cried out , " Yes , you know me , and you know where I am from . I am not here on my own authority , but he who sent me is true . You do not know him ,
43007029	but I know him because I am from him and he sent me . "
43007030	At this they tried to seize him , but no one laid a hand on him , because his hour had not yet come .
43007031	Still , many in the crowd believed in him . They said , " When the Messiah comes , will he perform more signs than this man ? "
43007032	The Pharisees heard the crowd whispering such things about him . Then the chief priests and the Pharisees sent temple guards to arrest him .
43007033	Jesus said , " I am with you for only a short time , and then I am going to the one who sent me .
43007034	You will look for me , but you will not find me ; and where I am , you cannot come . "
43007035	The Jews said to one another , " Where does this man intend to go that we cannot find him ? Will he go where our people live scattered among the Greeks , and teach the Greeks ?
43007036	What did he mean when he said , ' You will look for me , but you will not find me , ' and ' Where I am , you cannot come ' ? "
43007037	On the last and greatest day of the festival , Jesus stood and said in a loud voice , " Let anyone who is thirsty come to me and drink .
43007038	Whoever believes in me , as Scripture has said , rivers of living water will flow from within them . "
43007039	By this he meant the Spirit , whom those who believed in him were later to receive . Up to that time the Spirit had not been given , since Jesus had not yet been glorified .
43007040	On hearing his words , some of the people said , " Surely this man is the Prophet . "
43007041	Others said , " He is the Messiah . " Still others asked , " How can the Messiah come from Galilee ?
43007042	Does not Scripture say that the Messiah will come from David's descendants and from Bethlehem , the town where David lived ? "
43007043	Thus the people were divided because of Jesus .
43007044	Some wanted to seize him , but no one laid a hand on him .
43007045	Finally the temple guards went back to the chief priests and the Pharisees , who asked them , " Why didn't you bring him in ? "
43007046	" No one ever spoke the way this man does , " the guards replied .
43007047	" You mean he has deceived you also ? " the Pharisees retorted .
43007048	" Have any of the rulers or of the Pharisees believed in him ?
43007049	No ! But this mob that knows nothing of the law — there is a curse on them . "
43007050	Nicodemus , who had gone to Jesus earlier and who was one of their own number , asked ,
43007051	" Does our law condemn a man without first hearing him to find out what he has been doing ? "
43007052	They replied , " Are you from Galilee , too ? Look into it , and you will find that a prophet does not come out of Galilee . "
43007053	Then they all went home ,
43008001	but Jesus went to the Mount of Olives .
43008002	At dawn he appeared again in the temple courts , where all the people gathered around him , and he sat down to teach them .
43008003	The teachers of the law and the Pharisees brought in a woman caught in adultery . They made her stand before the group
43008004	and said to Jesus , " Teacher , this woman was caught in the act of adultery .
43008005	In the Law Moses commanded us to stone such women . Now what do you say ? "
43008006	They were using this question as a trap , in order to have a basis for accusing him . But Jesus bent down and started to write on the ground with his finger .
43008007	When they kept on questioning him , he straightened up and said to them , " Let any one of you who is without sin be the first to throw a stone at her . "
43008008	Again he stooped down and wrote on the ground .
43008009	At this , those who heard began to go away one at a time , the older ones first , until only Jesus was left , with the woman still standing there .
43008010	Jesus straightened up and asked her , " Woman , where are they ? Has no one condemned you ? "
43008011	" No one , sir , " she said . " Then neither do I condemn you , " Jesus declared . " Go now and leave your life of sin . "
43008012	When Jesus spoke again to the people , he said , " I am the light of the world . Whoever follows me will never walk in darkness , but will have the light of life . "
43008013	The Pharisees challenged him , " Here you are , appearing as your own witness ; your testimony is not valid . "
43008014	Jesus answered , " Even if I testify on my own behalf , my testimony is valid , for I know where I came from and where I am going . But you have no idea where I come from or where I am going .
43008015	You judge by human standards ; I pass judgment on no one .
43008016	But if I do judge , my decisions are true , because I am not alone . I stand with the Father , who sent me .
43008017	In your own Law it is written that the testimony of two witnesses is true .
43008018	I am one who testifies for myself ; my other witness is the Father , who sent me . "
43008019	Then they asked him , " Where is your father ? " " You do not know me or my Father , " Jesus replied . " If you knew me , you would know my Father also . "
43008020	He spoke these words while teaching in the temple courts near the place where the offerings were put . Yet no one seized him , because his hour had not yet come .
43008021	Once more Jesus said to them , " I am going away , and you will look for me , and you will die in your sin . Where I go , you cannot come . "
43008022	This made the Jews ask , " Will he kill himself ? Is that why he says , ' Where I go , you cannot come ' ? "
43008023	But he continued , " You are from below ; I am from above . You are of this world ; I am not of this world .
43008024	I told you that you would die in your sins ; if you do not believe that I am he , you will indeed die in your sins . "
43008025	" Who are you ? " they asked . " Just what I have been telling you from the beginning , " Jesus replied .
43008026	" I have much to say in judgment of you . But he who sent me is trustworthy , and what I have heard from him I tell the world . "
43008027	They did not understand that he was telling them about his Father .
43008028	So Jesus said , " When you have lifted up the Son of Man , then you will know that I am he and that I do nothing on my own but speak just what the Father has taught me .
43008029	The one who sent me is with me ; he has not left me alone , for I always do what pleases him . "
43008030	Even as he spoke , many believed in him .
43008031	To the Jews who had believed him , Jesus said , " If you hold to my teaching , you are really my disciples .
43008032	Then you will know the truth , and the truth will set you free . "
43008033	They answered him , " We are Abraham's descendants and have never been slaves of anyone . How can you say that we shall be set free ? "
43008034	Jesus replied , " Very truly I tell you , everyone who sins is a slave to sin .
43008035	Now a slave has no permanent place in the family , but a son belongs to it forever .
43008036	So if the Son sets you free , you will be free indeed .
43008037	I know that you are Abraham's descendants . Yet you are looking for a way to kill me , because you have no room for my word .
43008038	I am telling you what I have seen in the Father's presence , and you are doing what you have heard from your father . "
43008039	" Abraham is our father , " they answered . " If you were Abraham's children , " said Jesus , " then you would do what Abraham did .
43008040	As it is , you are looking for a way to kill me , a man who has told you the truth that I heard from God . Abraham did not do such things .
43008041	You are doing the works of your own father . " " We are not illegitimate children , " they protested . " The only Father we have is God himself . "
43008042	Jesus said to them , " If God were your Father , you would love me , for I have come here from God . I have not come on my own ; God sent me .
43008043	Why is my language not clear to you ? Because you are unable to hear what I say .
43008044	You belong to your father , the devil , and you want to carry out your father's desires . He was a murderer from the beginning , not holding to the truth , for there is no truth in him . When he lies , he speaks his native language , for he is a liar and the father of lies .
43008045	Yet because I tell the truth , you do not believe me !
43008046	Can any of you prove me guilty of sin ? If I am telling the truth , why don't you believe me ?
43008047	Whoever belongs to God hears what God says . The reason you do not hear is that you do not belong to God . "
43008048	The Jews answered him , " Aren't we right in saying that you are a Samaritan and demon-possessed ? "
43008049	" I am not possessed by a demon , " said Jesus , " but I honor my Father and you dishonor me .
43008050	I am not seeking glory for myself ; but there is one who seeks it , and he is the judge .
43008051	Very truly I tell you , whoever obeys my word will never see death . "
43008052	At this they exclaimed , " Now we know that you are demon-possessed ! Abraham died and so did the prophets , yet you say that whoever obeys your word will never taste death .
43008053	Are you greater than our father Abraham ? He died , and so did the prophets . Who do you think you are ? "
43008054	Jesus replied , " If I glorify myself , my glory means nothing . My Father , whom you claim as your God , is the one who glorifies me .
43008055	Though you do not know him , I know him . If I said I did not , I would be a liar like you , but I do know him and obey his word .
43008056	Your father Abraham rejoiced at the thought of seeing my day ; he saw it and was glad . "
43008057	" You are not yet fifty years old , " they said to him , " and you have seen Abraham ! "
43008058	" Very truly I tell you , " Jesus answered , " before Abraham was born , I am ! "
43008059	At this , they picked up stones to stone him , but Jesus hid himself , slipping away from the temple grounds .
43009001	As he went along , he saw a man blind from birth .
43009002	His disciples asked him , " Rabbi , who sinned , this man or his parents , that he was born blind ? "
43009003	" Neither this man nor his parents sinned , " said Jesus , " but this happened so that the works of God might be displayed in him .
43009004	As long as it is day , we must do the works of him who sent me . Night is coming , when no one can work .
43009005	While I am in the world , I am the light of the world . "
43009006	After saying this , he spit on the ground , made some mud with the saliva , and put it on the man's eyes .
43009007	" Go , " he told him , " wash in the Pool of Siloam " ( this word means " Sent " ) . So the man went and washed , and came home seeing .
