43009008	His neighbors and those who had formerly seen him begging asked , " Isn't this the same man who used to sit and beg ? "
43009009	Some claimed that he was . Others said , " No , he only looks like him . " But he himself insisted , " I am the man . "
43009010	" How then were your eyes opened ? " they asked .
43009011	He replied , " The man they call Jesus made some mud and put it on my eyes . He told me to go to Siloam and wash . So I went and washed , and then I could see . "
43009012	" Where is this man ? " they asked him . " I don't know , " he said .
43009013	They brought to the Pharisees the man who had been blind .
43009014	Now the day on which Jesus had made the mud and opened the man's eyes was a Sabbath .
43009015	Therefore the Pharisees also asked him how he had received his sight . " He put mud on my eyes , " the man replied , " and I washed , and now I see . "
43009016	Some of the Pharisees said , " This man is not from God , for he does not keep the Sabbath . " But others asked , " How can a sinner perform such signs ? " So they were divided .
43009017	Then they turned again to the blind man , " What have you to say about him ? It was your eyes he opened . " The man replied , " He is a prophet . "
43009018	They still did not believe that he had been blind and had received his sight until they sent for the man's parents .
43009019	" Is this your son ? " they asked . " Is this the one you say was born blind ? How is it that now he can see ? "
43009020	" We know he is our son , " the parents answered , " and we know he was born blind .
43009021	But how he can see now , or who opened his eyes , we don't know . Ask him . He is of age ; he will speak for himself . "
43009022	His parents said this because they were afraid of the Jewish leaders , who already had decided that anyone who acknowledged that Jesus was the Messiah would be put out of the synagogue .
43009023	That was why his parents said , " He is of age ; ask him . "
43009024	A second time they summoned the man who had been blind . " Give glory to God by telling the truth , " they said . " We know this man is a sinner . "
43009025	He replied , " Whether he is a sinner or not , I don't know . One thing I do know . I was blind but now I see ! "
43009026	Then they asked him , " What did he do to you ? How did he open your eyes ? "
43009027	He answered , " I have told you already and you did not listen . Why do you want to hear it again ? Do you want to become his disciples too ? "
43009028	Then they hurled insults at him and said , " You are this fellow's disciple ! We are disciples of Moses !
43009029	We know that God spoke to Moses , but as for this fellow , we don't even know where he comes from . "
43009030	The man answered , " Now that is remarkable ! You don't know where he comes from , yet he opened my eyes .
43009031	We know that God does not listen to sinners . He listens to the godly person who does his will .
43009032	Nobody has ever heard of opening the eyes of a man born blind .
43009033	If this man were not from God , he could do nothing . "
43009034	To this they replied , " You were steeped in sin at birth ; how dare you lecture us ! " And they threw him out .
43009035	Jesus heard that they had thrown him out , and when he found him , he said , " Do you believe in the Son of Man ? "
43009036	" Who is he , sir ? " the man asked . " Tell me so that I may believe in him . "
43009037	Jesus said , " You have now seen him ; in fact , he is the one speaking with you . "
43009038	Then the man said , " Lord , I believe , " and he worshiped him .
43009039	Jesus said , " For judgment I have come into this world , so that the blind will see and those who see will become blind . "
43009040	Some Pharisees who were with him heard him say this and asked , " What ? Are we blind too ? "
43009041	Jesus said , " If you were blind , you would not be guilty of sin ; but now that you claim you can see , your guilt remains .
43010001	" Very truly I tell you Pharisees , anyone who does not enter the sheep pen by the gate , but climbs in by some other way , is a thief and a robber .
43010002	The one who enters by the gate is the shepherd of the sheep .
43010003	The gatekeeper opens the gate for him , and the sheep listen to his voice . He calls his own sheep by name and leads them out .
43010004	When he has brought out all his own , he goes on ahead of them , and his sheep follow him because they know his voice .
43010005	But they will never follow a stranger ; in fact , they will run away from him because they do not recognize a stranger's voice . "
43010006	Jesus used this figure of speech , but the Pharisees did not understand what he was telling them .
43010007	Therefore Jesus said again , " Very truly I tell you , I am the gate for the sheep .
43010008	All who have come before me are thieves and robbers , but the sheep have not listened to them .
43010009	I am the gate ; whoever enters through me will be saved . They will come in and go out , and find pasture .
43010010	The thief comes only to steal and kill and destroy ; I have come that they may have life , and have it to the full .
43010011	" I am the good shepherd . The good shepherd lays down his life for the sheep .
43010012	The hired hand is not the shepherd and does not own the sheep . So when he sees the wolf coming , he abandons the sheep and runs away . Then the wolf attacks the flock and scatters it .
43010013	The man runs away because he is a hired hand and cares nothing for the sheep .
43010014	" I am the good shepherd ; I know my sheep and my sheep know me —
43010015	just as the Father knows me and I know the Father — and I lay down my life for the sheep .
43010016	I have other sheep that are not of this sheep pen . I must bring them also . They too will listen to my voice , and there shall be one flock and one shepherd .
43010017	The reason my Father loves me is that I lay down my life — only to take it up again .
43010018	No one takes it from me , but I lay it down of my own accord . I have authority to lay it down and authority to take it up again . This command I received from my Father . "
43010019	The Jews who heard these words were again divided .
43010020	Many of them said , " He is demon-possessed and raving mad . Why listen to him ? "
43010021	But others said , " These are not the sayings of a man possessed by a demon . Can a demon open the eyes of the blind ? "
43010022	Then came the Festival of Dedication at Jerusalem . It was winter ,
43010023	and Jesus was in the temple courts walking in Solomon's Colonnade .
43010024	The Jews who were there gathered around him , saying , " How long will you keep us in suspense ? If you are the Messiah , tell us plainly . "
43010025	Jesus answered , " I did tell you , but you do not believe . The works I do in my Father's name testify about me ,
43010026	but you do not believe because you are not my sheep .
43010027	My sheep listen to my voice ; I know them , and they follow me .
43010028	I give them eternal life , and they shall never perish ; no one will snatch them out of my hand .
43010029	My Father , who has given them to me , is greater than all ; no one can snatch them out of my Father's hand .
43010030	I and the Father are one . "
43010031	Again his Jewish opponents picked up stones to stone him ,
43010032	but Jesus said to them , " I have shown you many good works from the Father . For which of these do you stone me ? "
43010033	" We are not stoning you for any good work , " they replied , " but for blasphemy , because you , a mere man , claim to be God . "
43010034	Jesus answered them , " Is it not written in your Law , ' I have said you are " gods " ' ?
43010035	If he called them ' gods , ' to whom the word of God came — and Scripture cannot be set aside —
43010036	what about the one whom the Father set apart as his very own and sent into the world ? Why then do you accuse me of blasphemy because I said , ' I am God's Son ' ?
43010037	Do not believe me unless I do the works of my Father .
43010038	But if I do them , even though you do not believe me , believe the works , that you may know and understand that the Father is in me , and I in the Father . "
43010039	Again they tried to seize him , but he escaped their grasp .
43010040	Then Jesus went back across the Jordan to the place where John had been baptizing in the early days . There he stayed ,
43010041	and many people came to him . They said , " Though John never performed a sign , all that John said about this man was true . "
43010042	And in that place many believed in Jesus .
43011001	Now a man named Lazarus was sick . He was from Bethany , the village of Mary and her sister Martha .
43011002	( This Mary , whose brother Lazarus now lay sick , was the same one who poured perfume on the Lord and wiped his feet with her hair . )
43011003	So the sisters sent word to Jesus , " Lord , the one you love is sick . "
43011004	When he heard this , Jesus said , " This sickness will not end in death . No , it is for God's glory so that God's Son may be glorified through it . "
43011005	Now Jesus loved Martha and her sister and Lazarus .
43011006	So when he heard that Lazarus was sick , he stayed where he was two more days ,
43011007	and then he said to his disciples , " Let us go back to Judea . "
43011008	" But Rabbi , " they said , " a short while ago the Jews there tried to stone you , and yet you are going back ? "
43011009	Jesus answered , " Are there not twelve hours of daylight ? Anyone who walks in the daytime will not stumble , for they see by this world's light .
43011010	It is when a person walks at night that they stumble , for they have no light . "
43011011	After he had said this , he went on to tell them , " Our friend Lazarus has fallen asleep ; but I am going there to wake him up . "
43011012	His disciples replied , " Lord , if he sleeps , he will get better . "
43011013	Jesus had been speaking of his death , but his disciples thought he meant natural sleep .
43011014	So then he told them plainly , " Lazarus is dead ,
43011015	and for your sake I am glad I was not there , so that you may believe . But let us go to him . "
43011016	Then Thomas ( also known as Didymus ) said to the rest of the disciples , " Let us also go , that we may die with him . "
43011017	On his arrival , Jesus found that Lazarus had already been in the tomb for four days .
43011018	Now Bethany was less than two miles from Jerusalem ,
43011019	and many Jews had come to Martha and Mary to comfort them in the loss of their brother .
43011020	When Martha heard that Jesus was coming , she went out to meet him , but Mary stayed at home .
43011021	" Lord , " Martha said to Jesus , " if you had been here , my brother would not have died .
43011022	But I know that even now God will give you whatever you ask . "
43011023	Jesus said to her , " Your brother will rise again . "
43011024	Martha answered , " I know he will rise again in the resurrection at the last day . "
43011025	Jesus said to her , " I am the resurrection and the life . The one who believes in me will live , even though they die ;
43011026	and whoever lives by believing in me will never die . Do you believe this ? "
43011027	" Yes , Lord , " she replied , " I believe that you are the Messiah , the Son of God , who is to come into the world . "
43011028	After she had said this , she went back and called her sister Mary aside . " The Teacher is here , " she said , " and is asking for you . "
43011029	When Mary heard this , she got up quickly and went to him .
43011030	Now Jesus had not yet entered the village , but was still at the place where Martha had met him .
43011031	When the Jews who had been with Mary in the house , comforting her , noticed how quickly she got up and went out , they followed her , supposing she was going to the tomb to mourn there .
43011032	When Mary reached the place where Jesus was and saw him , she fell at his feet and said , " Lord , if you had been here , my brother would not have died . "
43011033	When Jesus saw her weeping , and the Jews who had come along with her also weeping , he was deeply moved in spirit and troubled .
43011034	" Where have you laid him ? " he asked . " Come and see , Lord , " they replied .
43011035	Jesus wept .
43011036	Then the Jews said , " See how he loved him ! "
43011037	But some of them said , " Could not he who opened the eyes of the blind man have kept this man from dying ? "
43011038	Jesus , once more deeply moved , came to the tomb . It was a cave with a stone laid across the entrance .
43011039	" Take away the stone , " he said . " But , Lord , " said Martha , the sister of the dead man , " by this time there is a bad odor , for he has been there four days . "
43011040	Then Jesus said , " Did I not tell you that if you believe , you will see the glory of God ? "
43011041	So they took away the stone . Then Jesus looked up and said , " Father , I thank you that you have heard me .
43011042	I knew that you always hear me , but I said this for the benefit of the people standing here , that they may believe that you sent me . "
43011043	When he had said this , Jesus called in a loud voice , " Lazarus , come out ! "
43011044	The dead man came out , his hands and feet wrapped with strips of linen , and a cloth around his face . Jesus said to them , " Take off the grave clothes and let him go . "
43011045	Therefore many of the Jews who had come to visit Mary , and had seen what Jesus did , believed in him .
43011046	But some of them went to the Pharisees and told them what Jesus had done .
43011047	Then the chief priests and the Pharisees called a meeting of the Sanhedrin . " What are we accomplishing ? " they asked . " Here is this man performing many signs .
43011048	If we let him go on like this , everyone will believe in him , and then the Romans will come and take away both our temple and our nation . "
43011049	Then one of them , named Caiaphas , who was high priest that year , spoke up , " You know nothing at all !
43011050	You do not realize that it is better for you that one man die for the people than that the whole nation perish . "
43011051	He did not say this on his own , but as high priest that year he prophesied that Jesus would die for the Jewish nation ,
43011052	and not only for that nation but also for the scattered children of God , to bring them together and make them one .
43011053	So from that day on they plotted to take his life .
43011054	Therefore Jesus no longer moved about publicly among the people of Judea . Instead he withdrew to a region near the wilderness , to a village called Ephraim , where he stayed with his disciples .
43011055	When it was almost time for the Jewish Passover , many went up from the country to Jerusalem for their ceremonial cleansing before the Passover .
43011056	They kept looking for Jesus , and as they stood in the temple courts they asked one another , " What do you think ? Isn't he coming to the festival at all ? "
43011057	But the chief priests and the Pharisees had given orders that anyone who found out where Jesus was should report it so that they might arrest him .
43012001	Six days before the Passover , Jesus came to Bethany , where Lazarus lived , whom Jesus had raised from the dead .
43012002	Here a dinner was given in Jesus' honor . Martha served , while Lazarus was among those reclining at the table with him .
43012003	Then Mary took about a pint of pure nard , an expensive perfume ; she poured it on Jesus' feet and wiped his feet with her hair . And the house was filled with the fragrance of the perfume .
43012004	But one of his disciples , Judas Iscariot , who was later to betray him , objected ,
43012005	" Why wasn't this perfume sold and the money given to the poor ? It was worth a year's wages . "
43012006	He did not say this because he cared about the poor but because he was a thief ; as keeper of the money bag , he used to help himself to what was put into it .
43012007	" Leave her alone , " Jesus replied . " It was intended that she should save this perfume for the day of my burial .
43012008	You will always have the poor among you , but you will not always have me . "
43012009	Meanwhile a large crowd of Jews found out that Jesus was there and came , not only because of him but also to see Lazarus , whom he had raised from the dead .
43012010	So the chief priests made plans to kill Lazarus as well ,
43012011	for on account of him many of the Jews were going over to Jesus and believing in him .
43012012	The next day the great crowd that had come for the festival heard that Jesus was on his way to Jerusalem .
43012013	They took palm branches and went out to meet him , shouting ,
43012015	" Do not be afraid , Daughter Zion ;
43012016	At first his disciples did not understand all this . Only after Jesus was glorified did they realize that these things had been written about him and that these things had been done to him .
43012017	Now the crowd that was with him when he called Lazarus from the tomb and raised him from the dead continued to spread the word .
43012018	Many people , because they had heard that he had performed this sign , went out to meet him .
43012019	So the Pharisees said to one another , " See , this is getting us nowhere . Look how the whole world has gone after him ! "
43012020	Now there were some Greeks among those who went up to worship at the festival .
43012021	They came to Philip , who was from Bethsaida in Galilee , with a request . " Sir , " they said , " we would like to see Jesus . "
43012022	Philip went to tell Andrew ; Andrew and Philip in turn told Jesus .
43012023	Jesus replied , " The hour has come for the Son of Man to be glorified .
43012024	Very truly I tell you , unless a kernel of wheat falls to the ground and dies , it remains only a single seed . But if it dies , it produces many seeds .
43012025	Anyone who loves their life will lose it , while anyone who hates their life in this world will keep it for eternal life .
43012026	Whoever serves me must follow me ; and where I am , my servant also will be . My Father will honor the one who serves me .
43012027	" Now my soul is troubled , and what shall I say ? ' Father , save me from this hour ' ? No , it was for this very reason I came to this hour .
43012028	Father , glorify your name ! " Then a voice came from heaven , " I have glorified it , and will glorify it again . "
43012029	The crowd that was there and heard it said it had thundered ; others said an angel had spoken to him .
43012030	Jesus said , " This voice was for your benefit , not mine .
43012031	Now is the time for judgment on this world ; now the prince of this world will be driven out .
43012032	And I , when I am lifted up from the earth , will draw all people to myself . "
43012033	He said this to show the kind of death he was going to die .
43012034	The crowd spoke up , " We have heard from the Law that the Messiah will remain forever , so how can you say , ' The Son of Man must be lifted up ' ? Who is this ' Son of Man ' ? "
43012035	Then Jesus told them , " You are going to have the light just a little while longer . Walk while you have the light , before darkness overtakes you . Whoever walks in the dark does not know where they are going .
43012036	Believe in the light while you have the light , so that you may become children of light . " When he had finished speaking , Jesus left and hid himself from them .
43012037	Even after Jesus had performed so many signs in their presence , they still would not believe in him .
43012038	This was to fulfill the word of Isaiah the prophet :
43012040	" He has blinded their eyes
43012041	Isaiah said this because he saw Jesus' glory and spoke about him .
43012042	Yet at the same time many even among the leaders believed in him . But because of the Pharisees they would not openly acknowledge their faith for fear they would be put out of the synagogue ;
43012043	for they loved human praise more than praise from God .
43012044	Then Jesus cried out , " Whoever believes in me does not believe in me only , but in the one who sent me .
43012045	The one who looks at me is seeing the one who sent me .
43012046	I have come into the world as a light , so that no one who believes in me should stay in darkness .
43012047	" If anyone hears my words but does not keep them , I do not judge that person . For I did not come to judge the world , but to save the world .
43012048	There is a judge for the one who rejects me and does not accept my words ; the very words I have spoken will condemn them at the last day .
43012049	For I did not speak on my own , but the Father who sent me commanded me to say all that I have spoken .
43012050	I know that his command leads to eternal life . So whatever I say is just what the Father has told me to say . "
43013001	It was just before the Passover Festival . Jesus knew that the hour had come for him to leave this world and go to the Father . Having loved his own who were in the world , he loved them to the end .
43013002	The evening meal was in progress , and the devil had already prompted Judas , the son of Simon Iscariot , to betray Jesus .
43013003	Jesus knew that the Father had put all things under his power , and that he had come from God and was returning to God ;
43013004	so he got up from the meal , took off his outer clothing , and wrapped a towel around his waist .
43013005	After that , he poured water into a basin and began to wash his disciples' feet , drying them with the towel that was wrapped around him .
43013006	He came to Simon Peter , who said to him , " Lord , are you going to wash my feet ? "
43013007	Jesus replied , " You do not realize now what I am doing , but later you will understand . "
43013008	" No , " said Peter , " you shall never wash my feet . " Jesus answered , " Unless I wash you , you have no part with me . "
43013009	" Then , Lord , " Simon Peter replied , " not just my feet but my hands and my head as well ! "
43013010	Jesus answered , " Those who have had a bath need only to wash their feet ; their whole body is clean . And you are clean , though not every one of you . "
43013011	For he knew who was going to betray him , and that was why he said not every one was clean .
43013012	When he had finished washing their feet , he put on his clothes and returned to his place . " Do you understand what I have done for you ? " he asked them .
43013013	" You call me ' Teacher ' and ' Lord , ' and rightly so , for that is what I am .
43013014	Now that I , your Lord and Teacher , have washed your feet , you also should wash one another's feet .
43013015	I have set you an example that you should do as I have done for you .
43013016	Very truly I tell you , no servant is greater than his master , nor is a messenger greater than the one who sent him .
43013017	Now that you know these things , you will be blessed if you do them .
43013018	" I am not referring to all of you ; I know those I have chosen . But this is to fulfill this passage of Scripture : ' He who shared my bread has turned against me . '
43013019	" I am telling you now before it happens , so that when it does happen you will believe that I am who I am .
43013020	Very truly I tell you , whoever accepts anyone I send accepts me ; and whoever accepts me accepts the one who sent me . "
43013021	After he had said this , Jesus was troubled in spirit and testified , " Very truly I tell you , one of you is going to betray me . "
43013022	His disciples stared at one another , at a loss to know which of them he meant .
43013023	One of them , the disciple whom Jesus loved , was reclining next to him .
43013024	Simon Peter motioned to this disciple and said , " Ask him which one he means . "
43013025	Leaning back against Jesus , he asked him , " Lord , who is it ? "
43013026	Jesus answered , " It is the one to whom I will give this piece of bread when I have dipped it in the dish . " Then , dipping the piece of bread , he gave it to Judas , the son of Simon Iscariot .
43013027	As soon as Judas took the bread , Satan entered into him . So Jesus told him , " What you are about to do , do quickly . "
43013028	But no one at the meal understood why Jesus said this to him .
43013029	Since Judas had charge of the money , some thought Jesus was telling him to buy what was needed for the festival , or to give something to the poor .
43013030	As soon as Judas had taken the bread , he went out . And it was night .
43013031	When he was gone , Jesus said , " Now the Son of Man is glorified and God is glorified in him .
43013032	If God is glorified in him , God will glorify the Son in himself , and will glorify him at once .
43013033	" My children , I will be with you only a little longer . You will look for me , and just as I told the Jews , so I tell you now : Where I am going , you cannot come .
43013034	" A new command I give you : Love one another . As I have loved you , so you must love one another .
43013035	By this everyone will know that you are my disciples , if you love one another . "
43013036	Simon Peter asked him , " Lord , where are you going ? " Jesus replied , " Where I am going , you cannot follow now , but you will follow later . "
43013037	Peter asked , " Lord , why can't I follow you now ? I will lay down my life for you . "
43013038	Then Jesus answered , " Will you really lay down your life for me ? Very truly I tell you , before the rooster crows , you will disown me three times !
43014001	" Do not let your hearts be troubled . You believe in God ; believe also in me .
43014002	My Father's house has many rooms ; if that were not so , would I have told you that I am going there to prepare a place for you ?
43014003	And if I go and prepare a place for you , I will come back and take you to be with me that you also may be where I am .
43014004	You know the way to the place where I am going . "
43014005	Thomas said to him , " Lord , we don't know where you are going , so how can we know the way ? "
43014006	Jesus answered , " I am the way and the truth and the life . No one comes to the Father except through me .
43014007	If you really know me , you will know my Father as well . From now on , you do know him and have seen him . "
43014008	Philip said , " Lord , show us the Father and that will be enough for us . "
43014009	Jesus answered : " Don't you know me , Philip , even after I have been among you such a long time ? Anyone who has seen me has seen the Father . How can you say , ' Show us the Father ' ?
43014010	Don't you believe that I am in the Father , and that the Father is in me ? The words I say to you I do not speak on my own authority . Rather , it is the Father , living in me , who is doing his work .
43014011	Believe me when I say that I am in the Father and the Father is in me ; or at least believe on the evidence of the works themselves .
43014012	Very truly I tell you , whoever believes in me will do the works I have been doing , and they will do even greater things than these , because I am going to the Father .
43014013	And I will do whatever you ask in my name , so that the Father may be glorified in the Son .
43014014	You may ask me for anything in my name , and I will do it .
43014015	" If you love me , keep my commands .
43014016	And I will ask the Father , and he will give you another advocate to help you and be with you forever —
43014017	the Spirit of truth . The world cannot accept him , because it neither sees him nor knows him . But you know him , for he lives with you and will be in you .
43014018	I will not leave you as orphans ; I will come to you .
43014019	Before long , the world will not see me anymore , but you will see me . Because I live , you also will live .
43014020	On that day you will realize that I am in my Father , and you are in me , and I am in you .
43014021	Whoever has my commands and keeps them is the one who loves me . The one who loves me will be loved by my Father , and I too will love them and show myself to them . "
43014022	Then Judas ( not Judas Iscariot ) said , " But , Lord , why do you intend to show yourself to us and not to the world ? "
43014023	Jesus replied , " Anyone who loves me will obey my teaching . My Father will love them , and we will come to them and make our home with them .
43014024	Anyone who does not love me will not obey my teaching . These words you hear are not my own ; they belong to the Father who sent me .
43014025	" All this I have spoken while still with you .
43014026	But the Advocate , the Holy Spirit , whom the Father will send in my name , will teach you all things and will remind you of everything I have said to you .
43014027	Peace I leave with you ; my peace I give you . I do not give to you as the world gives . Do not let your hearts be troubled and do not be afraid .
43014028	" You heard me say , ' I am going away and I am coming back to you . ' If you loved me , you would be glad that I am going to the Father , for the Father is greater than I .
43014029	I have told you now before it happens , so that when it does happen you will believe .
43014030	I will not say much more to you , for the prince of this world is coming . He has no hold over me ,
43014031	but he comes so that the world may learn that I love the Father and do exactly what my Father has commanded me . " Come now ; let us leave .
43015001	" I am the true vine , and my Father is the gardener .
43015002	He cuts off every branch in me that bears no fruit , while every branch that does bear fruit he prunes so that it will be even more fruitful .
43015003	You are already clean because of the word I have spoken to you .
43015004	Remain in me , as I also remain in you . No branch can bear fruit by itself ; it must remain in the vine . Neither can you bear fruit unless you remain in me .
43015005	" I am the vine ; you are the branches . If you remain in me and I in you , you will bear much fruit ; apart from me you can do nothing .
43015006	If you do not remain in me , you are like a branch that is thrown away and withers ; such branches are picked up , thrown into the fire and burned .
43015007	If you remain in me and my words remain in you , ask whatever you wish , and it will be done for you .
43015008	This is to my Father's glory , that you bear much fruit , showing yourselves to be my disciples .
43015009	" As the Father has loved me , so have I loved you . Now remain in my love .
43015010	If you keep my commands , you will remain in my love , just as I have kept my Father's commands and remain in his love .
43015011	I have told you this so that my joy may be in you and that your joy may be complete .
43015012	My command is this : Love each other as I have loved you .
43015013	Greater love has no one than this : to lay down one's life for one's friends .
43015014	You are my friends if you do what I command .
43015015	I no longer call you servants , because a servant does not know his master's business . Instead , I have called you friends , for everything that I learned from my Father I have made known to you .
43015016	You did not choose me , but I chose you and appointed you so that you might go and bear fruit — fruit that will last — and so that whatever you ask in my name the Father will give you .
43015017	This is my command : Love each other .
43015018	" If the world hates you , keep in mind that it hated me first .
43015019	If you belonged to the world , it would love you as its own . As it is , you do not belong to the world , but I have chosen you out of the world . That is why the world hates you .
43015020	Remember what I told you : ' A servant is not greater than his master . ' If they persecuted me , they will persecute you also . If they obeyed my teaching , they will obey yours also .
43015021	They will treat you this way because of my name , for they do not know the one who sent me .
43015022	If I had not come and spoken to them , they would not be guilty of sin ; but now they have no excuse for their sin .
43015023	Whoever hates me hates my Father as well .
43015024	If I had not done among them the works no one else did , they would not be guilty of sin . As it is , they have seen , and yet they have hated both me and my Father .
43015025	But this is to fulfill what is written in their Law : ' They hated me without reason . '
43015026	" When the Advocate comes , whom I will send to you from the Father — the Spirit of truth who goes out from the Father — he will testify about me .
43015027	And you also must testify , for you have been with me from the beginning .
43016001	" All this I have told you so that you will not fall away .
43016002	They will put you out of the synagogue ; in fact , the time is coming when anyone who kills you will think they are offering a service to God .
43016003	They will do such things because they have not known the Father or me .
43016004	I have told you this , so that when their time comes you will remember that I warned you about them . I did not tell you this from the beginning because I was with you ,
43016005	but now I am going to him who sent me . None of you asks me , ' Where are you going ? '
43016006	Rather , you are filled with grief because I have said these things .
43016007	But very truly I tell you , it is for your good that I am going away . Unless I go away , the Advocate will not come to you ; but if I go , I will send him to you .
43016008	When he comes , he will prove the world to be in the wrong about sin and righteousness and judgment :
43016009	about sin , because people do not believe in me ;
43016010	about righteousness , because I am going to the Father , where you can see me no longer ;
43016011	and about judgment , because the prince of this world now stands condemned .
43016012	" I have much more to say to you , more than you can now bear .
43016013	But when he , the Spirit of truth , comes , he will guide you into all the truth . He will not speak on his own ; he will speak only what he hears , and he will tell you what is yet to come .
43016014	He will glorify me because it is from me that he will receive what he will make known to you .
43016015	All that belongs to the Father is mine . That is why I said the Spirit will receive from me what he will make known to you . "
43016016	Jesus went on to say , " In a little while you will see me no more , and then after a little while you will see me . "
43016017	At this , some of his disciples said to one another , " What does he mean by saying , ' In a little while you will see me no more , and then after a little while you will see me , ' and ' Because I am going to the Father ' ? "
43016018	They kept asking , " What does he mean by ' a little while ' ? We don't understand what he is saying . "
43016019	Jesus saw that they wanted to ask him about this , so he said to them , " Are you asking one another what I meant when I said , ' In a little while you will see me no more , and then after a little while you will see me ' ?
43016020	Very truly I tell you , you will weep and mourn while the world rejoices . You will grieve , but your grief will turn to joy .
43016021	A woman giving birth to a child has pain because her time has come ; but when her baby is born she forgets the anguish because of her joy that a child is born into the world .
43016022	So with you : Now is your time of grief , but I will see you again and you will rejoice , and no one will take away your joy .
43016023	In that day you will no longer ask me anything . Very truly I tell you , my Father will give you whatever you ask in my name .
43016024	Until now you have not asked for anything in my name . Ask and you will receive , and your joy will be complete .
43016025	" Though I have been speaking figuratively , a time is coming when I will no longer use this kind of language but will tell you plainly about my Father .
43016026	In that day you will ask in my name . I am not saying that I will ask the Father on your behalf .
43016027	No , the Father himself loves you because you have loved me and have believed that I came from God .
43016028	I came from the Father and entered the world ; now I am leaving the world and going back to the Father . "
43016029	Then Jesus' disciples said , " Now you are speaking clearly and without figures of speech .
43016030	Now we can see that you know all things and that you do not even need to have anyone ask you questions . This makes us believe that you came from God . "
43016031	" Do you now believe ? " Jesus replied .
43016032	" A time is coming and in fact has come when you will be scattered , each to your own home . You will leave me all alone . Yet I am not alone , for my Father is with me .
43016033	" I have told you these things , so that in me you may have peace . In this world you will have trouble . But take heart ! I have overcome the world . "
43017001	After Jesus said this , he looked toward heaven and prayed : " Father , the hour has come . Glorify your Son , that your Son may glorify you .
43017002	For you granted him authority over all people that he might give eternal life to all those you have given him .
43017003	Now this is eternal life : that they know you , the only true God , and Jesus Christ , whom you have sent .
43017004	I have brought you glory on earth by finishing the work you gave me to do .
43017005	And now , Father , glorify me in your presence with the glory I had with you before the world began .
43017006	" I have revealed you to those whom you gave me out of the world . They were yours ; you gave them to me and they have obeyed your word .
43017007	Now they know that everything you have given me comes from you .
43017008	For I gave them the words you gave me and they accepted them . They knew with certainty that I came from you , and they believed that you sent me .
43017009	I pray for them . I am not praying for the world , but for those you have given me , for they are yours .
43017010	All I have is yours , and all you have is mine . And glory has come to me through them .
43017011	I will remain in the world no longer , but they are still in the world , and I am coming to you . Holy Father , protect them by the power of your name , the name you gave me , so that they may be one as we are one .
43017012	While I was with them , I protected them and kept them safe by that name you gave me . None has been lost except the one doomed to destruction so that Scripture would be fulfilled .
43017013	" I am coming to you now , but I say these things while I am still in the world , so that they may have the full measure of my joy within them .
43017014	I have given them your word and the world has hated them , for they are not of the world any more than I am of the world .
43017015	My prayer is not that you take them out of the world but that you protect them from the evil one .
43017016	They are not of the world , even as I am not of it .
43017017	Sanctify them by the truth ; your word is truth .
43017018	As you sent me into the world , I have sent them into the world .
43017019	For them I sanctify myself , that they too may be truly sanctified .
43017020	" My prayer is not for them alone . I pray also for those who will believe in me through their message ,
43017021	that all of them may be one , Father , just as you are in me and I am in you . May they also be in us so that the world may believe that you have sent me .
43017022	I have given them the glory that you gave me , that they may be one as we are one —
43017023	I in them and you in me — so that they may be brought to complete unity . Then the world will know that you sent me and have loved them even as you have loved me .
43017024	" Father , I want those you have given me to be with me where I am , and to see my glory , the glory you have given me because you loved me before the creation of the world .
43017025	" Righteous Father , though the world does not know you , I know you , and they know that you have sent me .
43017026	I have made you known to them , and will continue to make you known in order that the love you have for me may be in them and that I myself may be in them . "
43018001	When he had finished praying , Jesus left with his disciples and crossed the Kidron Valley . On the other side there was a garden , and he and his disciples went into it .
43018002	Now Judas , who betrayed him , knew the place , because Jesus had often met there with his disciples .
43018003	So Judas came to the garden , guiding a detachment of soldiers and some officials from the chief priests and the Pharisees . They were carrying torches , lanterns and weapons .
43018004	Jesus , knowing all that was going to happen to him , went out and asked them , " Who is it you want ? "
43018005	" Jesus of Nazareth , " they replied . " I am he , " Jesus said . ( And Judas the traitor was standing there with them . )
43018006	When Jesus said , " I am he , " they drew back and fell to the ground .
43018007	Again he asked them , " Who is it you want ? " " Jesus of Nazareth , " they said .
43018008	Jesus answered , " I told you that I am he . If you are looking for me , then let these men go . "
43018009	This happened so that the words he had spoken would be fulfilled : " I have not lost one of those you gave me . "
43018010	Then Simon Peter , who had a sword , drew it and struck the high priest's servant , cutting off his right ear . ( The servant's name was Malchus . )
43018011	Jesus commanded Peter , " Put your sword away ! Shall I not drink the cup the Father has given me ? "
43018012	Then the detachment of soldiers with its commander and the Jewish officials arrested Jesus . They bound him
43018013	and brought him first to Annas , who was the father-in-law of Caiaphas , the high priest that year .
43018014	Caiaphas was the one who had advised the Jewish leaders that it would be good if one man died for the people .
43018015	Simon Peter and another disciple were following Jesus . Because this disciple was known to the high priest , he went with Jesus into the high priest's courtyard ,
43018016	but Peter had to wait outside at the door . The other disciple , who was known to the high priest , came back , spoke to the servant girl on duty there and brought Peter in .
43018017	" You aren't one of this man's disciples too , are you ? " she asked Peter . He replied , " I am not . "
43018018	It was cold , and the servants and officials stood around a fire they had made to keep warm . Peter also was standing with them , warming himself .
43018019	Meanwhile , the high priest questioned Jesus about his disciples and his teaching .
43018020	" I have spoken openly to the world , " Jesus replied . " I always taught in synagogues or at the temple , where all the Jews come together . I said nothing in secret .
43018021	Why question me ? Ask those who heard me . Surely they know what I said . "
43018022	When Jesus said this , one of the officials nearby slapped him in the face . " Is this the way you answer the high priest ? " he demanded .
43018023	" If I said something wrong , " Jesus replied , " testify as to what is wrong . But if I spoke the truth , why did you strike me ? "
43018024	Then Annas sent him bound to Caiaphas the high priest .
43018025	Meanwhile , Simon Peter was still standing there warming himself . So they asked him , " You aren't one of his disciples too , are you ? " He denied it , saying , " I am not . "
43018026	One of the high priest's servants , a relative of the man whose ear Peter had cut off , challenged him , " Didn't I see you with him in the garden ? "
43018027	Again Peter denied it , and at that moment a rooster began to crow .
43018028	Then the Jewish leaders took Jesus from Caiaphas to the palace of the Roman governor . By now it was early morning , and to avoid ceremonial uncleanness they did not enter the palace , because they wanted to be able to eat the Passover .
43018029	So Pilate came out to them and asked , " What charges are you bringing against this man ? "
43018030	" If he were not a criminal , " they replied , " we would not have handed him over to you . "
43018031	Pilate said , " Take him yourselves and judge him by your own law . " " But we have no right to execute anyone , " they objected .
43018032	This took place to fulfill what Jesus had said about the kind of death he was going to die .
43018033	Pilate then went back inside the palace , summoned Jesus and asked him , " Are you the king of the Jews ? "
43018034	" Is that your own idea , " Jesus asked , " or did others talk to you about me ? "
43018035	" Am I a Jew ? " Pilate replied . " Your own people and chief priests handed you over to me . What is it you have done ? "
43018036	Jesus said , " My kingdom is not of this world . If it were , my servants would fight to prevent my arrest by the Jewish leaders . But now my kingdom is from another place . "
43018037	" You are a king , then ! " said Pilate . Jesus answered , " You say that I am a king . In fact , the reason I was born and came into the world is to testify to the truth . Everyone on the side of truth listens to me . "
43018038	" What is truth ? " retorted Pilate . With this he went out again to the Jews gathered there and said , " I find no basis for a charge against him .
43018039	But it is your custom for me to release to you one prisoner at the time of the Passover . Do you want me to release ' the king of the Jews ' ? "
43018040	They shouted back , " No , not him ! Give us Barabbas ! " Now Barabbas had taken part in an uprising .
43019001	Then Pilate took Jesus and had him flogged .
43019002	The soldiers twisted together a crown of thorns and put it on his head . They clothed him in a purple robe
43019003	and went up to him again and again , saying , " Hail , king of the Jews ! " And they slapped him in the face .
43019004	Once more Pilate came out and said to the Jews gathered there , " Look , I am bringing him out to you to let you know that I find no basis for a charge against him . "
43019005	When Jesus came out wearing the crown of thorns and the purple robe , Pilate said to them , " Here is the man ! "
43019006	As soon as the chief priests and their officials saw him , they shouted , " Crucify ! Crucify ! " But Pilate answered , " You take him and crucify him . As for me , I find no basis for a charge against him . "
43019007	The Jewish leaders insisted , " We have a law , and according to that law he must die , because he claimed to be the Son of God . "
43019008	When Pilate heard this , he was even more afraid ,
43019009	and he went back inside the palace . " Where do you come from ? " he asked Jesus , but Jesus gave him no answer .
43019010	" Do you refuse to speak to me ? " Pilate said . " Don't you realize I have power either to free you or to crucify you ? "
43019011	Jesus answered , " You would have no power over me if it were not given to you from above . Therefore the one who handed me over to you is guilty of a greater sin . "
43019012	From then on , Pilate tried to set Jesus free , but the Jewish leaders kept shouting , " If you let this man go , you are no friend of Caesar . Anyone who claims to be a king opposes Caesar . "
43019013	When Pilate heard this , he brought Jesus out and sat down on the judge's seat at a place known as the Stone Pavement ( which in Aramaic is Gabbatha ) .
43019014	It was the day of Preparation of the Passover ; it was about noon . " Here is your king , " Pilate said to the Jews .
43019015	But they shouted , " Take him away ! Take him away ! Crucify him ! " " Shall I crucify your king ? " Pilate asked . " We have no king but Caesar , " the chief priests answered .
43019016	Finally Pilate handed him over to them to be crucified . So the soldiers took charge of Jesus .
43019017	Carrying his own cross , he went out to the place of the Skull ( which in Aramaic is called Golgotha ) .
43019018	There they crucified him , and with him two others — one on each side and Jesus in the middle .
43019019	Pilate had a notice prepared and fastened to the cross . It read : jesus of nazareth , the king of the jews .
43019020	Many of the Jews read this sign , for the place where Jesus was crucified was near the city , and the sign was written in Aramaic , Latin and Greek .
43019021	The chief priests of the Jews protested to Pilate , " Do not write ' The King of the Jews , ' but that this man claimed to be king of the Jews . "
43019022	Pilate answered , " What I have written , I have written . "
43019023	When the soldiers crucified Jesus , they took his clothes , dividing them into four shares , one for each of them , with the undergarment remaining . This garment was seamless , woven in one piece from top to bottom .
43019024	" Let's not tear it , " they said to one another . " Let's decide by lot who will get it . " This happened that the scripture might be fulfilled that said ,
43019025	Near the cross of Jesus stood his mother , his mother's sister , Mary the wife of Clopas , and Mary Magdalene .
43019026	When Jesus saw his mother there , and the disciple whom he loved standing nearby , he said to her , " Woman , here is your son , "
43019027	and to the disciple , " Here is your mother . " From that time on , this disciple took her into his home .
43019028	Later , knowing that everything had now been finished , and so that Scripture would be fulfilled , Jesus said , " I am thirsty . "
43019029	A jar of wine vinegar was there , so they soaked a sponge in it , put the sponge on a stalk of the hyssop plant , and lifted it to Jesus' lips .
43019030	When he had received the drink , Jesus said , " It is finished . " With that , he bowed his head and gave up his spirit .
43019031	Now it was the day of Preparation , and the next day was to be a special Sabbath . Because the Jewish leaders did not want the bodies left on the crosses during the Sabbath , they asked Pilate to have the legs broken and the bodies taken down .
43019032	The soldiers therefore came and broke the legs of the first man who had been crucified with Jesus , and then those of the other .
43019033	But when they came to Jesus and found that he was already dead , they did not break his legs .
43019034	Instead , one of the soldiers pierced Jesus' side with a spear , bringing a sudden flow of blood and water .
43019035	The man who saw it has given testimony , and his testimony is true . He knows that he tells the truth , and he testifies so that you also may believe .
43019036	These things happened so that the scripture would be fulfilled : " Not one of his bones will be broken , "
43019037	and , as another scripture says , " They will look on the one they have pierced . "
43019038	Later , Joseph of Arimathea asked Pilate for the body of Jesus . Now Joseph was a disciple of Jesus , but secretly because he feared the Jewish leaders . With Pilate's permission , he came and took the body away .
43019039	He was accompanied by Nicodemus , the man who earlier had visited Jesus at night . Nicodemus brought a mixture of myrrh and aloes , about seventy-five pounds .
43019040	Taking Jesus' body , the two of them wrapped it , with the spices , in strips of linen . This was in accordance with Jewish burial customs .
43019041	At the place where Jesus was crucified , there was a garden , and in the garden a new tomb , in which no one had ever been laid .
43019042	Because it was the Jewish day of Preparation and since the tomb was nearby , they laid Jesus there .
43020001	Early on the first day of the week , while it was still dark , Mary Magdalene went to the tomb and saw that the stone had been removed from the entrance .
43020002	So she came running to Simon Peter and the other disciple , the one Jesus loved , and said , " They have taken the Lord out of the tomb , and we don't know where they have put him ! "
43020003	So Peter and the other disciple started for the tomb .
43020004	Both were running , but the other disciple outran Peter and reached the tomb first .
43020005	He bent over and looked in at the strips of linen lying there but did not go in .
43020006	Then Simon Peter came along behind him and went straight into the tomb . He saw the strips of linen lying there ,
43020007	as well as the cloth that had been wrapped around Jesus' head . The cloth was still lying in its place , separate from the linen .
43020008	Finally the other disciple , who had reached the tomb first , also went inside . He saw and believed .
43020009	( They still did not understand from Scripture that Jesus had to rise from the dead . )
43020010	Then the disciples went back to where they were staying .
43020011	Now Mary stood outside the tomb crying . As she wept , she bent over to look into the tomb
43020012	and saw two angels in white , seated where Jesus' body had been , one at the head and the other at the foot .
43020013	They asked her , " Woman , why are you crying ? " " They have taken my Lord away , " she said , " and I don't know where they have put him . "
43020014	At this , she turned around and saw Jesus standing there , but she did not realize that it was Jesus .
43020015	He asked her , " Woman , why are you crying ? Who is it you are looking for ? " Thinking he was the gardener , she said , " Sir , if you have carried him away , tell me where you have put him , and I will get him . "
43020016	Jesus said to her , " Mary . " She turned toward him and cried out in Aramaic , " Rabboni ! " ( which means " Teacher " ) .
43020017	Jesus said , " Do not hold on to me , for I have not yet ascended to the Father . Go instead to my brothers and tell them , ' I am ascending to my Father and your Father , to my God and your God . ' "
43020018	Mary Magdalene went to the disciples with the news : " I have seen the Lord ! " And she told them that he had said these things to her .
43020019	On the evening of that first day of the week , when the disciples were together , with the doors locked for fear of the Jewish leaders , Jesus came and stood among them and said , " Peace be with you ! "
43020020	After he said this , he showed them his hands and side . The disciples were overjoyed when they saw the Lord .
43020021	Again Jesus said , " Peace be with you ! As the Father has sent me , I am sending you . "
43020022	And with that he breathed on them and said , " Receive the Holy Spirit .
43020023	If you forgive anyone's sins , their sins are forgiven ; if you do not forgive them , they are not forgiven . "
43020024	Now Thomas ( also known as Didymus ) , one of the Twelve , was not with the disciples when Jesus came .
43020025	So the other disciples told him , " We have seen the Lord ! " But he said to them , " Unless I see the nail marks in his hands and put my finger where the nails were , and put my hand into his side , I will not believe . "
43020026	A week later his disciples were in the house again , and Thomas was with them . Though the doors were locked , Jesus came and stood among them and said , " Peace be with you ! "
43020027	Then he said to Thomas , " Put your finger here ; see my hands . Reach out your hand and put it into my side . Stop doubting and believe . "
43020028	Thomas said to him , " My Lord and my God ! "
43020029	Then Jesus told him , " Because you have seen me , you have believed ; blessed are those who have not seen and yet have believed . "
43020030	Jesus performed many other signs in the presence of his disciples , which are not recorded in this book .
43020031	But these are written that you may believe that Jesus is the Messiah , the Son of God , and that by believing you may have life in his name .
43021001	Afterward Jesus appeared again to his disciples , by the Sea of Galilee . It happened this way :
43021002	Simon Peter , Thomas ( also known as Didymus ) , Nathanael from Cana in Galilee , the sons of Zebedee , and two other disciples were together .
43021003	" I'm going out to fish , " Simon Peter told them , and they said , " We'll go with you . " So they went out and got into the boat , but that night they caught nothing .
43021004	Early in the morning , Jesus stood on the shore , but the disciples did not realize that it was Jesus .
43021005	He called out to them , " Friends , haven't you any fish ? " " No , " they answered .
43021006	He said , " Throw your net on the right side of the boat and you will find some . " When they did , they were unable to haul the net in because of the large number of fish .
43021007	Then the disciple whom Jesus loved said to Peter , " It is the Lord ! " As soon as Simon Peter heard him say , " It is the Lord , " he wrapped his outer garment around him ( for he had taken it off ) and jumped into the water .
43021008	The other disciples followed in the boat , towing the net full of fish , for they were not far from shore , about a hundred yards .
43021009	When they landed , they saw a fire of burning coals there with fish on it , and some bread .
43021010	Jesus said to them , " Bring some of the fish you have just caught . "
43021011	So Simon Peter climbed back into the boat and dragged the net ashore . It was full of large fish , 153 , but even with so many the net was not torn .
43021012	Jesus said to them , " Come and have breakfast . " None of the disciples dared ask him , " Who are you ? " They knew it was the Lord .
43021013	Jesus came , took the bread and gave it to them , and did the same with the fish .
43021014	This was now the third time Jesus appeared to his disciples after he was raised from the dead .
43021015	When they had finished eating , Jesus said to Simon Peter , " Simon son of John , do you love me more than these ? " " Yes , Lord , " he said , " you know that I love you . " Jesus said , " Feed my lambs . "
43021016	Again Jesus said , " Simon son of John , do you love me ? " He answered , " Yes , Lord , you know that I love you . " Jesus said , " Take care of my sheep . "
43021017	The third time he said to him , " Simon son of John , do you love me ? " Peter was hurt because Jesus asked him the third time , " Do you love me ? " He said , " Lord , you know all things ; you know that I love you . " Jesus said , " Feed my sheep .
43021018	Very truly I tell you , when you were younger you dressed yourself and went where you wanted ; but when you are old you will stretch out your hands , and someone else will dress you and lead you where you do not want to go . "
43021019	Jesus said this to indicate the kind of death by which Peter would glorify God . Then he said to him , " Follow me ! "
43021020	Peter turned and saw that the disciple whom Jesus loved was following them . ( This was the one who had leaned back against Jesus at the supper and had said , " Lord , who is going to betray you ? " )
43021021	When Peter saw him , he asked , " Lord , what about him ? "
43021022	Jesus answered , " If I want him to remain alive until I return , what is that to you ? You must follow me . "
43021023	Because of this , the rumor spread among the believers that this disciple would not die . But Jesus did not say that he would not die ; he only said , " If I want him to remain alive until I return , what is that to you ? "
43021024	This is the disciple who testifies to these things and who wrote them down . We know that his testimony is true .
43021025	Jesus did many other things as well . If every one of them were written down , I suppose that even the whole world would not have room for the books that would be written .
45001001	Paul , a servant of Christ Jesus , called to be an apostle and set apart for the gospel of God —
45001002	the gospel he promised beforehand through his prophets in the Holy Scriptures
45001003	regarding his Son , who as to his earthly life was a descendant of David ,
45001004	and who through the Spirit of holiness was appointed the Son of God in power by his resurrection from the dead : Jesus Christ our Lord .
45001005	Through him we received grace and apostleship to call all the Gentiles to the obedience that comes from faith for his name's sake .
45001006	And you also are among those Gentiles who are called to belong to Jesus Christ .
45001007	To all in Rome who are loved by God and called to be his holy people : Grace and peace to you from God our Father and from the Lord Jesus Christ .
45001008	First , I thank my God through Jesus Christ for all of you , because your faith is being reported all over the world .
45001009	God , whom I serve in my spirit in preaching the gospel of his Son , is my witness how constantly I remember you
45001010	in my prayers at all times ; and I pray that now at last by God's will the way may be opened for me to come to you .
45001011	I long to see you so that I may impart to you some spiritual gift to make you strong —
45001012	that is , that you and I may be mutually encouraged by each other's faith .
45001013	I do not want you to be unaware , brothers and sisters , that I planned many times to come to you ( but have been prevented from doing so until now ) in order that I might have a harvest among you , just as I have had among the other Gentiles .
45001014	I am obligated both to Greeks and non-Greeks , both to the wise and the foolish .
45001015	That is why I am so eager to preach the gospel also to you who are in Rome .
45001016	For I am not ashamed of the gospel , because it is the power of God that brings salvation to everyone who believes : first to the Jew , then to the Gentile .
45001017	For in the gospel the righteousness of God is revealed — a righteousness that is by faith from first to last , just as it is written : " The righteous will live by faith . "
45001018	The wrath of God is being revealed from heaven against all the godlessness and wickedness of people , who suppress the truth by their wickedness ,
45001019	since what may be known about God is plain to them , because God has made it plain to them .
45001020	For since the creation of the world God's invisible qualities — his eternal power and divine nature — have been clearly seen , being understood from what has been made , so that people are without excuse .
45001021	For although they knew God , they neither glorified him as God nor gave thanks to him , but their thinking became futile and their foolish hearts were darkened .
45001022	Although they claimed to be wise , they became fools
45001023	and exchanged the glory of the immortal God for images made to look like a mortal human being and birds and animals and reptiles .
45001024	Therefore God gave them over in the sinful desires of their hearts to sexual impurity for the degrading of their bodies with one another .
45001025	They exchanged the truth about God for a lie , and worshiped and served created things rather than the Creator — who is forever praised . Amen .
45001026	Because of this , God gave them over to shameful lusts . Even their women exchanged natural sexual relations for unnatural ones .
45001027	In the same way the men also abandoned natural relations with women and were inflamed with lust for one another . Men committed shameful acts with other men , and received in themselves the due penalty for their error .
45001028	Furthermore , just as they did not think it worthwhile to retain the knowledge of God , so God gave them over to a depraved mind , so that they do what ought not to be done .
45001029	They have become filled with every kind of wickedness , evil , greed and depravity . They are full of envy , murder , strife , deceit and malice . They are gossips ,
45001030	slanderers , God-haters , insolent , arrogant and boastful ; they invent ways of doing evil ; they disobey their parents ;
45001031	they have no understanding , no fidelity , no love , no mercy .
45001032	Although they know God's righteous decree that those who do such things deserve death , they not only continue to do these very things but also approve of those who practice them .
45002001	You , therefore , have no excuse , you who pass judgment on someone else , for at whatever point you judge another , you are condemning yourself , because you who pass judgment do the same things .
45002002	Now we know that God's judgment against those who do such things is based on truth .
45002003	So when you , a mere human being , pass judgment on them and yet do the same things , do you think you will escape God's judgment ?
45002004	Or do you show contempt for the riches of his kindness , forbearance and patience , not realizing that God's kindness is intended to lead you to repentance ?
45002005	But because of your stubbornness and your unrepentant heart , you are storing up wrath against yourself for the day of God's wrath , when his righteous judgment will be revealed .
45002006	God " will repay each person according to what they have done . "
45002007	To those who by persistence in doing good seek glory , honor and immortality , he will give eternal life .
45002008	But for those who are self-seeking and who reject the truth and follow evil , there will be wrath and anger .
45002009	There will be trouble and distress for every human being who does evil : first for the Jew , then for the Gentile ;
45002010	but glory , honor and peace for everyone who does good : first for the Jew , then for the Gentile .
45002011	For God does not show favoritism .
45002012	All who sin apart from the law will also perish apart from the law , and all who sin under the law will be judged by the law .
45002013	For it is not those who hear the law who are righteous in God's sight , but it is those who obey the law who will be declared righteous .
45002014	( Indeed , when Gentiles , who do not have the law , do by nature things required by the law , they are a law for themselves , even though they do not have the law .
45002015	They show that the requirements of the law are written on their hearts , their consciences also bearing witness , and their thoughts sometimes accusing them and at other times even defending them . )
45002016	This will take place on the day when God judges people's secrets through Jesus Christ , as my gospel declares .
45002017	Now you , if you call yourself a Jew ; if you rely on the law and boast in God ;
45002018	if you know his will and approve of what is superior because you are instructed by the law ;
45002019	if you are convinced that you are a guide for the blind , a light for those who are in the dark ,
45002020	an instructor of the foolish , a teacher of little children , because you have in the law the embodiment of knowledge and truth —
45002021	you , then , who teach others , do you not teach yourself ? You who preach against stealing , do you steal ?
45002022	You who say that people should not commit adultery , do you commit adultery ? You who abhor idols , do you rob temples ?
45002023	You who boast in the law , do you dishonor God by breaking the law ?
45002024	As it is written : " God's name is blasphemed among the Gentiles because of you . "
45002025	Circumcision has value if you observe the law , but if you break the law , you have become as though you had not been circumcised .
45002026	So then , if those who are not circumcised keep the law's requirements , will they not be regarded as though they were circumcised ?
45002027	The one who is not circumcised physically and yet obeys the law will condemn you who , even though you have the written code and circumcision , are a lawbreaker .
45002028	A person is not a Jew who is one only outwardly , nor is circumcision merely outward and physical .
45002029	No , a person is a Jew who is one inwardly ; and circumcision is circumcision of the heart , by the Spirit , not by the written code . Such a person's praise is not from other people , but from God .
45003001	What advantage , then , is there in being a Jew , or what value is there in circumcision ?
45003002	Much in every way ! First of all , the Jews have been entrusted with the very words of God .
45003003	What if some were unfaithful ? Will their unfaithfulness nullify God's faithfulness ?
45003004	Not at all ! Let God be true , and every human being a liar . As it is written :
45003006	Certainly not ! If that were so , how could God judge the world ?
45003007	Someone might argue , " If my falsehood enhances God's truthfulness and so increases his glory , why am I still condemned as a sinner ? "
45003008	Why not say — as some slanderously claim that we say — " Let us do evil that good may result " ? Their condemnation is just !
45003009	What shall we conclude then ? Do we have any advantage ? Not at all ! For we have already made the charge that Jews and Gentiles alike are all under the power of sin .
45003010	As it is written :
45003012	All have turned away ,
45003013	" Their throats are open graves ;
45003014	" Their mouths are full of cursing and bitterness . "
45003015	" Their feet are swift to shed blood ;
45003016	ruin and misery mark their ways ,
45003017	and the way of peace they do not know . "
45003018	" There is no fear of God before their eyes . "
45003019	Now we know that whatever the law says , it says to those who are under the law , so that every mouth may be silenced and the whole world held accountable to God .
45003020	Therefore no one will be declared righteous in God's sight by the works of the law ; rather , through the law we become conscious of our sin .
45003021	But now apart from the law the righteousness of God has been made known , to which the Law and the Prophets testify .
45003022	This righteousness is given through faith in Jesus Christ to all who believe . There is no difference between Jew and Gentile ,
45003023	for all have sinned and fall short of the glory of God ,
45003024	and all are justified freely by his grace through the redemption that came by Christ Jesus .
45003025	God presented Christ as a sacrifice of atonement , through the shedding of his blood — to be received by faith . He did this to demonstrate his righteousness , because in his forbearance he had left the sins committed beforehand unpunished —
45003026	he did it to demonstrate his righteousness at the present time , so as to be just and the one who justifies those who have faith in Jesus .
45003027	Where , then , is boasting ? It is excluded . Because of what law ? The law that requires works ? No , because of the law that requires faith .
45003028	For we maintain that a person is justified by faith apart from the works of the law .
45003029	Or is God the God of Jews only ? Is he not the God of Gentiles too ? Yes , of Gentiles too ,
45003030	since there is only one God , who will justify the circumcised by faith and the uncircumcised through that same faith .
45003031	Do we , then , nullify the law by this faith ? Not at all ! Rather , we uphold the law .
45004001	What then shall we say that Abraham , our forefather according to the flesh , discovered in this matter ?
45004002	If , in fact , Abraham was justified by works , he had something to boast about — but not before God .
45004003	What does Scripture say ? " Abraham believed God , and it was credited to him as righteousness . "
45004004	Now to the one who works , wages are not credited as a gift but as an obligation .
45004005	However , to the one who does not work but trusts God who justifies the ungodly , their faith is credited as righteousness .
45004006	David says the same thing when he speaks of the blessedness of the one to whom God credits righteousness apart from works :
45004007	" Blessed are those
45004008	Blessed is the one
45004009	Is this blessedness only for the circumcised , or also for the uncircumcised ? We have been saying that Abraham's faith was credited to him as righteousness .
45004010	Under what circumstances was it credited ? Was it after he was circumcised , or before ? It was not after , but before !
45004011	And he received circumcision as a sign , a seal of the righteousness that he had by faith while he was still uncircumcised . So then , he is the father of all who believe but have not been circumcised , in order that righteousness might be credited to them .
45004012	And he is then also the father of the circumcised who not only are circumcised but who also follow in the footsteps of the faith that our father Abraham had before he was circumcised .
45004013	It was not through the law that Abraham and his offspring received the promise that he would be heir of the world , but through the righteousness that comes by faith .
45004014	For if those who depend on the law are heirs , faith means nothing and the promise is worthless ,
45004015	because the law brings wrath . And where there is no law there is no transgression .
45004016	Therefore , the promise comes by faith , so that it may be by grace and may be guaranteed to all Abraham's offspring — not only to those who are of the law but also to those who have the faith of Abraham . He is the father of us all .
45004017	As it is written : " I have made you a father of many nations . " He is our father in the sight of God , in whom he believed — the God who gives life to the dead and calls into being things that were not .
45004018	Against all hope , Abraham in hope believed and so became the father of many nations , just as it had been said to him , " So shall your offspring be . "
45004019	Without weakening in his faith , he faced the fact that his body was as good as dead — since he was about a hundred years old — and that Sarah's womb was also dead .
45004020	Yet he did not waver through unbelief regarding the promise of God , but was strengthened in his faith and gave glory to God ,
45004021	being fully persuaded that God had power to do what he had promised .
45004022	This is why " it was credited to him as righteousness . "
45004023	The words " it was credited to him " were written not for him alone ,
45004024	but also for us , to whom God will credit righteousness — for us who believe in him who raised Jesus our Lord from the dead .
45004025	He was delivered over to death for our sins and was raised to life for our justification .
45005001	Therefore , since we have been justified through faith , we have peace with God through our Lord Jesus Christ ,
45005002	through whom we have gained access by faith into this grace in which we now stand . And we boast in the hope of the glory of God .
45005003	Not only so , but we also glory in our sufferings , because we know that suffering produces perseverance ;
45005004	perseverance , character ; and character , hope .
45005005	And hope does not put us to shame , because God's love has been poured out into our hearts through the Holy Spirit , who has been given to us .
45005006	You see , at just the right time , when we were still powerless , Christ died for the ungodly .
45005007	Very rarely will anyone die for a righteous person , though for a good person someone might possibly dare to die .
45005008	But God demonstrates his own love for us in this : While we were still sinners , Christ died for us .
45005009	Since we have now been justified by his blood , how much more shall we be saved from God's wrath through him !
45005010	For if , while we were God's enemies , we were reconciled to him through the death of his Son , how much more , having been reconciled , shall we be saved through his life !
45005011	Not only is this so , but we also boast in God through our Lord Jesus Christ , through whom we have now received reconciliation .
45005012	Therefore , just as sin entered the world through one man , and death through sin , and in this way death came to all people , because all sinned —
45005013	To be sure , sin was in the world before the law was given , but sin is not charged against anyone's account where there is no law .
45005014	Nevertheless , death reigned from the time of Adam to the time of Moses , even over those who did not sin by breaking a command , as did Adam , who is a pattern of the one to come .
45005015	But the gift is not like the trespass . For if the many died by the trespass of the one man , how much more did God's grace and the gift that came by the grace of the one man , Jesus Christ , overflow to the many !
45005016	Nor can the gift of God be compared with the result of one man's sin : The judgment followed one sin and brought condemnation , but the gift followed many trespasses and brought justification .
45005017	For if , by the trespass of the one man , death reigned through that one man , how much more will those who receive God's abundant provision of grace and of the gift of righteousness reign in life through the one man , Jesus Christ !
45005018	Consequently , just as one trespass resulted in condemnation for all people , so also one righteous act resulted in justification and life for all people .
45005019	For just as through the disobedience of the one man the many were made sinners , so also through the obedience of the one man the many will be made righteous .
45005020	The law was brought in so that the trespass might increase . But where sin increased , grace increased all the more ,
45005021	so that , just as sin reigned in death , so also grace might reign through righteousness to bring eternal life through Jesus Christ our Lord .
45006001	What shall we say , then ? Shall we go on sinning so that grace may increase ?
45006002	By no means ! We are those who have died to sin ; how can we live in it any longer ?
45006003	Or don't you know that all of us who were baptized into Christ Jesus were baptized into his death ?
45006004	We were therefore buried with him through baptism into death in order that , just as Christ was raised from the dead through the glory of the Father , we too may live a new life .
45006005	For if we have been united with him in a death like his , we will certainly also be united with him in a resurrection like his .
45006006	For we know that our old self was crucified with him so that the body ruled by sin might be done away with , that we should no longer be slaves to sin —
45006007	because anyone who has died has been set free from sin .
45006008	Now if we died with Christ , we believe that we will also live with him .
45006009	For we know that since Christ was raised from the dead , he cannot die again ; death no longer has mastery over him .
45006010	The death he died , he died to sin once for all ; but the life he lives , he lives to God .
45006011	In the same way , count yourselves dead to sin but alive to God in Christ Jesus .
45006012	Therefore do not let sin reign in your mortal body so that you obey its evil desires .
45006013	Do not offer any part of yourself to sin as an instrument of wickedness , but rather offer yourselves to God as those who have been brought from death to life ; and offer every part of yourself to him as an instrument of righteousness .
45006014	For sin shall no longer be your master , because you are not under the law , but under grace .
45006015	What then ? Shall we sin because we are not under the law but under grace ? By no means !
45006016	Don't you know that when you offer yourselves to someone as obedient slaves , you are slaves of the one you obey — whether you are slaves to sin , which leads to death , or to obedience , which leads to righteousness ?
45006017	But thanks be to God that , though you used to be slaves to sin , you have come to obey from your heart the pattern of teaching that has now claimed your allegiance .
45006018	You have been set free from sin and have become slaves to righteousness .
45006019	I am using an example from everyday life because of your human limitations . Just as you used to offer yourselves as slaves to impurity and to ever-increasing wickedness , so now offer yourselves as slaves to righteousness leading to holiness .
45006020	When you were slaves to sin , you were free from the control of righteousness .
45006021	What benefit did you reap at that time from the things you are now ashamed of ? Those things result in death !
45006022	But now that you have been set free from sin and have become slaves of God , the benefit you reap leads to holiness , and the result is eternal life .
