45006023	For the wages of sin is death , but the gift of God is eternal life in Christ Jesus our Lord .
45007001	Do you not know , brothers and sisters — for I am speaking to those who know the law — that the law has authority over someone only as long as that person lives ?
45007002	For example , by law a married woman is bound to her husband as long as he is alive , but if her husband dies , she is released from the law that binds her to him .
45007003	So then , if she has sexual relations with another man while her husband is still alive , she is called an adulteress . But if her husband dies , she is released from that law and is not an adulteress if she marries another man .
45007004	So , my brothers and sisters , you also died to the law through the body of Christ , that you might belong to another , to him who was raised from the dead , in order that we might bear fruit for God .
45007005	For when we were in the realm of the flesh , the sinful passions aroused by the law were at work in us , so that we bore fruit for death .
45007006	But now , by dying to what once bound us , we have been released from the law so that we serve in the new way of the Spirit , and not in the old way of the written code .
45007007	What shall we say , then ? Is the law sinful ? Certainly not ! Nevertheless , I would not have known what sin was had it not been for the law . For I would not have known what coveting really was if the law had not said , " You shall not covet . "
45007008	But sin , seizing the opportunity afforded by the commandment , produced in me every kind of coveting . For apart from the law , sin was dead .
45007009	Once I was alive apart from the law ; but when the commandment came , sin sprang to life and I died .
45007010	I found that the very commandment that was intended to bring life actually brought death .
45007011	For sin , seizing the opportunity afforded by the commandment , deceived me , and through the commandment put me to death .
45007012	So then , the law is holy , and the commandment is holy , righteous and good .
45007013	Did that which is good , then , become death to me ? By no means ! Nevertheless , in order that sin might be recognized as sin , it used what is good to bring about my death , so that through the commandment sin might become utterly sinful .
45007014	We know that the law is spiritual ; but I am unspiritual , sold as a slave to sin .
45007015	I do not understand what I do . For what I want to do I do not do , but what I hate I do .
45007016	And if I do what I do not want to do , I agree that the law is good .
45007017	As it is , it is no longer I myself who do it , but it is sin living in me .
45007018	For I know that good itself does not dwell in me , that is , in my sinful nature . For I have the desire to do what is good , but I cannot carry it out .
45007019	For I do not do the good I want to do , but the evil I do not want to do — this I keep on doing .
45007020	Now if I do what I do not want to do , it is no longer I who do it , but it is sin living in me that does it .
45007021	So I find this law at work : Although I want to do good , evil is right there with me .
45007022	For in my inner being I delight in God's law ;
45007023	but I see another law at work in me , waging war against the law of my mind and making me a prisoner of the law of sin at work within me .
45007024	What a wretched man I am ! Who will rescue me from this body that is subject to death ?
45007025	Thanks be to God , who delivers me through Jesus Christ our Lord ! So then , I myself in my mind am a slave to God's law , but in my sinful nature a slave to the law of sin .
45008001	Therefore , there is now no condemnation for those who are in Christ Jesus ,
45008002	because through Christ Jesus the law of the Spirit who gives life has set you free from the law of sin and death .
45008003	For what the law was powerless to do because it was weakened by the flesh , God did by sending his own Son in the likeness of sinful flesh to be a sin offering . And so he condemned sin in the flesh ,
45008004	in order that the righteous requirement of the law might be fully met in us , who do not live according to the flesh but according to the Spirit .
45008005	Those who live according to the flesh have their minds set on what the flesh desires ; but those who live in accordance with the Spirit have their minds set on what the Spirit desires .
45008006	The mind governed by the flesh is death , but the mind governed by the Spirit is life and peace .
45008007	The mind governed by the flesh is hostile to God ; it does not submit to God's law , nor can it do so .
45008008	Those who are in the realm of the flesh cannot please God .
45008009	You , however , are not in the realm of the flesh but are in the realm of the Spirit , if indeed the Spirit of God lives in you . And if anyone does not have the Spirit of Christ , they do not belong to Christ .
45008010	But if Christ is in you , then even though your body is subject to death because of sin , the Spirit gives life because of righteousness .
45008011	And if the Spirit of him who raised Jesus from the dead is living in you , he who raised Christ from the dead will also give life to your mortal bodies because of his Spirit who lives in you .
45008012	Therefore , brothers and sisters , we have an obligation — but it is not to the flesh , to live according to it .
45008013	For if you live according to the flesh , you will die ; but if by the Spirit you put to death the misdeeds of the body , you will live .
45008014	For those who are led by the Spirit of God are the children of God .
45008015	The Spirit you received does not make you slaves , so that you live in fear again ; rather , the Spirit you received brought about your adoption to sonship . And by him we cry , " Abba , Father . "
45008016	The Spirit himself testifies with our spirit that we are God's children .
45008017	Now if we are children , then we are heirs — heirs of God and co-heirs with Christ , if indeed we share in his sufferings in order that we may also share in his glory .
45008018	I consider that our present sufferings are not worth comparing with the glory that will be revealed in us .
45008019	For the creation waits in eager expectation for the children of God to be revealed .
45008020	For the creation was subjected to frustration , not by its own choice , but by the will of the one who subjected it , in hope
45008021	that the creation itself will be liberated from its bondage to decay and brought into the freedom and glory of the children of God .
45008022	We know that the whole creation has been groaning as in the pains of childbirth right up to the present time .
45008023	Not only so , but we ourselves , who have the firstfruits of the Spirit , groan inwardly as we wait eagerly for our adoption to sonship , the redemption of our bodies .
45008024	For in this hope we were saved . But hope that is seen is no hope at all . Who hopes for what they already have ?
45008025	But if we hope for what we do not yet have , we wait for it patiently .
45008026	In the same way , the Spirit helps us in our weakness . We do not know what we ought to pray for , but the Spirit himself intercedes for us through wordless groans .
45008027	And he who searches our hearts knows the mind of the Spirit , because the Spirit intercedes for God's people in accordance with the will of God .
45008028	And we know that in all things God works for the good of those who love him , who have been called according to his purpose .
45008029	For those God foreknew he also predestined to be conformed to the image of his Son , that he might be the firstborn among many brothers and sisters .
45008030	And those he predestined , he also called ; those he called , he also justified ; those he justified , he also glorified .
45008031	What , then , shall we say in response to these things ? If God is for us , who can be against us ?
45008032	He who did not spare his own Son , but gave him up for us all — how will he not also , along with him , graciously give us all things ?
45008033	Who will bring any charge against those whom God has chosen ? It is God who justifies .
45008034	Who then is the one who condemns ? No one . Christ Jesus who died — more than that , who was raised to life — is at the right hand of God and is also interceding for us .
45008035	Who shall separate us from the love of Christ ? Shall trouble or hardship or persecution or famine or nakedness or danger or sword ?
45008036	As it is written :
45008038	For I am convinced that neither death nor life , neither angels nor demons , neither the present nor the future , nor any powers ,
45008039	neither height nor depth , nor anything else in all creation , will be able to separate us from the love of God that is in Christ Jesus our Lord .
45009001	I speak the truth in Christ — I am not lying , my conscience confirms it through the Holy Spirit —
45009002	I have great sorrow and unceasing anguish in my heart .
45009003	For I could wish that I myself were cursed and cut off from Christ for the sake of my people , those of my own race ,
45009004	the people of Israel . Theirs is the adoption to sonship ; theirs the divine glory , the covenants , the receiving of the law , the temple worship and the promises .
45009005	Theirs are the patriarchs , and from them is traced the human ancestry of the Messiah , who is God over all , forever praised ! Amen .
45009006	It is not as though God's word had failed . For not all who are descended from Israel are Israel .
45009007	Nor because they are his descendants are they all Abraham's children . On the contrary , " It is through Isaac that your offspring will be reckoned . "
45009008	In other words , it is not the children by physical descent who are God's children , but it is the children of the promise who are regarded as Abraham's offspring .
45009009	For this was how the promise was stated : " At the appointed time I will return , and Sarah will have a son . "
45009010	Not only that , but Rebekah's children were conceived at the same time by our father Isaac .
45009011	Yet , before the twins were born or had done anything good or bad — in order that God's purpose in election might stand :
45009012	not by works but by him who calls — she was told , " The older will serve the younger . "
45009013	Just as it is written : " Jacob I loved , but Esau I hated . "
45009014	What then shall we say ? Is God unjust ? Not at all !
45009015	For he says to Moses ,
45009017	For Scripture says to Pharaoh : " I raised you up for this very purpose , that I might display my power in you and that my name might be proclaimed in all the earth . "
45009018	Therefore God has mercy on whom he wants to have mercy , and he hardens whom he wants to harden .
45009019	One of you will say to me : " Then why does God still blame us ? For who is able to resist his will ? "
45009020	But who are you , a human being , to talk back to God ? " Shall what is formed say to the one who formed it , ' Why did you make me like this ? ' "
45009021	Does not the potter have the right to make out of the same lump of clay some pottery for special purposes and some for common use ?
45009022	What if God , although choosing to show his wrath and make his power known , bore with great patience the objects of his wrath — prepared for destruction ?
45009023	What if he did this to make the riches of his glory known to the objects of his mercy , whom he prepared in advance for glory —
45009024	even us , whom he also called , not only from the Jews but also from the Gentiles ?
45009025	As he says in Hosea :
45009027	Isaiah cries out concerning Israel :
45009028	For the Lord will carry out
45009029	It is just as Isaiah said previously :
45009030	What then shall we say ? That the Gentiles , who did not pursue righteousness , have obtained it , a righteousness that is by faith ;
45009031	but the people of Israel , who pursued the law as the way of righteousness , have not attained their goal .
45009032	Why not ? Because they pursued it not by faith but as if it were by works . They stumbled over the stumbling stone .
45009033	As it is written :
45010001	Brothers and sisters , my heart's desire and prayer to God for the Israelites is that they may be saved .
45010002	For I can testify about them that they are zealous for God , but their zeal is not based on knowledge .
45010003	Since they did not know the righteousness of God and sought to establish their own , they did not submit to God's righteousness .
45010004	Christ is the culmination of the law so that there may be righteousness for everyone who believes .
45010005	Moses writes this about the righteousness that is by the law : " The person who does these things will live by them . "
45010006	But the righteousness that is by faith says : " Do not say in your heart , ' Who will ascend into heaven ? ' " ( that is , to bring Christ down )
45010007	" or ' Who will descend into the deep ? ' " ( that is , to bring Christ up from the dead ) .
45010008	But what does it say ? " The word is near you ; it is in your mouth and in your heart , " that is , the message concerning faith that we proclaim :
45010009	If you declare with your mouth , " Jesus is Lord , " and believe in your heart that God raised him from the dead , you will be saved .
45010010	For it is with your heart that you believe and are justified , and it is with your mouth that you profess your faith and are saved .
45010011	As Scripture says , " Anyone who believes in him will never be put to shame . "
45010012	For there is no difference between Jew and Gentile — the same Lord is Lord of all and richly blesses all who call on him ,
45010013	for , " Everyone who calls on the name of the Lord will be saved . "
45010014	How , then , can they call on the one they have not believed in ? And how can they believe in the one of whom they have not heard ? And how can they hear without someone preaching to them ?
45010015	And how can anyone preach unless they are sent ? As it is written : " How beautiful are the feet of those who bring good news ! "
45010016	But not all the Israelites accepted the good news . For Isaiah says , " Lord , who has believed our message ? "
45010017	Consequently , faith comes from hearing the message , and the message is heard through the word about Christ .
45010018	But I ask : Did they not hear ? Of course they did :
45010020	And Isaiah boldly says ,
45010021	But concerning Israel he says ,
45011001	I ask then : Did God reject his people ? By no means ! I am an Israelite myself , a descendant of Abraham , from the tribe of Benjamin .
45011002	God did not reject his people , whom he foreknew . Don't you know what Scripture says in the passage about Elijah — how he appealed to God against Israel :
45011003	" Lord , they have killed your prophets and torn down your altars ; I am the only one left , and they are trying to kill me " ?
45011004	And what was God's answer to him ? " I have reserved for myself seven thousand who have not bowed the knee to Baal . "
45011005	So too , at the present time there is a remnant chosen by grace .
45011006	And if by grace , then it cannot be based on works ; if it were , grace would no longer be grace .
45011007	What then ? What the people of Israel sought so earnestly they did not obtain . The elect among them did , but the others were hardened ,
45011008	as it is written :
45011010	May their eyes be darkened so they cannot see ,
45011011	Again I ask : Did they stumble so as to fall beyond recovery ? Not at all ! Rather , because of their transgression , salvation has come to the Gentiles to make Israel envious .
45011012	But if their transgression means riches for the world , and their loss means riches for the Gentiles , how much greater riches will their full inclusion bring !
45011013	I am talking to you Gentiles . Inasmuch as I am the apostle to the Gentiles , I take pride in my ministry
45011014	in the hope that I may somehow arouse my own people to envy and save some of them .
45011015	For if their rejection brought reconciliation to the world , what will their acceptance be but life from the dead ?
45011016	If the part of the dough offered as firstfruits is holy , then the whole batch is holy ; if the root is holy , so are the branches .
45011017	If some of the branches have been broken off , and you , though a wild olive shoot , have been grafted in among the others and now share in the nourishing sap from the olive root ,
45011018	do not consider yourself to be superior to those other branches . If you do , consider this : You do not support the root , but the root supports you .
45011019	You will say then , " Branches were broken off so that I could be grafted in . "
45011020	Granted . But they were broken off because of unbelief , and you stand by faith . Do not be arrogant , but tremble .
45011021	For if God did not spare the natural branches , he will not spare you either .
45011022	Consider therefore the kindness and sternness of God : sternness to those who fell , but kindness to you , provided that you continue in his kindness . Otherwise , you also will be cut off .
45011023	And if they do not persist in unbelief , they will be grafted in , for God is able to graft them in again .
45011024	After all , if you were cut out of an olive tree that is wild by nature , and contrary to nature were grafted into a cultivated olive tree , how much more readily will these , the natural branches , be grafted into their own olive tree !
45011025	I do not want you to be ignorant of this mystery , brothers and sisters , so that you may not be conceited : Israel has experienced a hardening in part until the full number of the Gentiles has come in ,
45011026	and in this way all Israel will be saved . As it is written :
45011028	As far as the gospel is concerned , they are enemies for your sake ; but as far as election is concerned , they are loved on account of the patriarchs ,
45011029	for God's gifts and his call are irrevocable .
45011030	Just as you who were at one time disobedient to God have now received mercy as a result of their disobedience ,
45011031	so they too have now become disobedient in order that they too may now receive mercy as a result of God's mercy to you .
45011032	For God has bound everyone over to disobedience so that he may have mercy on them all .
45011033	Oh , the depth of the riches of the wisdom and knowledge of God !
45011035	" Who has ever given to God ,
45011036	For from him and through him and for him are all things .
45012001	Therefore , I urge you , brothers and sisters , in view of God's mercy , to offer your bodies as a living sacrifice , holy and pleasing to God — this is your true and proper worship .
45012002	Do not conform to the pattern of this world , but be transformed by the renewing of your mind . Then you will be able to test and approve what God's will is — his good , pleasing and perfect will .
45012003	For by the grace given me I say to every one of you : Do not think of yourself more highly than you ought , but rather think of yourself with sober judgment , in accordance with the faith God has distributed to each of you .
45012004	For just as each of us has one body with many members , and these members do not all have the same function ,
45012005	so in Christ we , though many , form one body , and each member belongs to all the others .
45012006	We have different gifts , according to the grace given to each of us . If your gift is prophesying , then prophesy in accordance with your faith ;
45012007	if it is serving , then serve ; if it is teaching , then teach ;
45012008	if it is to encourage , then give encouragement ; if it is giving , then give generously ; if it is to lead , do it diligently ; if it is to show mercy , do it cheerfully .
45012009	Love must be sincere . Hate what is evil ; cling to what is good .
45012010	Be devoted to one another in love . Honor one another above yourselves .
45012011	Never be lacking in zeal , but keep your spiritual fervor , serving the Lord .
45012012	Be joyful in hope , patient in affliction , faithful in prayer .
45012013	Share with the Lord's people who are in need . Practice hospitality .
45012014	Bless those who persecute you ; bless and do not curse .
45012015	Rejoice with those who rejoice ; mourn with those who mourn .
45012016	Live in harmony with one another . Do not be proud , but be willing to associate with people of low position . Do not be conceited .
45012017	Do not repay anyone evil for evil . Be careful to do what is right in the eyes of everyone .
45012018	If it is possible , as far as it depends on you , live at peace with everyone .
45012019	Do not take revenge , my dear friends , but leave room for God's wrath , for it is written : " It is mine to avenge ; I will repay , " says the Lord .
45012020	On the contrary :
45013001	Let everyone be subject to the governing authorities , for there is no authority except that which God has established . The authorities that exist have been established by God .
45013002	Consequently , whoever rebels against the authority is rebelling against what God has instituted , and those who do so will bring judgment on themselves .
45013003	For rulers hold no terror for those who do right , but for those who do wrong . Do you want to be free from fear of the one in authority ? Then do what is right and you will be commended .
45013004	For the one in authority is God's servant for your good . But if you do wrong , be afraid , for rulers do not bear the sword for no reason . They are God's servants , agents of wrath to bring punishment on the wrongdoer .
45013005	Therefore , it is necessary to submit to the authorities , not only because of possible punishment but also as a matter of conscience .
45013006	This is also why you pay taxes , for the authorities are God's servants , who give their full time to governing .
45013007	Give to everyone what you owe them : If you owe taxes , pay taxes ; if revenue , then revenue ; if respect , then respect ; if honor , then honor .
45013008	Let no debt remain outstanding , except the continuing debt to love one another , for whoever loves others has fulfilled the law .
45013009	The commandments , " You shall not commit adultery , " " You shall not murder , " " You shall not steal , " " You shall not covet , " and whatever other command there may be , are summed up in this one command : " Love your neighbor as yourself . "
45013010	Love does no harm to a neighbor . Therefore love is the fulfillment of the law .
45013011	And do this , understanding the present time : The hour has already come for you to wake up from your slumber , because our salvation is nearer now than when we first believed .
45013012	The night is nearly over ; the day is almost here . So let us put aside the deeds of darkness and put on the armor of light .
45013013	Let us behave decently , as in the daytime , not in carousing and drunkenness , not in sexual immorality and debauchery , not in dissension and jealousy .
45013014	Rather , clothe yourselves with the Lord Jesus Christ , and do not think about how to gratify the desires of the flesh .
45014001	Accept the one whose faith is weak , without quarreling over disputable matters .
45014002	One person's faith allows them to eat anything , but another , whose faith is weak , eats only vegetables .
45014003	The one who eats everything must not treat with contempt the one who does not , and the one who does not eat everything must not judge the one who does , for God has accepted them .
45014004	Who are you to judge someone else's servant ? To their own master , servants stand or fall . And they will stand , for the Lord is able to make them stand .
45014005	One person considers one day more sacred than another ; another considers every day alike . Each of them should be fully convinced in their own mind .
45014006	Whoever regards one day as special does so to the Lord . Whoever eats meat does so to the Lord , for they give thanks to God ; and whoever abstains does so to the Lord and gives thanks to God .
45014007	For none of us lives for ourselves alone , and none of us dies for ourselves alone .
45014008	If we live , we live for the Lord ; and if we die , we die for the Lord . So , whether we live or die , we belong to the Lord .
45014009	For this very reason , Christ died and returned to life so that he might be the Lord of both the dead and the living .
45014010	You , then , why do you judge your brother or sister ? Or why do you treat them with contempt ? For we will all stand before God's judgment seat .
45014011	It is written :
45014013	Therefore let us stop passing judgment on one another . Instead , make up your mind not to put any stumbling block or obstacle in the way of a brother or sister .
45014014	I am convinced , being fully persuaded in the Lord Jesus , that nothing is unclean in itself . But if anyone regards something as unclean , then for that person it is unclean .
45014015	If your brother or sister is distressed because of what you eat , you are no longer acting in love . Do not by your eating destroy someone for whom Christ died .
45014016	Therefore do not let what you know is good be spoken of as evil .
45014017	For the kingdom of God is not a matter of eating and drinking , but of righteousness , peace and joy in the Holy Spirit ,
45014018	because anyone who serves Christ in this way is pleasing to God and receives human approval .
45014019	Let us therefore make every effort to do what leads to peace and to mutual edification .
45014020	Do not destroy the work of God for the sake of food . All food is clean , but it is wrong for a person to eat anything that causes someone else to stumble .
45014021	It is better not to eat meat or drink wine or to do anything else that will cause your brother or sister to fall .
45014022	So whatever you believe about these things keep between yourself and God . Blessed is the one who does not condemn himself by what he approves .
45014023	But whoever has doubts is condemned if they eat , because their eating is not from faith ; and everything that does not come from faith is sin .
45015001	We who are strong ought to bear with the failings of the weak and not to please ourselves .
45015002	Each of us should please our neighbors for their good , to build them up .
45015003	For even Christ did not please himself but , as it is written : " The insults of those who insult you have fallen on me . "
45015004	For everything that was written in the past was written to teach us , so that through the endurance taught in the Scriptures and the encouragement they provide we might have hope .
45015005	May the God who gives endurance and encouragement give you the same attitude of mind toward each other that Christ Jesus had ,
45015006	so that with one mind and one voice you may glorify the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ .
45015007	Accept one another , then , just as Christ accepted you , in order to bring praise to God .
45015008	For I tell you that Christ has become a servant of the Jews on behalf of God's truth , so that the promises made to the patriarchs might be confirmed
45015009	and , moreover , that the Gentiles might glorify God for his mercy . As it is written :
45015011	And again ,
45015012	And again , Isaiah says ,
45015013	May the God of hope fill you with all joy and peace as you trust in him , so that you may overflow with hope by the power of the Holy Spirit .
45015014	I myself am convinced , my brothers and sisters , that you yourselves are full of goodness , filled with knowledge and competent to instruct one another .
45015015	Yet I have written you quite boldly on some points to remind you of them again , because of the grace God gave me
45015016	to be a minister of Christ Jesus to the Gentiles . He gave me the priestly duty of proclaiming the gospel of God , so that the Gentiles might become an offering acceptable to God , sanctified by the Holy Spirit .
45015017	Therefore I glory in Christ Jesus in my service to God .
45015018	I will not venture to speak of anything except what Christ has accomplished through me in leading the Gentiles to obey God by what I have said and done —
45015019	by the power of signs and wonders , through the power of the Spirit of God . So from Jerusalem all the way around to Illyricum , I have fully proclaimed the gospel of Christ .
45015020	It has always been my ambition to preach the gospel where Christ was not known , so that I would not be building on someone else's foundation .
45015021	Rather , as it is written :
45015023	But now that there is no more place for me to work in these regions , and since I have been longing for many years to visit you ,
45015024	I plan to do so when I go to Spain . I hope to see you while passing through and to have you assist me on my journey there , after I have enjoyed your company for a while .
45015025	Now , however , I am on my way to Jerusalem in the service of the Lord's people there .
45015026	For Macedonia and Achaia were pleased to make a contribution for the poor among the Lord's people in Jerusalem .
45015027	They were pleased to do it , and indeed they owe it to them . For if the Gentiles have shared in the Jews' spiritual blessings , they owe it to the Jews to share with them their material blessings .
45015028	So after I have completed this task and have made sure that they have received this contribution , I will go to Spain and visit you on the way .
45015029	I know that when I come to you , I will come in the full measure of the blessing of Christ .
45015030	I urge you , brothers and sisters , by our Lord Jesus Christ and by the love of the Spirit , to join me in my struggle by praying to God for me .
45015031	Pray that I may be kept safe from the unbelievers in Judea and that the contribution I take to Jerusalem may be favorably received by the Lord's people there ,
45015032	so that I may come to you with joy , by God's will , and in your company be refreshed .
45015033	The God of peace be with you all . Amen .
45016001	I commend to you our sister Phoebe , a deacon of the church in Cenchreae .
45016002	I ask you to receive her in the Lord in a way worthy of his people and to give her any help she may need from you , for she has been the benefactor of many people , including me .
45016003	Greet Priscilla and Aquila , my co-workers in Christ Jesus .
45016004	They risked their lives for me . Not only I but all the churches of the Gentiles are grateful to them .
45016005	Greet also the church that meets at their house . Greet my dear friend Epenetus , who was the first convert to Christ in the province of Asia .
45016006	Greet Mary , who worked very hard for you .
45016007	Greet Andronicus and Junia , my fellow Jews who have been in prison with me . They are outstanding among the apostles , and they were in Christ before I was .
45016008	Greet Ampliatus , my dear friend in the Lord .
45016009	Greet Urbanus , our co-worker in Christ , and my dear friend Stachys .
45016010	Greet Apelles , whose fidelity to Christ has stood the test . Greet those who belong to the household of Aristobulus .
45016011	Greet Herodion , my fellow Jew . Greet those in the household of Narcissus who are in the Lord .
45016012	Greet Tryphena and Tryphosa , those women who work hard in the Lord . Greet my dear friend Persis , another woman who has worked very hard in the Lord .
45016013	Greet Rufus , chosen in the Lord , and his mother , who has been a mother to me , too .
45016014	Greet Asyncritus , Phlegon , Hermes , Patrobas , Hermas and the other brothers and sisters with them .
45016015	Greet Philologus , Julia , Nereus and his sister , and Olympas and all the Lord's people who are with them .
45016016	Greet one another with a holy kiss . All the churches of Christ send greetings .
45016017	I urge you , brothers and sisters , to watch out for those who cause divisions and put obstacles in your way that are contrary to the teaching you have learned . Keep away from them .
45016018	For such people are not serving our Lord Christ , but their own appetites . By smooth talk and flattery they deceive the minds of naive people .
45016019	Everyone has heard about your obedience , so I rejoice because of you ; but I want you to be wise about what is good , and innocent about what is evil .
45016020	The God of peace will soon crush Satan under your feet . The grace of our Lord Jesus be with you .
45016021	Timothy , my co-worker , sends his greetings to you , as do Lucius , Jason and Sosipater , my fellow Jews .
45016022	I , Tertius , who wrote down this letter , greet you in the Lord .
45016023	Gaius , whose hospitality I and the whole church here enjoy , sends you his greetings . Erastus , who is the city's director of public works , and our brother Quartus send you their greetings .
45016025	Now to him who is able to establish you in accordance with my gospel , the message I proclaim about Jesus Christ , in keeping with the revelation of the mystery hidden for long ages past ,
45016026	but now revealed and made known through the prophetic writings by the command of the eternal God , so that all the Gentiles might come to the obedience that comes from faith —
45016027	to the only wise God be glory forever through Jesus Christ ! Amen .
46001001	Paul , called to be an apostle of Christ Jesus by the will of God , and our brother Sosthenes ,
46001002	To the church of God in Corinth , to those sanctified in Christ Jesus and called to be his holy people , together with all those everywhere who call on the name of our Lord Jesus Christ — their Lord and ours :
46001003	Grace and peace to you from God our Father and the Lord Jesus Christ .
46001004	I always thank my God for you because of his grace given you in Christ Jesus .
46001005	For in him you have been enriched in every way — with all kinds of speech and with all knowledge —
46001006	God thus confirming our testimony about Christ among you .
46001007	Therefore you do not lack any spiritual gift as you eagerly wait for our Lord Jesus Christ to be revealed .
46001008	He will also keep you firm to the end , so that you will be blameless on the day of our Lord Jesus Christ .
46001009	God is faithful , who has called you into fellowship with his Son , Jesus Christ our Lord .
46001010	I appeal to you , brothers and sisters , in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ , that all of you agree with one another in what you say and that there be no divisions among you , but that you be perfectly united in mind and thought .
46001011	My brothers and sisters , some from Chloe's household have informed me that there are quarrels among you .
46001012	What I mean is this : One of you says , " I follow Paul " ; another , " I follow Apollos " ; another , " I follow Cephas " ; still another , " I follow Christ . "
46001013	Is Christ divided ? Was Paul crucified for you ? Were you baptized in the name of Paul ?
46001014	I thank God that I did not baptize any of you except Crispus and Gaius ,
46001015	so no one can say that you were baptized in my name .
46001016	( Yes , I also baptized the household of Stephanas ; beyond that , I don't remember if I baptized anyone else . )
46001017	For Christ did not send me to baptize , but to preach the gospel — not with wisdom and eloquence , lest the cross of Christ be emptied of its power .
46001018	For the message of the cross is foolishness to those who are perishing , but to us who are being saved it is the power of God .
46001019	For it is written :
46001021	For since in the wisdom of God the world through its wisdom did not know him , God was pleased through the foolishness of what was preached to save those who believe .
46001022	Jews demand signs and Greeks look for wisdom ,
46001023	but we preach Christ crucified : a stumbling block to Jews and foolishness to Gentiles ,
46001024	but to those whom God has called , both Jews and Greeks , Christ the power of God and the wisdom of God .
46001025	For the foolishness of God is wiser than human wisdom , and the weakness of God is stronger than human strength .
46001026	Brothers and sisters , think of what you were when you were called . Not many of you were wise by human standards ; not many were influential ; not many were of noble birth .
46001027	But God chose the foolish things of the world to shame the wise ; God chose the weak things of the world to shame the strong .
46001028	God chose the lowly things of this world and the despised things — and the things that are not — to nullify the things that are ,
46001029	so that no one may boast before him .
46001030	It is because of him that you are in Christ Jesus , who has become for us wisdom from God — that is , our righteousness , holiness and redemption .
46001031	Therefore , as it is written : " Let the one who boasts boast in the Lord . "
46002001	And so it was with me , brothers and sisters . When I came to you , I did not come with eloquence or human wisdom as I proclaimed to you the testimony about God .
46002002	For I resolved to know nothing while I was with you except Jesus Christ and him crucified .
46002003	I came to you in weakness with great fear and trembling .
46002004	My message and my preaching were not with wise and persuasive words , but with a demonstration of the Spirit's power ,
46002005	so that your faith might not rest on human wisdom , but on God's power .
46002006	We do , however , speak a message of wisdom among the mature , but not the wisdom of this age or of the rulers of this age , who are coming to nothing .
46002007	No , we declare God's wisdom , a mystery that has been hidden and that God destined for our glory before time began .
46002008	None of the rulers of this age understood it , for if they had , they would not have crucified the Lord of glory .
46002009	However , as it is written :
46002011	For who knows a person's thoughts except their own spirit within them ? In the same way no one knows the thoughts of God except the Spirit of God .
46002012	What we have received is not the spirit of the world , but the Spirit who is from God , so that we may understand what God has freely given us .
46002013	This is what we speak , not in words taught us by human wisdom but in words taught by the Spirit , explaining spiritual realities with Spirit-taught words .
46002014	The person without the Spirit does not accept the things that come from the Spirit of God but considers them foolishness , and cannot understand them because they are discerned only through the Spirit .
46002015	The person with the Spirit makes judgments about all things , but such a person is not subject to merely human judgments ,
46002016	for , " Who has known the mind of the Lord so as to instruct him ? " But we have the mind of Christ .
46003001	Brothers and sisters , I could not address you as people who live by the Spirit but as people who are still worldly — mere infants in Christ .
46003002	I gave you milk , not solid food , for you were not yet ready for it . Indeed , you are still not ready .
46003003	You are still worldly . For since there is jealousy and quarreling among you , are you not worldly ? Are you not acting like mere humans ?
46003004	For when one says , " I follow Paul , " and another , " I follow Apollos , " are you not mere human beings ?
46003005	What , after all , is Apollos ? And what is Paul ? Only servants , through whom you came to believe — as the Lord has assigned to each his task .
46003006	I planted the seed , Apollos watered it , but God has been making it grow .
46003007	So neither the one who plants nor the one who waters is anything , but only God , who makes things grow .
46003008	The one who plants and the one who waters have one purpose , and they will each be rewarded according to their own labor .
46003009	For we are co-workers in God's service ; you are God's field , God's building .
46003010	By the grace God has given me , I laid a foundation as a wise builder , and someone else is building on it . But each one should build with care .
46003011	For no one can lay any foundation other than the one already laid , which is Jesus Christ .
46003012	If anyone builds on this foundation using gold , silver , costly stones , wood , hay or straw ,
46003013	their work will be shown for what it is , because the Day will bring it to light . It will be revealed with fire , and the fire will test the quality of each person's work .
46003014	If what has been built survives , the builder will receive a reward .
46003015	If it is burned up , the builder will suffer loss but yet will be saved — even though only as one escaping through the flames .
46003016	Don't you know that you yourselves are God's temple and that God's Spirit dwells in your midst ?
46003017	If anyone destroys God's temple , God will destroy that person ; for God's temple is sacred , and you together are that temple .
46003018	Do not deceive yourselves . If any of you think you are wise by the standards of this age , you should become " fools " so that you may become wise .
46003019	For the wisdom of this world is foolishness in God's sight . As it is written : " He catches the wise in their craftiness " ;
46003020	and again , " The Lord knows that the thoughts of the wise are futile . "
46003021	So then , no more boasting about human leaders ! All things are yours ,
46003022	whether Paul or Apollos or Cephas or the world or life or death or the present or the future — all are yours ,
46003023	and you are of Christ , and Christ is of God .
46004001	This , then , is how you ought to regard us : as servants of Christ and as those entrusted with the mysteries God has revealed .
46004002	Now it is required that those who have been given a trust must prove faithful .
46004003	I care very little if I am judged by you or by any human court ; indeed , I do not even judge myself .
46004004	My conscience is clear , but that does not make me innocent . It is the Lord who judges me .
46004005	Therefore judge nothing before the appointed time ; wait until the Lord comes . He will bring to light what is hidden in darkness and will expose the motives of the heart . At that time each will receive their praise from God .
46004006	Now , brothers and sisters , I have applied these things to myself and Apollos for your benefit , so that you may learn from us the meaning of the saying , " Do not go beyond what is written . " Then you will not be puffed up in being a follower of one of us over against the other .
46004007	For who makes you different from anyone else ? What do you have that you did not receive ? And if you did receive it , why do you boast as though you did not ?
46004008	Already you have all you want ! Already you have become rich ! You have begun to reign — and that without us ! How I wish that you really had begun to reign so that we also might reign with you !
46004009	For it seems to me that God has put us apostles on display at the end of the procession , like those condemned to die in the arena . We have been made a spectacle to the whole universe , to angels as well as to human beings .
46004010	We are fools for Christ , but you are so wise in Christ ! We are weak , but you are strong ! You are honored , we are dishonored !
46004011	To this very hour we go hungry and thirsty , we are in rags , we are brutally treated , we are homeless .
46004012	We work hard with our own hands . When we are cursed , we bless ; when we are persecuted , we endure it ;
46004013	when we are slandered , we answer kindly . We have become the scum of the earth , the garbage of the world — right up to this moment .
46004014	I am writing this not to shame you but to warn you as my dear children .
46004015	Even if you had ten thousand guardians in Christ , you do not have many fathers , for in Christ Jesus I became your father through the gospel .
46004016	Therefore I urge you to imitate me .
46004017	For this reason I have sent to you Timothy , my son whom I love , who is faithful in the Lord . He will remind you of my way of life in Christ Jesus , which agrees with what I teach everywhere in every church .
46004018	Some of you have become arrogant , as if I were not coming to you .
46004019	But I will come to you very soon , if the Lord is willing , and then I will find out not only how these arrogant people are talking , but what power they have .
46004020	For the kingdom of God is not a matter of talk but of power .
46004021	What do you prefer ? Shall I come to you with a rod of discipline , or shall I come in love and with a gentle spirit ?
46005001	It is actually reported that there is sexual immorality among you , and of a kind that even pagans do not tolerate : A man is sleeping with his father's wife .
46005002	And you are proud ! Shouldn't you rather have gone into mourning and have put out of your fellowship the man who has been doing this ?
46005003	For my part , even though I am not physically present , I am with you in spirit . As one who is present with you in this way , I have already passed judgment in the name of our Lord Jesus on the one who has been doing this .
46005004	So when you are assembled and I am with you in spirit , and the power of our Lord Jesus is present ,
46005005	hand this man over to Satan for the destruction of the flesh , so that his spirit may be saved on the day of the Lord .
46005006	Your boasting is not good . Don't you know that a little yeast leavens the whole batch of dough ?
46005007	Get rid of the old yeast , so that you may be a new unleavened batch — as you really are . For Christ , our Passover lamb , has been sacrificed .
46005008	Therefore let us keep the Festival , not with the old bread leavened with malice and wickedness , but with the unleavened bread of sincerity and truth .
46005009	I wrote to you in my letter not to associate with sexually immoral people —
46005010	not at all meaning the people of this world who are immoral , or the greedy and swindlers , or idolaters . In that case you would have to leave this world .
46005011	But now I am writing to you that you must not associate with anyone who claims to be a brother or sister but is sexually immoral or greedy , an idolater or slanderer , a drunkard or swindler . Do not even eat with such people .
46005012	What business is it of mine to judge those outside the church ? Are you not to judge those inside ?
46005013	God will judge those outside . " Expel the wicked person from among you . "
46006001	If any of you has a dispute with another , do you dare to take it before the ungodly for judgment instead of before the Lord's people ?
46006002	Or do you not know that the Lord's people will judge the world ? And if you are to judge the world , are you not competent to judge trivial cases ?
46006003	Do you not know that we will judge angels ? How much more the things of this life !
46006004	Therefore , if you have disputes about such matters , do you ask for a ruling from those whose way of life is scorned in the church ?
46006005	I say this to shame you . Is it possible that there is nobody among you wise enough to judge a dispute between believers ?
46006006	But instead , one brother takes another to court — and this in front of unbelievers !
46006007	The very fact that you have lawsuits among you means you have been completely defeated already . Why not rather be wronged ? Why not rather be cheated ?
46006008	Instead , you yourselves cheat and do wrong , and you do this to your brothers and sisters .
46006009	Or do you not know that wrongdoers will not inherit the kingdom of God ? Do not be deceived : Neither the sexually immoral nor idolaters nor adulterers nor men who have sex with men
46006010	nor thieves nor the greedy nor drunkards nor slanderers nor swindlers will inherit the kingdom of God .
46006011	And that is what some of you were . But you were washed , you were sanctified , you were justified in the name of the Lord Jesus Christ and by the Spirit of our God .
46006012	" I have the right to do anything , " you say — but not everything is beneficial . " I have the right to do anything " — but I will not be mastered by anything .
46006013	You say , " Food for the stomach and the stomach for food , and God will destroy them both . " The body , however , is not meant for sexual immorality but for the Lord , and the Lord for the body .
46006014	By his power God raised the Lord from the dead , and he will raise us also .
46006015	Do you not know that your bodies are members of Christ himself ? Shall I then take the members of Christ and unite them with a prostitute ? Never !
46006016	Do you not know that he who unites himself with a prostitute is one with her in body ? For it is said , " The two will become one flesh . "
46006017	But whoever is united with the Lord is one with him in spirit .
46006018	Flee from sexual immorality . All other sins a person commits are outside the body , but whoever sins sexually , sins against their own body .
46006019	Do you not know that your bodies are temples of the Holy Spirit , who is in you , whom you have received from God ? You are not your own ;
46006020	you were bought at a price . Therefore honor God with your bodies .
46007001	Now for the matters you wrote about : " It is good for a man not to have sexual relations with a woman . "
46007002	But since sexual immorality is occurring , each man should have sexual relations with his own wife , and each woman with her own husband .
46007003	The husband should fulfill his marital duty to his wife , and likewise the wife to her husband .
46007004	The wife does not have authority over her own body but yields it to her husband . In the same way , the husband does not have authority over his own body but yields it to his wife .
46007005	Do not deprive each other except perhaps by mutual consent and for a time , so that you may devote yourselves to prayer . Then come together again so that Satan will not tempt you because of your lack of self-control .
46007006	I say this as a concession , not as a command .
46007007	I wish that all of you were as I am . But each of you has your own gift from God ; one has this gift , another has that .
46007008	Now to the unmarried and the widows I say : It is good for them to stay unmarried , as I do .
46007009	But if they cannot control themselves , they should marry , for it is better to marry than to burn with passion .
46007010	To the married I give this command ( not I , but the Lord ) : A wife must not separate from her husband .
46007011	But if she does , she must remain unmarried or else be reconciled to her husband . And a husband must not divorce his wife .
46007012	To the rest I say this ( I , not the Lord ) : If any brother has a wife who is not a believer and she is willing to live with him , he must not divorce her .
46007013	And if a woman has a husband who is not a believer and he is willing to live with her , she must not divorce him .
46007014	For the unbelieving husband has been sanctified through his wife , and the unbelieving wife has been sanctified through her believing husband . Otherwise your children would be unclean , but as it is , they are holy .
46007015	But if the unbeliever leaves , let it be so . The brother or the sister is not bound in such circumstances ; God has called us to live in peace .
46007016	How do you know , wife , whether you will save your husband ? Or , how do you know , husband , whether you will save your wife ?
46007017	Nevertheless , each person should live as a believer in whatever situation the Lord has assigned to them , just as God has called them . This is the rule I lay down in all the churches .
46007018	Was a man already circumcised when he was called ? He should not become uncircumcised . Was a man uncircumcised when he was called ? He should not be circumcised .
46007019	Circumcision is nothing and uncircumcision is nothing . Keeping God's commands is what counts .
46007020	Each person should remain in the situation they were in when God called them .
46007021	Were you a slave when you were called ? Don't let it trouble you — although if you can gain your freedom , do so .
46007022	For the one who was a slave when called to faith in the Lord is the Lord's freed person ; similarly , the one who was free when called is Christ's slave .
46007023	You were bought at a price ; do not become slaves of human beings .
46007024	Brothers and sisters , each person , as responsible to God , should remain in the situation they were in when God called them .
46007025	Now about virgins : I have no command from the Lord , but I give a judgment as one who by the Lord's mercy is trustworthy .
46007026	Because of the present crisis , I think that it is good for a man to remain as he is .
46007027	Are you pledged to a woman ? Do not seek to be released . Are you free from such a commitment ? Do not look for a wife .
46007028	But if you do marry , you have not sinned ; and if a virgin marries , she has not sinned . But those who marry will face many troubles in this life , and I want to spare you this .
46007029	What I mean , brothers and sisters , is that the time is short . From now on those who have wives should live as if they do not ;
46007030	those who mourn , as if they did not ; those who are happy , as if they were not ; those who buy something , as if it were not theirs to keep ;
46007031	those who use the things of the world , as if not engrossed in them . For this world in its present form is passing away .
46007032	I would like you to be free from concern . An unmarried man is concerned about the Lord's affairs — how he can please the Lord .
46007033	But a married man is concerned about the affairs of this world — how he can please his wife —
46007034	and his interests are divided . An unmarried woman or virgin is concerned about the Lord's affairs : Her aim is to be devoted to the Lord in both body and spirit . But a married woman is concerned about the affairs of this world — how she can please her husband .
46007035	I am saying this for your own good , not to restrict you , but that you may live in a right way in undivided devotion to the Lord .
46007036	If anyone is worried that he might not be acting honorably toward the virgin he is engaged to , and if his passions are too strong and he feels he ought to marry , he should do as he wants . He is not sinning . They should get married .
46007037	But the man who has settled the matter in his own mind , who is under no compulsion but has control over his own will , and who has made up his mind not to marry the virgin — this man also does the right thing .
46007038	So then , he who marries the virgin does right , but he who does not marry her does better .
46007039	A woman is bound to her husband as long as he lives . But if her husband dies , she is free to marry anyone she wishes , but he must belong to the Lord .
46007040	In my judgment , she is happier if she stays as she is — and I think that I too have the Spirit of God .
46008001	Now about food sacrificed to idols : We know that " We all possess knowledge . " But knowledge puffs up while love builds up .
46008002	Those who think they know something do not yet know as they ought to know .
46008003	But whoever loves God is known by God .
46008004	So then , about eating food sacrificed to idols : We know that " An idol is nothing at all in the world " and that " There is no God but one . "
46008005	For even if there are so-called gods , whether in heaven or on earth ( as indeed there are many " gods " and many " lords " ) ,
46008006	yet for us there is but one God , the Father , from whom all things came and for whom we live ; and there is but one Lord , Jesus Christ , through whom all things came and through whom we live .
46008007	But not everyone possesses this knowledge . Some people are still so accustomed to idols that when they eat sacrificial food they think of it as having been sacrificed to a god , and since their conscience is weak , it is defiled .
46008008	But food does not bring us near to God ; we are no worse if we do not eat , and no better if we do .
46008009	Be careful , however , that the exercise of your rights does not become a stumbling block to the weak .
46008010	For if someone with a weak conscience sees you , with all your knowledge , eating in an idol's temple , won't that person be emboldened to eat what is sacrificed to idols ?
46008011	So this weak brother or sister , for whom Christ died , is destroyed by your knowledge .
46008012	When you sin against them in this way and wound their weak conscience , you sin against Christ .
46008013	Therefore , if what I eat causes my brother or sister to fall into sin , I will never eat meat again , so that I will not cause them to fall .
46009001	Am I not free ? Am I not an apostle ? Have I not seen Jesus our Lord ? Are you not the result of my work in the Lord ?
46009002	Even though I may not be an apostle to others , surely I am to you ! For you are the seal of my apostleship in the Lord .
46009003	This is my defense to those who sit in judgment on me .
46009004	Don't we have the right to food and drink ?
46009005	Don't we have the right to take a believing wife along with us , as do the other apostles and the Lord's brothers and Cephas ?
46009006	Or is it only I and Barnabas who lack the right to not work for a living ?
46009007	Who serves as a soldier at his own expense ? Who plants a vineyard and does not eat its grapes ? Who tends a flock and does not drink the milk ?
46009008	Do I say this merely on human authority ? Doesn't the Law say the same thing ?
46009009	For it is written in the Law of Moses : " Do not muzzle an ox while it is treading out the grain . " Is it about oxen that God is concerned ?
46009010	Surely he says this for us , doesn't he ? Yes , this was written for us , because whoever plows and threshes should be able to do so in the hope of sharing in the harvest .
46009011	If we have sown spiritual seed among you , is it too much if we reap a material harvest from you ?
46009012	If others have this right of support from you , shouldn't we have it all the more ? But we did not use this right . On the contrary , we put up with anything rather than hinder the gospel of Christ .
46009013	Don't you know that those who serve in the temple get their food from the temple , and that those who serve at the altar share in what is offered on the altar ?
46009014	In the same way , the Lord has commanded that those who preach the gospel should receive their living from the gospel .
46009015	But I have not used any of these rights . And I am not writing this in the hope that you will do such things for me , for I would rather die than allow anyone to deprive me of this boast .
46009016	For when I preach the gospel , I cannot boast , since I am compelled to preach . Woe to me if I do not preach the gospel !
46009017	If I preach voluntarily , I have a reward ; if not voluntarily , I am simply discharging the trust committed to me .
46009018	What then is my reward ? Just this : that in preaching the gospel I may offer it free of charge , and so not make full use of my rights as a preacher of the gospel .
46009019	Though I am free and belong to no one , I have made myself a slave to everyone , to win as many as possible .
46009020	To the Jews I became like a Jew , to win the Jews . To those under the law I became like one under the law ( though I myself am not under the law ) , so as to win those under the law .
46009021	To those not having the law I became like one not having the law ( though I am not free from God's law but am under Christ's law ) , so as to win those not having the law .
46009022	To the weak I became weak , to win the weak . I have become all things to all people so that by all possible means I might save some .
46009023	I do all this for the sake of the gospel , that I may share in its blessings .
46009024	Do you not know that in a race all the runners run , but only one gets the prize ? Run in such a way as to get the prize .
46009025	Everyone who competes in the games goes into strict training . They do it to get a crown that will not last , but we do it to get a crown that will last forever .
46009026	Therefore I do not run like someone running aimlessly ; I do not fight like a boxer beating the air .
46009027	No , I strike a blow to my body and make it my slave so that after I have preached to others , I myself will not be disqualified for the prize .
46010001	For I do not want you to be ignorant of the fact , brothers and sisters , that our ancestors were all under the cloud and that they all passed through the sea .
46010002	They were all baptized into Moses in the cloud and in the sea .
46010003	They all ate the same spiritual food
46010004	and drank the same spiritual drink ; for they drank from the spiritual rock that accompanied them , and that rock was Christ .
46010005	Nevertheless , God was not pleased with most of them ; their bodies were scattered in the wilderness .
46010006	Now these things occurred as examples to keep us from setting our hearts on evil things as they did .
46010007	Do not be idolaters , as some of them were ; as it is written : " The people sat down to eat and drink and got up to indulge in revelry . "
46010008	We should not commit sexual immorality , as some of them did — and in one day twenty-three thousand of them died .
46010009	We should not test Christ , as some of them did — and were killed by snakes .
46010010	And do not grumble , as some of them did — and were killed by the destroying angel .
46010011	These things happened to them as examples and were written down as warnings for us , on whom the culmination of the ages has come .
46010012	So , if you think you are standing firm , be careful that you don't fall !
46010013	No temptation has overtaken you except what is common to mankind . And God is faithful ; he will not let you be tempted beyond what you can bear . But when you are tempted , he will also provide a way out so that you can endure it .
46010014	Therefore , my dear friends , flee from idolatry .
46010015	I speak to sensible people ; judge for yourselves what I say .
46010016	Is not the cup of thanksgiving for which we give thanks a participation in the blood of Christ ? And is not the bread that we break a participation in the body of Christ ?
46010017	Because there is one loaf , we , who are many , are one body , for we all share the one loaf .
46010018	Consider the people of Israel : Do not those who eat the sacrifices participate in the altar ?
46010019	Do I mean then that food sacrificed to an idol is anything , or that an idol is anything ?
46010020	No , but the sacrifices of pagans are offered to demons , not to God , and I do not want you to be participants with demons .
46010021	You cannot drink the cup of the Lord and the cup of demons too ; you cannot have a part in both the Lord's table and the table of demons .
46010022	Are we trying to arouse the Lord's jealousy ? Are we stronger than he ?
46010023	" I have the right to do anything , " you say — but not everything is beneficial . " I have the right to do anything " — but not everything is constructive .
46010024	No one should seek their own good , but the good of others .
46010025	Eat anything sold in the meat market without raising questions of conscience ,
46010026	for , " The earth is the Lord's , and everything in it . "
46010027	If an unbeliever invites you to a meal and you want to go , eat whatever is put before you without raising questions of conscience .
46010028	But if someone says to you , " This has been offered in sacrifice , " then do not eat it , both for the sake of the one who told you and for the sake of conscience .
46010029	I am referring to the other person's conscience , not yours . For why is my freedom being judged by another's conscience ?
46010030	If I take part in the meal with thankfulness , why am I denounced because of something I thank God for ?
46010031	So whether you eat or drink or whatever you do , do it all for the glory of God .
46010032	Do not cause anyone to stumble , whether Jews , Greeks or the church of God —
46010033	even as I try to please everyone in every way . For I am not seeking my own good but the good of many , so that they may be saved .
46011001	Follow my example , as I follow the example of Christ .
46011002	I praise you for remembering me in everything and for holding to the traditions just as I passed them on to you .
46011003	But I want you to realize that the head of every man is Christ , and the head of the woman is man , and the head of Christ is God .
46011004	Every man who prays or prophesies with his head covered dishonors his head .
46011005	But every woman who prays or prophesies with her head uncovered dishonors her head — it is the same as having her head shaved .
46011006	For if a woman does not cover her head , she might as well have her hair cut off ; but if it is a disgrace for a woman to have her hair cut off or her head shaved , then she should cover her head .
46011007	A man ought not to cover his head , since he is the image and glory of God ; but woman is the glory of man .
46011008	For man did not come from woman , but woman from man ;
46011009	neither was man created for woman , but woman for man .
46011010	It is for this reason that a woman ought to have authority over her own head , because of the angels .
46011011	Nevertheless , in the Lord woman is not independent of man , nor is man independent of woman .
46011012	For as woman came from man , so also man is born of woman . But everything comes from God .
46011013	Judge for yourselves : Is it proper for a woman to pray to God with her head uncovered ?
46011014	Does not the very nature of things teach you that if a man has long hair , it is a disgrace to him ,
46011015	but that if a woman has long hair , it is her glory ? For long hair is given to her as a covering .
46011016	If anyone wants to be contentious about this , we have no other practice — nor do the churches of God .
46011017	In the following directives I have no praise for you , for your meetings do more harm than good .
46011018	In the first place , I hear that when you come together as a church , there are divisions among you , and to some extent I believe it .
46011019	No doubt there have to be differences among you to show which of you have God's approval .
46011020	So then , when you come together , it is not the Lord's Supper you eat ,
46011021	for when you are eating , some of you go ahead with your own private suppers . As a result , one person remains hungry and another gets drunk .
46011022	Don't you have homes to eat and drink in ? Or do you despise the church of God by humiliating those who have nothing ? What shall I say to you ? Shall I praise you ? Certainly not in this matter !
46011023	For I received from the Lord what I also passed on to you : The Lord Jesus , on the night he was betrayed , took bread ,
46011024	and when he had given thanks , he broke it and said , " This is my body , which is for you ; do this in remembrance of me . "
46011025	In the same way , after supper he took the cup , saying , " This cup is the new covenant in my blood ; do this , whenever you drink it , in remembrance of me . "
46011026	For whenever you eat this bread and drink this cup , you proclaim the Lord's death until he comes .
46011027	So then , whoever eats the bread or drinks the cup of the Lord in an unworthy manner will be guilty of sinning against the body and blood of the Lord .
46011028	Everyone ought to examine themselves before they eat of the bread and drink from the cup .
46011029	For those who eat and drink without discerning the body of Christ eat and drink judgment on themselves .
46011030	That is why many among you are weak and sick , and a number of you have fallen asleep .
46011031	But if we were more discerning with regard to ourselves , we would not come under such judgment .
46011032	Nevertheless , when we are judged in this way by the Lord , we are being disciplined so that we will not be finally condemned with the world .
46011033	So then , my brothers and sisters , when you gather to eat , you should all eat together .
46011034	Anyone who is hungry should eat something at home , so that when you meet together it may not result in judgment . And when I come I will give further directions .
46012001	Now about the gifts of the Spirit , brothers and sisters , I do not want you to be uninformed .
46012002	You know that when you were pagans , somehow or other you were influenced and led astray to mute idols .
46012003	Therefore I want you to know that no one who is speaking by the Spirit of God says , " Jesus be cursed , " and no one can say , " Jesus is Lord , " except by the Holy Spirit .
46012004	There are different kinds of gifts , but the same Spirit distributes them .
46012005	There are different kinds of service , but the same Lord .
46012006	There are different kinds of working , but in all of them and in everyone it is the same God at work .
46012007	Now to each one the manifestation of the Spirit is given for the common good .
46012008	To one there is given through the Spirit a message of wisdom , to another a message of knowledge by means of the same Spirit ,
46012009	to another faith by the same Spirit , to another gifts of healing by that one Spirit ,
46012010	to another miraculous powers , to another prophecy , to another distinguishing between spirits , to another speaking in different kinds of tongues , and to still another the interpretation of tongues .
46012011	All these are the work of one and the same Spirit , and he distributes them to each one , just as he determines .
46012012	Just as a body , though one , has many parts , but all its many parts form one body , so it is with Christ .
46012013	For we were all baptized by one Spirit so as to form one body — whether Jews or Gentiles , slave or free — and we were all given the one Spirit to drink .
46012014	Even so the body is not made up of one part but of many .
46012015	Now if the foot should say , " Because I am not a hand , I do not belong to the body , " it would not for that reason stop being part of the body .
46012016	And if the ear should say , " Because I am not an eye , I do not belong to the body , " it would not for that reason stop being part of the body .
46012017	If the whole body were an eye , where would the sense of hearing be ? If the whole body were an ear , where would the sense of smell be ?
46012018	But in fact God has placed the parts in the body , every one of them , just as he wanted them to be .
46012019	If they were all one part , where would the body be ?
46012020	As it is , there are many parts , but one body .
46012021	The eye cannot say to the hand , " I don't need you ! " And the head cannot say to the feet , " I don't need you ! "
46012022	On the contrary , those parts of the body that seem to be weaker are indispensable ,
46012023	and the parts that we think are less honorable we treat with special honor . And the parts that are unpresentable are treated with special modesty ,
46012024	while our presentable parts need no special treatment . But God has put the body together , giving greater honor to the parts that lacked it ,
46012025	so that there should be no division in the body , but that its parts should have equal concern for each other .
46012026	If one part suffers , every part suffers with it ; if one part is honored , every part rejoices with it .
46012027	Now you are the body of Christ , and each one of you is a part of it .
46012028	And God has placed in the church first of all apostles , second prophets , third teachers , then miracles , then gifts of healing , of helping , of guidance , and of different kinds of tongues .
46012029	Are all apostles ? Are all prophets ? Are all teachers ? Do all work miracles ?
46012030	Do all have gifts of healing ? Do all speak in tongues ? Do all interpret ?
46012031	Now eagerly desire the greater gifts . And yet I will show you the most excellent way .
46013001	If I speak in the tongues of men or of angels , but do not have love , I am only a resounding gong or a clanging cymbal .
46013002	If I have the gift of prophecy and can fathom all mysteries and all knowledge , and if I have a faith that can move mountains , but do not have love , I am nothing .
46013003	If I give all I possess to the poor and give over my body to hardship that I may boast , but do not have love , I gain nothing .
46013004	Love is patient , love is kind . It does not envy , it does not boast , it is not proud .
46013005	It does not dishonor others , it is not self-seeking , it is not easily angered , it keeps no record of wrongs .
46013006	Love does not delight in evil but rejoices with the truth .
46013007	It always protects , always trusts , always hopes , always perseveres .
46013008	Love never fails . But where there are prophecies , they will cease ; where there are tongues , they will be stilled ; where there is knowledge , it will pass away .
46013009	For we know in part and we prophesy in part ,
46013010	but when completeness comes , what is in part disappears .
46013011	When I was a child , I talked like a child , I thought like a child , I reasoned like a child . When I became a man , I put the ways of childhood behind me .
46013012	For now we see only a reflection as in a mirror ; then we shall see face to face . Now I know in part ; then I shall know fully , even as I am fully known .
46013013	And now these three remain : faith , hope and love . But the greatest of these is love .
46014001	Follow the way of love and eagerly desire gifts of the Spirit , especially prophecy .
46014002	For anyone who speaks in a tongue does not speak to people but to God . Indeed , no one understands them ; they utter mysteries by the Spirit .
46014003	But the one who prophesies speaks to people for their strengthening , encouraging and comfort .
46014004	Anyone who speaks in a tongue edifies themselves , but the one who prophesies edifies the church .
46014005	I would like every one of you to speak in tongues , but I would rather have you prophesy . The one who prophesies is greater than the one who speaks in tongues , unless someone interprets , so that the church may be edified .
46014006	Now , brothers and sisters , if I come to you and speak in tongues , what good will I be to you , unless I bring you some revelation or knowledge or prophecy or word of instruction ?
46014007	Even in the case of lifeless things that make sounds , such as the pipe or harp , how will anyone know what tune is being played unless there is a distinction in the notes ?
46014008	Again , if the trumpet does not sound a clear call , who will get ready for battle ?
46014009	So it is with you . Unless you speak intelligible words with your tongue , how will anyone know what you are saying ? You will just be speaking into the air .
46014010	Undoubtedly there are all sorts of languages in the world , yet none of them is without meaning .
46014011	If then I do not grasp the meaning of what someone is saying , I am a foreigner to the speaker , and the speaker is a foreigner to me .
46014012	So it is with you . Since you are eager for gifts of the Spirit , try to excel in those that build up the church .
46014013	For this reason the one who speaks in a tongue should pray that they may interpret what they say .
46014014	For if I pray in a tongue , my spirit prays , but my mind is unfruitful .
46014015	So what shall I do ? I will pray with my spirit , but I will also pray with my understanding ; I will sing with my spirit , but I will also sing with my understanding .
46014016	Otherwise when you are praising God in the Spirit , how can someone else , who is now put in the position of an inquirer , say " Amen " to your thanksgiving , since they do not know what you are saying ?
46014017	You are giving thanks well enough , but no one else is edified .
46014018	I thank God that I speak in tongues more than all of you .
46014019	But in the church I would rather speak five intelligible words to instruct others than ten thousand words in a tongue .
46014020	Brothers and sisters , stop thinking like children . In regard to evil be infants , but in your thinking be adults .
46014021	In the Law it is written :
46014022	Tongues , then , are a sign , not for believers but for unbelievers ; prophecy , however , is not for unbelievers but for believers .
46014023	So if the whole church comes together and everyone speaks in tongues , and inquirers or unbelievers come in , will they not say that you are out of your mind ?
46014024	But if an unbeliever or an inquirer comes in while everyone is prophesying , they are convicted of sin and are brought under judgment by all ,
46014025	as the secrets of their hearts are laid bare . So they will fall down and worship God , exclaiming , " God is really among you ! "
46014026	What then shall we say , brothers and sisters ? When you come together , each of you has a hymn , or a word of instruction , a revelation , a tongue or an interpretation . Everything must be done so that the church may be built up .
46014027	If anyone speaks in a tongue , two — or at the most three — should speak , one at a time , and someone must interpret .
46014028	If there is no interpreter , the speaker should keep quiet in the church and speak to himself and to God .
46014029	Two or three prophets should speak , and the others should weigh carefully what is said .
46014030	And if a revelation comes to someone who is sitting down , the first speaker should stop .
46014031	For you can all prophesy in turn so that everyone may be instructed and encouraged .
46014032	The spirits of prophets are subject to the control of prophets .
46014033	For God is not a God of disorder but of peace — as in all the congregations of the Lord's people .
46014034	Women should remain silent in the churches . They are not allowed to speak , but must be in submission , as the law says .
46014035	If they want to inquire about something , they should ask their own husbands at home ; for it is disgraceful for a woman to speak in the church .
46014036	Or did the word of God originate with you ? Or are you the only people it has reached ?
46014037	If anyone thinks they are a prophet or otherwise gifted by the Spirit , let them acknowledge that what I am writing to you is the Lord's command .
46014038	But if anyone ignores this , they will themselves be ignored .
46014039	Therefore , my brothers and sisters , be eager to prophesy , and do not forbid speaking in tongues .
46014040	But everything should be done in a fitting and orderly way .
46015001	Now , brothers and sisters , I want to remind you of the gospel I preached to you , which you received and on which you have taken your stand .
46015002	By this gospel you are saved , if you hold firmly to the word I preached to you . Otherwise , you have believed in vain .
46015003	For what I received I passed on to you as of first importance : that Christ died for our sins according to the Scriptures ,
46015004	that he was buried , that he was raised on the third day according to the Scriptures ,
46015005	and that he appeared to Cephas , and then to the Twelve .
46015006	After that , he appeared to more than five hundred of the brothers and sisters at the same time , most of whom are still living , though some have fallen asleep .
46015007	Then he appeared to James , then to all the apostles ,
46015008	and last of all he appeared to me also , as to one abnormally born .
46015009	For I am the least of the apostles and do not even deserve to be called an apostle , because I persecuted the church of God .
46015010	But by the grace of God I am what I am , and his grace to me was not without effect . No , I worked harder than all of them — yet not I , but the grace of God that was with me .
