58003012	See to it , brothers and sisters , that none of you has a sinful , unbelieving heart that turns away from the living God .
58003013	But encourage one another daily , as long as it is called " Today , " so that none of you may be hardened by sin's deceitfulness .
58003014	We have come to share in Christ , if indeed we hold our original conviction firmly to the very end .
58003015	As has just been said :
58003017	And with whom was he angry for forty years ? Was it not with those who sinned , whose bodies perished in the wilderness ?
58003018	And to whom did God swear that they would never enter his rest if not to those who disobeyed ?
58003019	So we see that they were not able to enter , because of their unbelief .
58004001	Therefore , since the promise of entering his rest still stands , let us be careful that none of you be found to have fallen short of it .
58004002	For we also have had the good news proclaimed to us , just as they did ; but the message they heard was of no value to them , because they did not share the faith of those who obeyed .
58004003	Now we who have believed enter that rest , just as God has said ,
58004004	For somewhere he has spoken about the seventh day in these words : " On the seventh day God rested from all his works . "
58004005	And again in the passage above he says , " They shall never enter my rest . "
58004006	Therefore since it still remains for some to enter that rest , and since those who formerly had the good news proclaimed to them did not go in because of their disobedience ,
58004007	God again set a certain day , calling it " Today . " This he did when a long time later he spoke through David , as in the passage already quoted :
58004009	There remains , then , a Sabbath-rest for the people of God ;
58004010	for anyone who enters God's rest also rests from their works , just as God did from his .
58004011	Let us , therefore , make every effort to enter that rest , so that no one will perish by following their example of disobedience .
58004012	For the word of God is alive and active . Sharper than any double-edged sword , it penetrates even to dividing soul and spirit , joints and marrow ; it judges the thoughts and attitudes of the heart .
58004013	Nothing in all creation is hidden from God's sight . Everything is uncovered and laid bare before the eyes of him to whom we must give account .
58004014	Therefore , since we have a great high priest who has ascended into heaven , Jesus the Son of God , let us hold firmly to the faith we profess .
58004015	For we do not have a high priest who is unable to empathize with our weaknesses , but we have one who has been tempted in every way , just as we are — yet he did not sin .
58004016	Let us then approach God's throne of grace with confidence , so that we may receive mercy and find grace to help us in our time of need .
58005001	Every high priest is selected from among the people and is appointed to represent the people in matters related to God , to offer gifts and sacrifices for sins .
58005002	He is able to deal gently with those who are ignorant and are going astray , since he himself is subject to weakness .
58005003	This is why he has to offer sacrifices for his own sins , as well as for the sins of the people .
58005004	And no one takes this honor on himself , but he receives it when called by God , just as Aaron was .
58005005	In the same way , Christ did not take on himself the glory of becoming a high priest . But God said to him ,
58005006	And he says in another place ,
58005007	During the days of Jesus' life on earth , he offered up prayers and petitions with fervent cries and tears to the one who could save him from death , and he was heard because of his reverent submission .
58005008	Son though he was , he learned obedience from what he suffered
58005009	and , once made perfect , he became the source of eternal salvation for all who obey him
58005010	and was designated by God to be high priest in the order of Melchizedek .
58005011	We have much to say about this , but it is hard to make it clear to you because you no longer try to understand .
58005012	In fact , though by this time you ought to be teachers , you need someone to teach you the elementary truths of God's word all over again . You need milk , not solid food !
58005013	Anyone who lives on milk , being still an infant , is not acquainted with the teaching about righteousness .
58005014	But solid food is for the mature , who by constant use have trained themselves to distinguish good from evil .
58006001	Therefore let us move beyond the elementary teachings about Christ and be taken forward to maturity , not laying again the foundation of repentance from acts that lead to death , and of faith in God ,
58006002	instruction about cleansing rites , the laying on of hands , the resurrection of the dead , and eternal judgment .
58006003	And God permitting , we will do so .
58006004	It is impossible for those who have once been enlightened , who have tasted the heavenly gift , who have shared in the Holy Spirit ,
58006005	who have tasted the goodness of the word of God and the powers of the coming age
58006006	and who have fallen away , to be brought back to repentance . To their loss they are crucifying the Son of God all over again and subjecting him to public disgrace .
58006007	Land that drinks in the rain often falling on it and that produces a crop useful to those for whom it is farmed receives the blessing of God .
58006008	But land that produces thorns and thistles is worthless and is in danger of being cursed . In the end it will be burned .
58006009	Even though we speak like this , dear friends , we are convinced of better things in your case — the things that have to do with salvation .
58006010	God is not unjust ; he will not forget your work and the love you have shown him as you have helped his people and continue to help them .
58006011	We want each of you to show this same diligence to the very end , so that what you hope for may be fully realized .
58006012	We do not want you to become lazy , but to imitate those who through faith and patience inherit what has been promised .
58006013	When God made his promise to Abraham , since there was no one greater for him to swear by , he swore by himself ,
58006014	saying , " I will surely bless you and give you many descendants . "
58006015	And so after waiting patiently , Abraham received what was promised .
58006016	People swear by someone greater than themselves , and the oath confirms what is said and puts an end to all argument .
58006017	Because God wanted to make the unchanging nature of his purpose very clear to the heirs of what was promised , he confirmed it with an oath .
58006018	God did this so that , by two unchangeable things in which it is impossible for God to lie , we who have fled to take hold of the hope set before us may be greatly encouraged .
58006019	We have this hope as an anchor for the soul , firm and secure . It enters the inner sanctuary behind the curtain ,
58006020	where our forerunner , Jesus , has entered on our behalf . He has become a high priest forever , in the order of Melchizedek .
58007001	This Melchizedek was king of Salem and priest of God Most High . He met Abraham returning from the defeat of the kings and blessed him ,
58007002	and Abraham gave him a tenth of everything . First , the name Melchizedek means " king of righteousness " ; then also , " king of Salem " means " king of peace . "
58007003	Without father or mother , without genealogy , without beginning of days or end of life , resembling the Son of God , he remains a priest forever .
58007004	Just think how great he was : Even the patriarch Abraham gave him a tenth of the plunder !
58007005	Now the law requires the descendants of Levi who become priests to collect a tenth from the people — that is , from their fellow Israelites — even though they also are descended from Abraham .
58007006	This man , however , did not trace his descent from Levi , yet he collected a tenth from Abraham and blessed him who had the promises .
58007007	And without doubt the lesser is blessed by the greater .
58007008	In the one case , the tenth is collected by people who die ; but in the other case , by him who is declared to be living .
58007009	One might even say that Levi , who collects the tenth , paid the tenth through Abraham ,
58007010	because when Melchizedek met Abraham , Levi was still in the body of his ancestor .
58007011	If perfection could have been attained through the Levitical priesthood — and indeed the law given to the people established that priesthood — why was there still need for another priest to come , one in the order of Melchizedek , not in the order of Aaron ?
58007012	For when the priesthood is changed , the law must be changed also .
58007013	He of whom these things are said belonged to a different tribe , and no one from that tribe has ever served at the altar .
58007014	For it is clear that our Lord descended from Judah , and in regard to that tribe Moses said nothing about priests .
58007015	And what we have said is even more clear if another priest like Melchizedek appears ,
58007016	one who has become a priest not on the basis of a regulation as to his ancestry but on the basis of the power of an indestructible life .
58007017	For it is declared :
58007019	( for the law made nothing perfect ) , and a better hope is introduced , by which we draw near to God .
58007020	And it was not without an oath ! Others became priests without any oath ,
58007021	but he became a priest with an oath when God said to him :
58007023	Now there have been many of those priests , since death prevented them from continuing in office ;
58007024	but because Jesus lives forever , he has a permanent priesthood .
58007025	Therefore he is able to save completely those who come to God through him , because he always lives to intercede for them .
58007026	Such a high priest truly meets our need — one who is holy , blameless , pure , set apart from sinners , exalted above the heavens .
58007027	Unlike the other high priests , he does not need to offer sacrifices day after day , first for his own sins , and then for the sins of the people . He sacrificed for their sins once for all when he offered himself .
58007028	For the law appoints as high priests men in all their weakness ; but the oath , which came after the law , appointed the Son , who has been made perfect forever .
58008001	Now the main point of what we are saying is this : We do have such a high priest , who sat down at the right hand of the throne of the Majesty in heaven ,
58008002	and who serves in the sanctuary , the true tabernacle set up by the Lord , not by a mere human being .
58008003	Every high priest is appointed to offer both gifts and sacrifices , and so it was necessary for this one also to have something to offer .
58008004	If he were on earth , he would not be a priest , for there are already priests who offer the gifts prescribed by the law .
58008005	They serve at a sanctuary that is a copy and shadow of what is in heaven . This is why Moses was warned when he was about to build the tabernacle : " See to it that you make everything according to the pattern shown you on the mountain . "
58008006	But in fact the ministry Jesus has received is as superior to theirs as the covenant of which he is mediator is superior to the old one , since the new covenant is established on better promises .
58008007	For if there had been nothing wrong with that first covenant , no place would have been sought for another .
58008008	But God found fault with the people and said :
58008010	This is the covenant I will establish with the people of Israel
58008011	No longer will they teach their neighbor ,
58008012	For I will forgive their wickedness
58008013	By calling this covenant " new , " he has made the first one obsolete ; and what is obsolete and outdated will soon disappear .
58009001	Now the first covenant had regulations for worship and also an earthly sanctuary .
58009002	A tabernacle was set up . In its first room were the lampstand and the table with its consecrated bread ; this was called the Holy Place .
58009003	Behind the second curtain was a room called the Most Holy Place ,
58009004	which had the golden altar of incense and the gold-covered ark of the covenant . This ark contained the gold jar of manna , Aaron's staff that had budded , and the stone tablets of the covenant .
58009005	Above the ark were the cherubim of the Glory , overshadowing the atonement cover . But we cannot discuss these things in detail now .
58009006	When everything had been arranged like this , the priests entered regularly into the outer room to carry on their ministry .
58009007	But only the high priest entered the inner room , and that only once a year , and never without blood , which he offered for himself and for the sins the people had committed in ignorance .
58009008	The Holy Spirit was showing by this that the way into the Most Holy Place had not yet been disclosed as long as the first tabernacle was still functioning .
58009009	This is an illustration for the present time , indicating that the gifts and sacrifices being offered were not able to clear the conscience of the worshiper .
58009010	They are only a matter of food and drink and various ceremonial washings — external regulations applying until the time of the new order .
58009011	But when Christ came as high priest of the good things that are now already here , he went through the greater and more perfect tabernacle that is not made with human hands , that is to say , is not a part of this creation .
58009012	He did not enter by means of the blood of goats and calves ; but he entered the Most Holy Place once for all by his own blood , thus obtaining eternal redemption .
58009013	The blood of goats and bulls and the ashes of a heifer sprinkled on those who are ceremonially unclean sanctify them so that they are outwardly clean .
58009014	How much more , then , will the blood of Christ , who through the eternal Spirit offered himself unblemished to God , cleanse our consciences from acts that lead to death , so that we may serve the living God !
58009015	For this reason Christ is the mediator of a new covenant , that those who are called may receive the promised eternal inheritance — now that he has died as a ransom to set them free from the sins committed under the first covenant .
58009016	In the case of a will , it is necessary to prove the death of the one who made it ,
58009017	because a will is in force only when somebody has died ; it never takes effect while the one who made it is living .
58009018	This is why even the first covenant was not put into effect without blood .
58009019	When Moses had proclaimed every command of the law to all the people , he took the blood of calves , together with water , scarlet wool and branches of hyssop , and sprinkled the scroll and all the people .
58009020	He said , " This is the blood of the covenant , which God has commanded you to keep . "
58009021	In the same way , he sprinkled with the blood both the tabernacle and everything used in its ceremonies .
58009022	In fact , the law requires that nearly everything be cleansed with blood , and without the shedding of blood there is no forgiveness .
58009023	It was necessary , then , for the copies of the heavenly things to be purified with these sacrifices , but the heavenly things themselves with better sacrifices than these .
58009024	For Christ did not enter a sanctuary made with human hands that was only a copy of the true one ; he entered heaven itself , now to appear for us in God's presence .
58009025	Nor did he enter heaven to offer himself again and again , the way the high priest enters the Most Holy Place every year with blood that is not his own .
58009026	Otherwise Christ would have had to suffer many times since the creation of the world . But he has appeared once for all at the culmination of the ages to do away with sin by the sacrifice of himself .
58009027	Just as people are destined to die once , and after that to face judgment ,
58009028	so Christ was sacrificed once to take away the sins of many ; and he will appear a second time , not to bear sin , but to bring salvation to those who are waiting for him .
58010001	The law is only a shadow of the good things that are coming — not the realities themselves . For this reason it can never , by the same sacrifices repeated endlessly year after year , make perfect those who draw near to worship .
58010002	Otherwise , would they not have stopped being offered ? For the worshipers would have been cleansed once for all , and would no longer have felt guilty for their sins .
58010003	But those sacrifices are an annual reminder of sins .
58010004	It is impossible for the blood of bulls and goats to take away sins .
58010005	Therefore , when Christ came into the world , he said : " Sacrifice and offering you did not desire , but a body you prepared for me ;
58010006	with burnt offerings and sin offerings you were not pleased .
58010007	Then I said , ' Here I am — it is written about me in the scroll — I have come to do your will , my God . ' "
58010008	First he said , " Sacrifices and offerings , burnt offerings and sin offerings you did not desire , nor were you pleased with them " — though they were offered in accordance with the law .
58010009	Then he said , " Here I am , I have come to do your will . " He sets aside the first to establish the second .
58010010	And by that will , we have been made holy through the sacrifice of the body of Jesus Christ once for all .
58010011	Day after day every priest stands and performs his religious duties ; again and again he offers the same sacrifices , which can never take away sins .
58010012	But when this priest had offered for all time one sacrifice for sins , he sat down at the right hand of God ,
58010013	and since that time he waits for his enemies to be made his footstool .
58010014	For by one sacrifice he has made perfect forever those who are being made holy .
58010015	The Holy Spirit also testifies to us about this . First he says :
58010016	" This is the covenant I will make with them after that time , says the Lord . I will put my laws in their hearts , and I will write them on their minds . "
58010017	Then he adds : " Their sins and lawless acts I will remember no more . "
58010018	And where these have been forgiven , sacrifice for sin is no longer necessary .
58010019	Therefore , brothers and sisters , since we have confidence to enter the Most Holy Place by the blood of Jesus ,
58010020	by a new and living way opened for us through the curtain , that is , his body ,
58010021	and since we have a great priest over the house of God ,
58010022	let us draw near to God with a sincere heart and with the full assurance that faith brings , having our hearts sprinkled to cleanse us from a guilty conscience and having our bodies washed with pure water .
58010023	Let us hold unswervingly to the hope we profess , for he who promised is faithful .
58010024	And let us consider how we may spur one another on toward love and good deeds ,
58010025	not giving up meeting together , as some are in the habit of doing , but encouraging one another — and all the more as you see the Day approaching .
58010026	If we deliberately keep on sinning after we have received the knowledge of the truth , no sacrifice for sins is left ,
58010027	but only a fearful expectation of judgment and of raging fire that will consume the enemies of God .
58010028	Anyone who rejected the law of Moses died without mercy on the testimony of two or three witnesses .
58010029	How much more severely do you think someone deserves to be punished who has trampled the Son of God underfoot , who has treated as an unholy thing the blood of the covenant that sanctified them , and who has insulted the Spirit of grace ?
58010030	For we know him who said , " It is mine to avenge ; I will repay , " and again , " The Lord will judge his people . "
58010031	It is a dreadful thing to fall into the hands of the living God .
58010032	Remember those earlier days after you had received the light , when you endured in a great conflict full of suffering .
58010033	Sometimes you were publicly exposed to insult and persecution ; at other times you stood side by side with those who were so treated .
58010034	You suffered along with those in prison and joyfully accepted the confiscation of your property , because you knew that you yourselves had better and lasting possessions .
58010035	So do not throw away your confidence ; it will be richly rewarded .
58010036	You need to persevere so that when you have done the will of God , you will receive what he has promised .
58010037	For , " In just a little while , he who is coming will come and will not delay . "
58010038	And , " But my righteous one will live by faith . And I take no pleasure in the one who shrinks back . "
58010039	But we do not belong to those who shrink back and are destroyed , but to those who have faith and are saved .
58011001	Now faith is confidence in what we hope for and assurance about what we do not see .
58011002	This is what the ancients were commended for .
58011003	By faith we understand that the universe was formed at God's command , so that what is seen was not made out of what was visible .
58011004	By faith Abel brought God a better offering than Cain did . By faith he was commended as righteous , when God spoke well of his offerings . And by faith Abel still speaks , even though he is dead .
58011005	By faith Enoch was taken from this life , so that he did not experience death : " He could not be found , because God had taken him away . " For before he was taken , he was commended as one who pleased God .
58011006	And without faith it is impossible to please God , because anyone who comes to him must believe that he exists and that he rewards those who earnestly seek him .
58011007	By faith Noah , when warned about things not yet seen , in holy fear built an ark to save his family . By his faith he condemned the world and became heir of the righteousness that is in keeping with faith .
58011008	By faith Abraham , when called to go to a place he would later receive as his inheritance , obeyed and went , even though he did not know where he was going .
58011009	By faith he made his home in the promised land like a stranger in a foreign country ; he lived in tents , as did Isaac and Jacob , who were heirs with him of the same promise .
58011010	For he was looking forward to the city with foundations , whose architect and builder is God .
58011011	And by faith even Sarah , who was past childbearing age , was enabled to bear children because she considered him faithful who had made the promise .
58011012	And so from this one man , and he as good as dead , came descendants as numerous as the stars in the sky and as countless as the sand on the seashore .
58011013	All these people were still living by faith when they died . They did not receive the things promised ; they only saw them and welcomed them from a distance , admitting that they were foreigners and strangers on earth .
58011014	People who say such things show that they are looking for a country of their own .
58011015	If they had been thinking of the country they had left , they would have had opportunity to return .
58011016	Instead , they were longing for a better country — a heavenly one . Therefore God is not ashamed to be called their God , for he has prepared a city for them .
58011017	By faith Abraham , when God tested him , offered Isaac as a sacrifice . He who had embraced the promises was about to sacrifice his one and only son ,
58011018	even though God had said to him , " It is through Isaac that your offspring will be reckoned . "
58011019	Abraham reasoned that God could even raise the dead , and so in a manner of speaking he did receive Isaac back from death .
58011020	By faith Isaac blessed Jacob and Esau in regard to their future .
58011021	By faith Jacob , when he was dying , blessed each of Joseph's sons , and worshiped as he leaned on the top of his staff .
58011022	By faith Joseph , when his end was near , spoke about the exodus of the Israelites from Egypt and gave instructions concerning the burial of his bones .
58011023	By faith Moses' parents hid him for three months after he was born , because they saw he was no ordinary child , and they were not afraid of the king's edict .
58011024	By faith Moses , when he had grown up , refused to be known as the son of Pharaoh's daughter .
58011025	He chose to be mistreated along with the people of God rather than to enjoy the fleeting pleasures of sin .
58011026	He regarded disgrace for the sake of Christ as of greater value than the treasures of Egypt , because he was looking ahead to his reward .
58011027	By faith he left Egypt , not fearing the king's anger ; he persevered because he saw him who is invisible .
58011028	By faith he kept the Passover and the application of blood , so that the destroyer of the firstborn would not touch the firstborn of Israel .
58011029	By faith the people passed through the Red Sea as on dry land ; but when the Egyptians tried to do so , they were drowned .
58011030	By faith the walls of Jericho fell , after the army had marched around them for seven days .
58011031	By faith the prostitute Rahab , because she welcomed the spies , was not killed with those who were disobedient .
58011032	And what more shall I say ? I do not have time to tell about Gideon , Barak , Samson and Jephthah , about David and Samuel and the prophets ,
58011033	who through faith conquered kingdoms , administered justice , and gained what was promised ; who shut the mouths of lions ,
58011034	quenched the fury of the flames , and escaped the edge of the sword ; whose weakness was turned to strength ; and who became powerful in battle and routed foreign armies .
58011035	Women received back their dead , raised to life again . There were others who were tortured , refusing to be released so that they might gain an even better resurrection .
58011036	Some faced jeers and flogging , and even chains and imprisonment .
58011037	They were put to death by stoning ; they were sawed in two ; they were killed by the sword . They went about in sheepskins and goatskins , destitute , persecuted and mistreated —
58011038	the world was not worthy of them . They wandered in deserts and mountains , living in caves and in holes in the ground .
58011039	These were all commended for their faith , yet none of them received what had been promised ,
58011040	since God had planned something better for us so that only together with us would they be made perfect .
58012001	Therefore , since we are surrounded by such a great cloud of witnesses , let us throw off everything that hinders and the sin that so easily entangles . And let us run with perseverance the race marked out for us ,
58012002	fixing our eyes on Jesus , the pioneer and perfecter of faith . For the joy set before him he endured the cross , scorning its shame , and sat down at the right hand of the throne of God .
58012003	Consider him who endured such opposition from sinners , so that you will not grow weary and lose heart .
58012004	In your struggle against sin , you have not yet resisted to the point of shedding your blood .
58012005	And have you completely forgotten this word of encouragement that addresses you as a father addresses his son ? It says ,
58012007	Endure hardship as discipline ; God is treating you as his children . For what children are not disciplined by their father ?
58012008	If you are not disciplined — and everyone undergoes discipline — then you are not legitimate , not true sons and daughters at all .
58012009	Moreover , we have all had human fathers who disciplined us and we respected them for it . How much more should we submit to the Father of spirits and live !
58012010	They disciplined us for a little while as they thought best ; but God disciplines us for our good , in order that we may share in his holiness .
58012011	No discipline seems pleasant at the time , but painful . Later on , however , it produces a harvest of righteousness and peace for those who have been trained by it .
58012012	Therefore , strengthen your feeble arms and weak knees .
58012013	" Make level paths for your feet , " so that the lame may not be disabled , but rather healed .
58012014	Make every effort to live in peace with everyone and to be holy ; without holiness no one will see the Lord .
58012015	See to it that no one falls short of the grace of God and that no bitter root grows up to cause trouble and defile many .
58012016	See that no one is sexually immoral , or is godless like Esau , who for a single meal sold his inheritance rights as the oldest son .
58012017	Afterward , as you know , when he wanted to inherit this blessing , he was rejected . Even though he sought the blessing with tears , he could not change what he had done .
58012018	You have not come to a mountain that can be touched and that is burning with fire ; to darkness , gloom and storm ;
58012019	to a trumpet blast or to such a voice speaking words that those who heard it begged that no further word be spoken to them ,
58012020	because they could not bear what was commanded : " If even an animal touches the mountain , it must be stoned to death . "
58012021	The sight was so terrifying that Moses said , " I am trembling with fear . "
58012022	But you have come to Mount Zion , to the city of the living God , the heavenly Jerusalem . You have come to thousands upon thousands of angels in joyful assembly ,
58012023	to the church of the firstborn , whose names are written in heaven . You have come to God , the Judge of all , to the spirits of the righteous made perfect ,
58012024	to Jesus the mediator of a new covenant , and to the sprinkled blood that speaks a better word than the blood of Abel .
58012025	See to it that you do not refuse him who speaks . If they did not escape when they refused him who warned them on earth , how much less will we , if we turn away from him who warns us from heaven ?
58012026	At that time his voice shook the earth , but now he has promised , " Once more I will shake not only the earth but also the heavens . "
58012027	The words " once more " indicate the removing of what can be shaken — that is , created things — so that what cannot be shaken may remain .
58012028	Therefore , since we are receiving a kingdom that cannot be shaken , let us be thankful , and so worship God acceptably with reverence and awe ,
58012029	for our " God is a consuming fire . "
58013001	Keep on loving one another as brothers and sisters .
58013002	Do not forget to show hospitality to strangers , for by so doing some people have shown hospitality to angels without knowing it .
58013003	Continue to remember those in prison as if you were together with them in prison , and those who are mistreated as if you yourselves were suffering .
58013004	Marriage should be honored by all , and the marriage bed kept pure , for God will judge the adulterer and all the sexually immoral .
58013005	Keep your lives free from the love of money and be content with what you have , because God has said ,
58013007	Remember your leaders , who spoke the word of God to you . Consider the outcome of their way of life and imitate their faith .
58013008	Jesus Christ is the same yesterday and today and forever .
58013009	Do not be carried away by all kinds of strange teachings . It is good for our hearts to be strengthened by grace , not by eating ceremonial foods , which is of no benefit to those who do so .
58013010	We have an altar from which those who minister at the tabernacle have no right to eat .
58013011	The high priest carries the blood of animals into the Most Holy Place as a sin offering , but the bodies are burned outside the camp .
58013012	And so Jesus also suffered outside the city gate to make the people holy through his own blood .
58013013	Let us , then , go to him outside the camp , bearing the disgrace he bore .
58013014	For here we do not have an enduring city , but we are looking for the city that is to come .
58013015	Through Jesus , therefore , let us continually offer to God a sacrifice of praise — the fruit of lips that openly profess his name .
58013016	And do not forget to do good and to share with others , for with such sacrifices God is pleased .
58013017	Have confidence in your leaders and submit to their authority , because they keep watch over you as those who must give an account . Do this so that their work will be a joy , not a burden , for that would be of no benefit to you .
58013018	Pray for us . We are sure that we have a clear conscience and desire to live honorably in every way .
58013019	I particularly urge you to pray so that I may be restored to you soon .
58013020	Now may the God of peace , who through the blood of the eternal covenant brought back from the dead our Lord Jesus , that great Shepherd of the sheep ,
58013021	equip you with everything good for doing his will , and may he work in us what is pleasing to him , through Jesus Christ , to whom be glory for ever and ever . Amen .
58013022	Brothers and sisters , I urge you to bear with my word of exhortation , for in fact I have written to you quite briefly .
58013023	I want you to know that our brother Timothy has been released . If he arrives soon , I will come with him to see you .
58013024	Greet all your leaders and all the Lord's people . Those from Italy send you their greetings .
58013025	Grace be with you all .
59001001	James , a servant of God and of the Lord Jesus Christ , To the twelve tribes scattered among the nations : Greetings .
59001002	Consider it pure joy , my brothers and sisters , whenever you face trials of many kinds ,
59001003	because you know that the testing of your faith produces perseverance .
59001004	Let perseverance finish its work so that you may be mature and complete , not lacking anything .
59001005	If any of you lacks wisdom , you should ask God , who gives generously to all without finding fault , and it will be given to you .
59001006	But when you ask , you must believe and not doubt , because the one who doubts is like a wave of the sea , blown and tossed by the wind .
59001007	That person should not expect to receive anything from the Lord .
59001008	Such a person is double-minded and unstable in all they do .
59001009	Believers in humble circumstances ought to take pride in their high position .
59001010	But the rich should take pride in their humiliation — since they will pass away like a wild flower .
59001011	For the sun rises with scorching heat and withers the plant ; its blossom falls and its beauty is destroyed . In the same way , the rich will fade away even while they go about their business .
59001012	Blessed is the one who perseveres under trial because , having stood the test , that person will receive the crown of life that the Lord has promised to those who love him .
59001013	When tempted , no one should say , " God is tempting me . " For God cannot be tempted by evil , nor does he tempt anyone ;
59001014	but each person is tempted when they are dragged away by their own evil desire and enticed .
59001015	Then , after desire has conceived , it gives birth to sin ; and sin , when it is full-grown , gives birth to death .
59001016	Don't be deceived , my dear brothers and sisters .
59001017	Every good and perfect gift is from above , coming down from the Father of the heavenly lights , who does not change like shifting shadows .
59001018	He chose to give us birth through the word of truth , that we might be a kind of firstfruits of all he created .
59001019	My dear brothers and sisters , take note of this : Everyone should be quick to listen , slow to speak and slow to become angry ,
59001020	because human anger does not produce the righteousness that God desires .
59001021	Therefore , get rid of all moral filth and the evil that is so prevalent and humbly accept the word planted in you , which can save you .
59001022	Do not merely listen to the word , and so deceive yourselves . Do what it says .
59001023	Anyone who listens to the word but does not do what it says is like someone who looks at his face in a mirror
59001024	and , after looking at himself , goes away and immediately forgets what he looks like .
59001025	But whoever looks intently into the perfect law that gives freedom , and continues in it — not forgetting what they have heard , but doing it — they will be blessed in what they do .
59001026	Those who consider themselves religious and yet do not keep a tight rein on their tongues deceive themselves , and their religion is worthless .
59001027	Religion that God our Father accepts as pure and faultless is this : to look after orphans and widows in their distress and to keep oneself from being polluted by the world .
59002001	My brothers and sisters , believers in our glorious Lord Jesus Christ must not show favoritism .
59002002	Suppose a man comes into your meeting wearing a gold ring and fine clothes , and a poor man in filthy old clothes also comes in .
59002003	If you show special attention to the man wearing fine clothes and say , " Here's a good seat for you , " but say to the poor man , " You stand there " or " Sit on the floor by my feet , "
59002004	have you not discriminated among yourselves and become judges with evil thoughts ?
59002005	Listen , my dear brothers and sisters : Has not God chosen those who are poor in the eyes of the world to be rich in faith and to inherit the kingdom he promised those who love him ?
59002006	But you have dishonored the poor . Is it not the rich who are exploiting you ? Are they not the ones who are dragging you into court ?
59002007	Are they not the ones who are blaspheming the noble name of him to whom you belong ?
59002008	If you really keep the royal law found in Scripture , " Love your neighbor as yourself , " you are doing right .
59002009	But if you show favoritism , you sin and are convicted by the law as lawbreakers .
59002010	For whoever keeps the whole law and yet stumbles at just one point is guilty of breaking all of it .
59002011	For he who said , " You shall not commit adultery , " also said , " You shall not murder . " If you do not commit adultery but do commit murder , you have become a lawbreaker .
59002012	Speak and act as those who are going to be judged by the law that gives freedom ,
59002013	because judgment without mercy will be shown to anyone who has not been merciful . Mercy triumphs over judgment .
59002014	What good is it , my brothers and sisters , if someone claims to have faith but has no deeds ? Can such faith save them ?
59002015	Suppose a brother or a sister is without clothes and daily food .
59002016	If one of you says to them , " Go in peace ; keep warm and well fed , " but does nothing about their physical needs , what good is it ?
59002017	In the same way , faith by itself , if it is not accompanied by action , is dead .
59002018	But someone will say , " You have faith ; I have deeds . " Show me your faith without deeds , and I will show you my faith by my deeds .
59002019	You believe that there is one God . Good ! Even the demons believe that — and shudder .
59002020	You foolish person , do you want evidence that faith without deeds is useless ?
59002021	Was not our father Abraham considered righteous for what he did when he offered his son Isaac on the altar ?
59002022	You see that his faith and his actions were working together , and his faith was made complete by what he did .
59002023	And the scripture was fulfilled that says , " Abraham believed God , and it was credited to him as righteousness , " and he was called God's friend .
59002024	You see that a person is considered righteous by what they do and not by faith alone .
59002025	In the same way , was not even Rahab the prostitute considered righteous for what she did when she gave lodging to the spies and sent them off in a different direction ?
59002026	As the body without the spirit is dead , so faith without deeds is dead .
59003001	Not many of you should become teachers , my fellow believers , because you know that we who teach will be judged more strictly .
59003002	We all stumble in many ways . Anyone who is never at fault in what they say is perfect , able to keep their whole body in check .
59003003	When we put bits into the mouths of horses to make them obey us , we can turn the whole animal .
59003004	Or take ships as an example . Although they are so large and are driven by strong winds , they are steered by a very small rudder wherever the pilot wants to go .
59003005	Likewise , the tongue is a small part of the body , but it makes great boasts . Consider what a great forest is set on fire by a small spark .
59003006	The tongue also is a fire , a world of evil among the parts of the body . It corrupts the whole body , sets the whole course of one's life on fire , and is itself set on fire by hell .
59003007	All kinds of animals , birds , reptiles and sea creatures are being tamed and have been tamed by mankind ,
59003008	but no human being can tame the tongue . It is a restless evil , full of deadly poison .
59003009	With the tongue we praise our Lord and Father , and with it we curse human beings , who have been made in God's likeness .
59003010	Out of the same mouth come praise and cursing . My brothers and sisters , this should not be .
59003011	Can both fresh water and salt water flow from the same spring ?
59003012	My brothers and sisters , can a fig tree bear olives , or a grapevine bear figs ? Neither can a salt spring produce fresh water .
59003013	Who is wise and understanding among you ? Let them show it by their good life , by deeds done in the humility that comes from wisdom .
59003014	But if you harbor bitter envy and selfish ambition in your hearts , do not boast about it or deny the truth .
59003015	Such " wisdom " does not come down from heaven but is earthly , unspiritual , demonic .
59003016	For where you have envy and selfish ambition , there you find disorder and every evil practice .
59003017	But the wisdom that comes from heaven is first of all pure ; then peace-loving , considerate , submissive , full of mercy and good fruit , impartial and sincere .
59003018	Peacemakers who sow in peace reap a harvest of righteousness .
59004001	What causes fights and quarrels among you ? Don't they come from your desires that battle within you ?
59004002	You desire but do not have , so you kill . You covet but you cannot get what you want , so you quarrel and fight . You do not have because you do not ask God .
59004003	When you ask , you do not receive , because you ask with wrong motives , that you may spend what you get on your pleasures .
59004004	You adulterous people , don't you know that friendship with the world means enmity against God ? Therefore , anyone who chooses to be a friend of the world becomes an enemy of God .
59004005	Or do you think Scripture says without reason that he jealously longs for the spirit he has caused to dwell in us ?
59004006	But he gives us more grace . That is why Scripture says :
59004008	Come near to God and he will come near to you . Wash your hands , you sinners , and purify your hearts , you double-minded .
59004009	Grieve , mourn and wail . Change your laughter to mourning and your joy to gloom .
59004010	Humble yourselves before the Lord , and he will lift you up .
59004011	Brothers and sisters , do not slander one another . Anyone who speaks against a brother or sister or judges them speaks against the law and judges it . When you judge the law , you are not keeping it , but sitting in judgment on it .
59004012	There is only one Lawgiver and Judge , the one who is able to save and destroy . But you — who are you to judge your neighbor ?
59004013	Now listen , you who say , " Today or tomorrow we will go to this or that city , spend a year there , carry on business and make money . "
59004014	Why , you do not even know what will happen tomorrow . What is your life ? You are a mist that appears for a little while and then vanishes .
59004015	Instead , you ought to say , " If it is the Lord's will , we will live and do this or that . "
59004016	As it is , you boast in your arrogant schemes . All such boasting is evil .
59004017	If anyone , then , knows the good they ought to do and doesn't do it , it is sin for them .
59005001	Now listen , you rich people , weep and wail because of the misery that is coming on you .
59005002	Your wealth has rotted , and moths have eaten your clothes .
59005003	Your gold and silver are corroded . Their corrosion will testify against you and eat your flesh like fire . You have hoarded wealth in the last days .
59005004	Look ! The wages you failed to pay the workers who mowed your fields are crying out against you . The cries of the harvesters have reached the ears of the Lord Almighty .
59005005	You have lived on earth in luxury and self-indulgence . You have fattened yourselves in the day of slaughter .
59005006	You have condemned and murdered the innocent one , who was not opposing you .
59005007	Be patient , then , brothers and sisters , until the Lord's coming . See how the farmer waits for the land to yield its valuable crop , patiently waiting for the autumn and spring rains .
59005008	You too , be patient and stand firm , because the Lord's coming is near .
59005009	Don't grumble against one another , brothers and sisters , or you will be judged . The Judge is standing at the door !
59005010	Brothers and sisters , as an example of patience in the face of suffering , take the prophets who spoke in the name of the Lord .
59005011	As you know , we count as blessed those who have persevered . You have heard of Job's perseverance and have seen what the Lord finally brought about . The Lord is full of compassion and mercy .
59005012	Above all , my brothers and sisters , do not swear — not by heaven or by earth or by anything else . All you need to say is a simple " Yes " or " No . " Otherwise you will be condemned .
59005013	Is anyone among you in trouble ? Let them pray . Is anyone happy ? Let them sing songs of praise .
59005014	Is anyone among you sick ? Let them call the elders of the church to pray over them and anoint them with oil in the name of the Lord .
59005015	And the prayer offered in faith will make the sick person well ; the Lord will raise them up . If they have sinned , they will be forgiven .
59005016	Therefore confess your sins to each other and pray for each other so that you may be healed . The prayer of a righteous person is powerful and effective .
59005017	Elijah was a human being , even as we are . He prayed earnestly that it would not rain , and it did not rain on the land for three and a half years .
59005018	Again he prayed , and the heavens gave rain , and the earth produced its crops .
59005019	My brothers and sisters , if one of you should wander from the truth and someone should bring that person back ,
59005020	remember this : Whoever turns a sinner from the error of their way will save them from death and cover over a multitude of sins .
60001001	Peter , an apostle of Jesus Christ , To God's elect , exiles scattered throughout the provinces of Pontus , Galatia , Cappadocia , Asia and Bithynia ,
60001002	who have been chosen according to the foreknowledge of God the Father , through the sanctifying work of the Spirit , to be obedient to Jesus Christ and sprinkled with his blood : Grace and peace be yours in abundance .
60001003	Praise be to the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ ! In his great mercy he has given us new birth into a living hope through the resurrection of Jesus Christ from the dead ,
60001004	and into an inheritance that can never perish , spoil or fade . This inheritance is kept in heaven for you ,
60001005	who through faith are shielded by God's power until the coming of the salvation that is ready to be revealed in the last time .
60001006	In all this you greatly rejoice , though now for a little while you may have had to suffer grief in all kinds of trials .
60001007	These have come so that the proven genuineness of your faith — of greater worth than gold , which perishes even though refined by fire — may result in praise , glory and honor when Jesus Christ is revealed .
60001008	Though you have not seen him , you love him ; and even though you do not see him now , you believe in him and are filled with an inexpressible and glorious joy ,
60001009	for you are receiving the end result of your faith , the salvation of your souls .
60001010	Concerning this salvation , the prophets , who spoke of the grace that was to come to you , searched intently and with the greatest care ,
60001011	trying to find out the time and circumstances to which the Spirit of Christ in them was pointing when he predicted the sufferings of the Messiah and the glories that would follow .
60001012	It was revealed to them that they were not serving themselves but you , when they spoke of the things that have now been told you by those who have preached the gospel to you by the Holy Spirit sent from heaven . Even angels long to look into these things .
60001013	Therefore , with minds that are alert and fully sober , set your hope on the grace to be brought to you when Jesus Christ is revealed at his coming .
60001014	As obedient children , do not conform to the evil desires you had when you lived in ignorance .
60001015	But just as he who called you is holy , so be holy in all you do ;
60001016	for it is written : " Be holy , because I am holy . "
60001017	Since you call on a Father who judges each person's work impartially , live out your time as foreigners here in reverent fear .
60001018	For you know that it was not with perishable things such as silver or gold that you were redeemed from the empty way of life handed down to you from your ancestors ,
60001019	but with the precious blood of Christ , a lamb without blemish or defect .
60001020	He was chosen before the creation of the world , but was revealed in these last times for your sake .
60001021	Through him you believe in God , who raised him from the dead and glorified him , and so your faith and hope are in God .
60001022	Now that you have purified yourselves by obeying the truth so that you have sincere love for each other , love one another deeply , from the heart .
60001023	For you have been born again , not of perishable seed , but of imperishable , through the living and enduring word of God .
60001024	For , " All people are like grass , and all their glory is like the flowers of the field ; the grass withers and the flowers fall ,
60001025	but the word of the Lord endures forever . " And this is the word that was preached to you .
60002001	Therefore , rid yourselves of all malice and all deceit , hypocrisy , envy , and slander of every kind .
60002002	Like newborn babies , crave pure spiritual milk , so that by it you may grow up in your salvation ,
60002003	now that you have tasted that the Lord is good .
60002004	As you come to him , the living Stone — rejected by humans but chosen by God and precious to him —
60002005	you also , like living stones , are being built into a spiritual house to be a holy priesthood , offering spiritual sacrifices acceptable to God through Jesus Christ .
60002006	For in Scripture it says : " See , I lay a stone in Zion , a chosen and precious cornerstone , and the one who trusts in him will never be put to shame . "
60002007	Now to you who believe , this stone is precious . But to those who do not believe , " The stone the builders rejected has become the cornerstone , "
60002008	and , " A stone that causes people to stumble and a rock that makes them fall . " They stumble because they disobey the message — which is also what they were destined for .
60002009	But you are a chosen people , a royal priesthood , a holy nation , God's special possession , that you may declare the praises of him who called you out of darkness into his wonderful light .
60002010	Once you were not a people , but now you are the people of God ; once you had not received mercy , but now you have received mercy .
60002011	Dear friends , I urge you , as foreigners and exiles , to abstain from sinful desires , which wage war against your soul .
60002012	Live such good lives among the pagans that , though they accuse you of doing wrong , they may see your good deeds and glorify God on the day he visits us .
60002013	Submit yourselves for the Lord's sake to every human authority : whether to the emperor , as the supreme authority ,
60002014	or to governors , who are sent by him to punish those who do wrong and to commend those who do right .
60002015	For it is God's will that by doing good you should silence the ignorant talk of foolish people .
60002016	Live as free people , but do not use your freedom as a cover-up for evil ; live as God's slaves .
60002017	Show proper respect to everyone , love the family of believers , fear God , honor the emperor .
60002018	Slaves , in reverent fear of God submit yourselves to your masters , not only to those who are good and considerate , but also to those who are harsh .
60002019	For it is commendable if someone bears up under the pain of unjust suffering because they are conscious of God .
60002020	But how is it to your credit if you receive a beating for doing wrong and endure it ? But if you suffer for doing good and you endure it , this is commendable before God .
60002021	To this you were called , because Christ suffered for you , leaving you an example , that you should follow in his steps .
60002022	" He committed no sin , and no deceit was found in his mouth . "
60002023	When they hurled their insults at him , he did not retaliate ; when he suffered , he made no threats . Instead , he entrusted himself to him who judges justly .
60002024	" He himself bore our sins " in his body on the cross , so that we might die to sins and live for righteousness ; " by his wounds you have been healed . "
60002025	For " you were like sheep going astray , " but now you have returned to the Shepherd and Overseer of your souls .
60003001	Wives , in the same way submit yourselves to your own husbands so that , if any of them do not believe the word , they may be won over without words by the behavior of their wives ,
60003002	when they see the purity and reverence of your lives .
60003003	Your beauty should not come from outward adornment , such as elaborate hairstyles and the wearing of gold jewelry or fine clothes .
60003004	Rather , it should be that of your inner self , the unfading beauty of a gentle and quiet spirit , which is of great worth in God's sight .
60003005	For this is the way the holy women of the past who put their hope in God used to adorn themselves . They submitted themselves to their own husbands ,
60003006	like Sarah , who obeyed Abraham and called him her lord . You are her daughters if you do what is right and do not give way to fear .
60003007	Husbands , in the same way be considerate as you live with your wives , and treat them with respect as the weaker partner and as heirs with you of the gracious gift of life , so that nothing will hinder your prayers .
60003008	Finally , all of you , be like-minded , be sympathetic , love one another , be compassionate and humble .
60003009	Do not repay evil with evil or insult with insult . On the contrary , repay evil with blessing , because to this you were called so that you may inherit a blessing .
60003010	For , " Whoever would love life and see good days must keep their tongue from evil and their lips from deceitful speech .
60003011	They must turn from evil and do good ; they must seek peace and pursue it .
60003012	For the eyes of the Lord are on the righteous and his ears are attentive to their prayer , but the face of the Lord is against those who do evil . "
60003013	Who is going to harm you if you are eager to do good ?
60003014	But even if you should suffer for what is right , you are blessed . " Do not fear their threats ; do not be frightened . "
60003015	But in your hearts revere Christ as Lord . Always be prepared to give an answer to everyone who asks you to give the reason for the hope that you have . But do this with gentleness and respect ,
60003016	keeping a clear conscience , so that those who speak maliciously against your good behavior in Christ may be ashamed of their slander .
60003017	For it is better , if it is God's will , to suffer for doing good than for doing evil .
60003018	For Christ also suffered once for sins , the righteous for the unrighteous , to bring you to God . He was put to death in the body but made alive in the Spirit .
60003019	After being made alive , he went and made proclamation to the imprisoned spirits —
60003020	to those who were disobedient long ago when God waited patiently in the days of Noah while the ark was being built . In it only a few people , eight in all , were saved through water ,
60003021	and this water symbolizes baptism that now saves you also — not the removal of dirt from the body but the pledge of a clear conscience toward God . It saves you by the resurrection of Jesus Christ ,
60003022	who has gone into heaven and is at God's right hand — with angels , authorities and powers in submission to him .
60004001	Therefore , since Christ suffered in his body , arm yourselves also with the same attitude , because whoever suffers in the body is done with sin .
60004002	As a result , they do not live the rest of their earthly lives for evil human desires , but rather for the will of God .
60004003	For you have spent enough time in the past doing what pagans choose to do — living in debauchery , lust , drunkenness , orgies , carousing and detestable idolatry .
60004004	They are surprised that you do not join them in their reckless , wild living , and they heap abuse on you .
60004005	But they will have to give account to him who is ready to judge the living and the dead .
60004006	For this is the reason the gospel was preached even to those who are now dead , so that they might be judged according to human standards in regard to the body , but live according to God in regard to the spirit .
60004007	The end of all things is near . Therefore be alert and of sober mind so that you may pray .
60004008	Above all , love each other deeply , because love covers over a multitude of sins .
60004009	Offer hospitality to one another without grumbling .
60004010	Each of you should use whatever gift you have received to serve others , as faithful stewards of God's grace in its various forms .
60004011	If anyone speaks , they should do so as one who speaks the very words of God . If anyone serves , they should do so with the strength God provides , so that in all things God may be praised through Jesus Christ . To him be the glory and the power for ever and ever . Amen .
60004012	Dear friends , do not be surprised at the fiery ordeal that has come on you to test you , as though something strange were happening to you .
60004013	But rejoice inasmuch as you participate in the sufferings of Christ , so that you may be overjoyed when his glory is revealed .
60004014	If you are insulted because of the name of Christ , you are blessed , for the Spirit of glory and of God rests on you .
60004015	If you suffer , it should not be as a murderer or thief or any other kind of criminal , or even as a meddler .
60004016	However , if you suffer as a Christian , do not be ashamed , but praise God that you bear that name .
60004017	For it is time for judgment to begin with God's household ; and if it begins with us , what will the outcome be for those who do not obey the gospel of God ?
60004018	And , " If it is hard for the righteous to be saved , what will become of the ungodly and the sinner ? "
60004019	So then , those who suffer according to God's will should commit themselves to their faithful Creator and continue to do good .
60005001	To the elders among you , I appeal as a fellow elder and a witness of Christ's sufferings who also will share in the glory to be revealed :
60005002	Be shepherds of God's flock that is under your care , watching over them — not because you must , but because you are willing , as God wants you to be ; not pursuing dishonest gain , but eager to serve ;
60005003	not lording it over those entrusted to you , but being examples to the flock .
60005004	And when the Chief Shepherd appears , you will receive the crown of glory that will never fade away .
60005005	In the same way , you who are younger , submit yourselves to your elders . All of you , clothe yourselves with humility toward one another , because ,
60005006	Humble yourselves , therefore , under God's mighty hand , that he may lift you up in due time .
60005007	Cast all your anxiety on him because he cares for you .
60005008	Be alert and of sober mind . Your enemy the devil prowls around like a roaring lion looking for someone to devour .
60005009	Resist him , standing firm in the faith , because you know that the family of believers throughout the world is undergoing the same kind of sufferings .
60005010	And the God of all grace , who called you to his eternal glory in Christ , after you have suffered a little while , will himself restore you and make you strong , firm and steadfast .
60005011	To him be the power for ever and ever . Amen .
60005012	With the help of Silas , whom I regard as a faithful brother , I have written to you briefly , encouraging you and testifying that this is the true grace of God . Stand fast in it .
60005013	She who is in Babylon , chosen together with you , sends you her greetings , and so does my son Mark .
60005014	Greet one another with a kiss of love . Peace to all of you who are in Christ .
61001001	Simon Peter , a servant and apostle of Jesus Christ , To those who through the righteousness of our God and Savior Jesus Christ have received a faith as precious as ours :
61001002	Grace and peace be yours in abundance through the knowledge of God and of Jesus our Lord .
61001003	His divine power has given us everything we need for a godly life through our knowledge of him who called us by his own glory and goodness .
61001004	Through these he has given us his very great and precious promises , so that through them you may participate in the divine nature , having escaped the corruption in the world caused by evil desires .
61001005	For this very reason , make every effort to add to your faith goodness ; and to goodness , knowledge ;
61001006	and to knowledge , self-control ; and to self-control , perseverance ; and to perseverance , godliness ;
61001007	and to godliness , mutual affection ; and to mutual affection , love .
61001008	For if you possess these qualities in increasing measure , they will keep you from being ineffective and unproductive in your knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ .
61001009	But whoever does not have them is nearsighted and blind , forgetting that they have been cleansed from their past sins .
61001010	Therefore , my brothers and sisters , make every effort to confirm your calling and election . For if you do these things , you will never stumble ,
61001011	and you will receive a rich welcome into the eternal kingdom of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ .
61001012	So I will always remind you of these things , even though you know them and are firmly established in the truth you now have .
61001013	I think it is right to refresh your memory as long as I live in the tent of this body ,
61001014	because I know that I will soon put it aside , as our Lord Jesus Christ has made clear to me .
61001015	And I will make every effort to see that after my departure you will always be able to remember these things .
61001016	For we did not follow cleverly devised stories when we told you about the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ in power , but we were eyewitnesses of his majesty .
61001017	He received honor and glory from God the Father when the voice came to him from the Majestic Glory , saying , " This is my Son , whom I love ; with him I am well pleased . "
61001018	We ourselves heard this voice that came from heaven when we were with him on the sacred mountain .
61001019	We also have the prophetic message as something completely reliable , and you will do well to pay attention to it , as to a light shining in a dark place , until the day dawns and the morning star rises in your hearts .
61001020	Above all , you must understand that no prophecy of Scripture came about by the prophet's own interpretation of things .
61001021	For prophecy never had its origin in the human will , but prophets , though human , spoke from God as they were carried along by the Holy Spirit .
61002001	But there were also false prophets among the people , just as there will be false teachers among you . They will secretly introduce destructive heresies , even denying the sovereign Lord who bought them — bringing swift destruction on themselves .
61002002	Many will follow their depraved conduct and will bring the way of truth into disrepute .
61002003	In their greed these teachers will exploit you with fabricated stories . Their condemnation has long been hanging over them , and their destruction has not been sleeping .
61002004	For if God did not spare angels when they sinned , but sent them to hell , putting them in chains of darkness to be held for judgment ;
61002005	if he did not spare the ancient world when he brought the flood on its ungodly people , but protected Noah , a preacher of righteousness , and seven others ;
61002006	if he condemned the cities of Sodom and Gomorrah by burning them to ashes , and made them an example of what is going to happen to the ungodly ;
61002007	and if he rescued Lot , a righteous man , who was distressed by the depraved conduct of the lawless
61002008	( for that righteous man , living among them day after day , was tormented in his righteous soul by the lawless deeds he saw and heard ) —
61002009	if this is so , then the Lord knows how to rescue the godly from trials and to hold the unrighteous for punishment on the day of judgment .
61002010	This is especially true of those who follow the corrupt desire of the flesh and despise authority . Bold and arrogant , they are not afraid to heap abuse on celestial beings ;
61002011	yet even angels , although they are stronger and more powerful , do not heap abuse on such beings when bringing judgment on them from the Lord .
61002012	But these people blaspheme in matters they do not understand . They are like unreasoning animals , creatures of instinct , born only to be caught and destroyed , and like animals they too will perish .
61002013	They will be paid back with harm for the harm they have done . Their idea of pleasure is to carouse in broad daylight . They are blots and blemishes , reveling in their pleasures while they feast with you .
61002014	With eyes full of adultery , they never stop sinning ; they seduce the unstable ; they are experts in greed — an accursed brood !
61002015	They have left the straight way and wandered off to follow the way of Balaam son of Bezer , who loved the wages of wickedness .
61002016	But he was rebuked for his wrongdoing by a donkey — an animal without speech — who spoke with a human voice and restrained the prophet's madness .
61002017	These people are springs without water and mists driven by a storm . Blackest darkness is reserved for them .
61002018	For they mouth empty , boastful words and , by appealing to the lustful desires of the flesh , they entice people who are just escaping from those who live in error .
61002019	They promise them freedom , while they themselves are slaves of depravity — for " people are slaves to whatever has mastered them . "
61002020	If they have escaped the corruption of the world by knowing our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ and are again entangled in it and are overcome , they are worse off at the end than they were at the beginning .
61002021	It would have been better for them not to have known the way of righteousness , than to have known it and then to turn their backs on the sacred command that was passed on to them .
61002022	Of them the proverbs are true : " A dog returns to its vomit , " and , " A sow that is washed returns to her wallowing in the mud . "
61003001	Dear friends , this is now my second letter to you . I have written both of them as reminders to stimulate you to wholesome thinking .
61003002	I want you to recall the words spoken in the past by the holy prophets and the command given by our Lord and Savior through your apostles .
61003003	Above all , you must understand that in the last days scoffers will come , scoffing and following their own evil desires .
61003004	They will say , " Where is this ' coming ' he promised ? Ever since our ancestors died , everything goes on as it has since the beginning of creation . "
61003005	But they deliberately forget that long ago by God's word the heavens came into being and the earth was formed out of water and by water .
61003006	By these waters also the world of that time was deluged and destroyed .
61003007	By the same word the present heavens and earth are reserved for fire , being kept for the day of judgment and destruction of the ungodly .
61003008	But do not forget this one thing , dear friends : With the Lord a day is like a thousand years , and a thousand years are like a day .
61003009	The Lord is not slow in keeping his promise , as some understand slowness . Instead he is patient with you , not wanting anyone to perish , but everyone to come to repentance .
61003010	But the day of the Lord will come like a thief . The heavens will disappear with a roar ; the elements will be destroyed by fire , and the earth and everything done in it will be laid bare .
61003011	Since everything will be destroyed in this way , what kind of people ought you to be ? You ought to live holy and godly lives
61003012	as you look forward to the day of God and speed its coming . That day will bring about the destruction of the heavens by fire , and the elements will melt in the heat .
61003013	But in keeping with his promise we are looking forward to a new heaven and a new earth , where righteousness dwells .
61003014	So then , dear friends , since you are looking forward to this , make every effort to be found spotless , blameless and at peace with him .
61003015	Bear in mind that our Lord's patience means salvation , just as our dear brother Paul also wrote you with the wisdom that God gave him .
61003016	He writes the same way in all his letters , speaking in them of these matters . His letters contain some things that are hard to understand , which ignorant and unstable people distort , as they do the other Scriptures , to their own destruction .
61003017	Therefore , dear friends , since you have been forewarned , be on your guard so that you may not be carried away by the error of the lawless and fall from your secure position .
61003018	But grow in the grace and knowledge of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ . To him be glory both now and forever ! Amen .
62001001	That which was from the beginning , which we have heard , which we have seen with our eyes , which we have looked at and our hands have touched — this we proclaim concerning the Word of life .
62001002	The life appeared ; we have seen it and testify to it , and we proclaim to you the eternal life , which was with the Father and has appeared to us .
62001003	We proclaim to you what we have seen and heard , so that you also may have fellowship with us . And our fellowship is with the Father and with his Son , Jesus Christ .
62001004	We write this to make our joy complete .
62001005	This is the message we have heard from him and declare to you : God is light ; in him there is no darkness at all .
62001006	If we claim to have fellowship with him and yet walk in the darkness , we lie and do not live out the truth .
62001007	But if we walk in the light , as he is in the light , we have fellowship with one another , and the blood of Jesus , his Son , purifies us from all sin .
62001008	If we claim to be without sin , we deceive ourselves and the truth is not in us .
62001009	If we confess our sins , he is faithful and just and will forgive us our sins and purify us from all unrighteousness .
62001010	If we claim we have not sinned , we make him out to be a liar and his word is not in us .
62002001	My dear children , I write this to you so that you will not sin . But if anybody does sin , we have an advocate with the Father — Jesus Christ , the Righteous One .
62002002	He is the atoning sacrifice for our sins , and not only for ours but also for the sins of the whole world .
62002003	We know that we have come to know him if we keep his commands .
62002004	Whoever says , " I know him , " but does not do what he commands is a liar , and the truth is not in that person .
62002005	But if anyone obeys his word , love for God is truly made complete in them . This is how we know we are in him :
62002006	Whoever claims to live in him must live as Jesus did .
62002007	Dear friends , I am not writing you a new command but an old one , which you have had since the beginning . This old command is the message you have heard .
62002008	Yet I am writing you a new command ; its truth is seen in him and in you , because the darkness is passing and the true light is already shining .
62002009	Anyone who claims to be in the light but hates a brother or sister is still in the darkness .
62002010	Anyone who loves their brother and sister lives in the light , and there is nothing in them to make them stumble .
62002011	But anyone who hates a brother or sister is in the darkness and walks around in the darkness . They do not know where they are going , because the darkness has blinded them .
62002012	I am writing to you , dear children ,
62002014	I write to you , dear children ,
62002015	Do not love the world or anything in the world . If anyone loves the world , love for the Father is not in them .
62002016	For everything in the world — the lust of the flesh , the lust of the eyes , and the pride of life — comes not from the Father but from the world .
62002017	The world and its desires pass away , but whoever does the will of God lives forever .
62002018	Dear children , this is the last hour ; and as you have heard that the antichrist is coming , even now many antichrists have come . This is how we know it is the last hour .
62002019	They went out from us , but they did not really belong to us . For if they had belonged to us , they would have remained with us ; but their going showed that none of them belonged to us .
62002020	But you have an anointing from the Holy One , and all of you know the truth .
62002021	I do not write to you because you do not know the truth , but because you do know it and because no lie comes from the truth .
62002022	Who is the liar ? It is whoever denies that Jesus is the Christ . Such a person is the antichrist — denying the Father and the Son .
62002023	No one who denies the Son has the Father ; whoever acknowledges the Son has the Father also .
62002024	As for you , see that what you have heard from the beginning remains in you . If it does , you also will remain in the Son and in the Father .
62002025	And this is what he promised us — eternal life .
62002026	I am writing these things to you about those who are trying to lead you astray .
62002027	As for you , the anointing you received from him remains in you , and you do not need anyone to teach you . But as his anointing teaches you about all things and as that anointing is real , not counterfeit — just as it has taught you , remain in him .
62002028	And now , dear children , continue in him , so that when he appears we may be confident and unashamed before him at his coming .
62002029	If you know that he is righteous , you know that everyone who does what is right has been born of him .
62003001	See what great love the Father has lavished on us , that we should be called children of God ! And that is what we are ! The reason the world does not know us is that it did not know him .
62003002	Dear friends , now we are children of God , and what we will be has not yet been made known . But we know that when Christ appears , we shall be like him , for we shall see him as he is .
62003003	All who have this hope in him purify themselves , just as he is pure .
62003004	Everyone who sins breaks the law ; in fact , sin is lawlessness .
62003005	But you know that he appeared so that he might take away our sins . And in him is no sin .
62003006	No one who lives in him keeps on sinning . No one who continues to sin has either seen him or known him .
62003007	Dear children , do not let anyone lead you astray . The one who does what is right is righteous , just as he is righteous .
62003008	The one who does what is sinful is of the devil , because the devil has been sinning from the beginning . The reason the Son of God appeared was to destroy the devil's work .
62003009	No one who is born of God will continue to sin , because God's seed remains in them ; they cannot go on sinning , because they have been born of God .
62003010	This is how we know who the children of God are and who the children of the devil are : Anyone who does not do what is right is not God's child , nor is anyone who does not love their brother and sister .
62003011	For this is the message you heard from the beginning : We should love one another .
62003012	Do not be like Cain , who belonged to the evil one and murdered his brother . And why did he murder him ? Because his own actions were evil and his brother's were righteous .
62003013	Do not be surprised , my brothers and sisters , if the world hates you .
62003014	We know that we have passed from death to life , because we love each other . Anyone who does not love remains in death .
62003015	Anyone who hates a brother or sister is a murderer , and you know that no murderer has eternal life residing in him .
62003016	This is how we know what love is : Jesus Christ laid down his life for us . And we ought to lay down our lives for our brothers and sisters .
62003017	If anyone has material possessions and sees a brother or sister in need but has no pity on them , how can the love of God be that person ?
62003018	Dear children , let us not love with words or speech but with actions and in truth .
62003019	This is how we know that we belong to the truth and how we set our hearts at rest in his presence :
62003020	If our hearts condemn us , we know that God is greater than our hearts , and he knows everything .
62003021	Dear friends , if our hearts do not condemn us , we have confidence before God
62003022	and receive from him anything we ask , because we keep his commands and do what pleases him .
62003023	And this is his command : to believe in the name of his Son , Jesus Christ , and to love one another as he commanded us .
62003024	The one who keeps God's commands lives in him , and he in them . And this is how we know that he lives in us : We know it by the Spirit he gave us .
62004001	Dear friends , do not believe every spirit , but test the spirits to see whether they are from God , because many false prophets have gone out into the world .
62004002	This is how you can recognize the Spirit of God : Every spirit that acknowledges that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is from God ,
62004003	but every spirit that does not acknowledge Jesus is not from God . This is the spirit of the antichrist , which you have heard is coming and even now is already in the world .
62004004	You , dear children , are from God and have overcome them , because the one who is in you is greater than the one who is in the world .
