62004005	They are from the world and therefore speak from the viewpoint of the world , and the world listens to them .
62004006	We are from God , and whoever knows God listens to us ; but whoever is not from God does not listen to us . This is how we recognize the Spirit of truth and the spirit of falsehood .
62004007	Dear friends , let us love one another , for love comes from God . Everyone who loves has been born of God and knows God .
62004008	Whoever does not love does not know God , because God is love .
62004009	This is how God showed his love among us : He sent his one and only Son into the world that we might live through him .
62004010	This is love : not that we loved God , but that he loved us and sent his Son as an atoning sacrifice for our sins .
62004011	Dear friends , since God so loved us , we also ought to love one another .
62004012	No one has ever seen God ; but if we love one another , God lives in us and his love is made complete in us .
62004013	This is how we know that we live in him and he in us : He has given us of his Spirit .
62004014	And we have seen and testify that the Father has sent his Son to be the Savior of the world .
62004015	If anyone acknowledges that Jesus is the Son of God , God lives in them and they in God .
62004016	And so we know and rely on the love God has for us . God is love . Whoever lives in love lives in God , and God in them .
62004017	This is how love is made complete among us so that we will have confidence on the day of judgment : In this world we are like Jesus .
62004018	There is no fear in love . But perfect love drives out fear , because fear has to do with punishment . The one who fears is not made perfect in love .
62004019	We love because he first loved us .
62004020	Whoever claims to love God yet hates a brother or sister is a liar . For whoever does not love their brother and sister , whom they have seen , cannot love God , whom they have not seen .
62004021	And he has given us this command : Anyone who loves God must also love their brother and sister .
62005001	Everyone who believes that Jesus is the Christ is born of God , and everyone who loves the father loves his child as well .
62005002	This is how we know that we love the children of God : by loving God and carrying out his commands .
62005003	In fact , this is love for God : to keep his commands . And his commands are not burdensome ,
62005004	for everyone born of God overcomes the world . This is the victory that has overcome the world , even our faith .
62005005	Who is it that overcomes the world ? Only the one who believes that Jesus is the Son of God .
62005006	This is the one who came by water and blood — Jesus Christ . He did not come by water only , but by water and blood . And it is the Spirit who testifies , because the Spirit is the truth .
62005007	For there are three that testify :
62005008	the Spirit , the water and the blood ; and the three are in agreement .
62005009	We accept human testimony , but God's testimony is greater because it is the testimony of God , which he has given about his Son .
62005010	Whoever believes in the Son of God accepts this testimony . Whoever does not believe God has made him out to be a liar , because they have not believed the testimony God has given about his Son .
62005011	And this is the testimony : God has given us eternal life , and this life is in his Son .
62005012	Whoever has the Son has life ; whoever does not have the Son of God does not have life .
62005013	I write these things to you who believe in the name of the Son of God so that you may know that you have eternal life .
62005014	This is the confidence we have in approaching God : that if we ask anything according to his will , he hears us .
62005015	And if we know that he hears us — whatever we ask — we know that we have what we asked of him .
62005016	If you see any brother or sister commit a sin that does not lead to death , you should pray and God will give them life . I refer to those whose sin does not lead to death . There is a sin that leads to death . I am not saying that you should pray about that .
62005017	All wrongdoing is sin , and there is sin that does not lead to death .
62005018	We know that anyone born of God does not continue to sin ; the One who was born of God keeps them safe , and the evil one cannot harm them .
62005019	We know that we are children of God , and that the whole world is under the control of the evil one .
62005020	We know also that the Son of God has come and has given us understanding , so that we may know him who is true . And we are in him who is true by being in his Son Jesus Christ . He is the true God and eternal life .
62005021	Dear children , keep yourselves from idols .
63001001	The elder , To the lady chosen by God and to her children , whom I love in the truth — and not I only , but also all who know the truth —
63001002	because of the truth , which lives in us and will be with us forever :
63001003	Grace , mercy and peace from God the Father and from Jesus Christ , the Father's Son , will be with us in truth and love .
63001004	It has given me great joy to find some of your children walking in the truth , just as the Father commanded us .
63001005	And now , dear lady , I am not writing you a new command but one we have had from the beginning . I ask that we love one another .
63001006	And this is love : that we walk in obedience to his commands . As you have heard from the beginning , his command is that you walk in love .
63001007	I say this because many deceivers , who do not acknowledge Jesus Christ as coming in the flesh , have gone out into the world . Any such person is the deceiver and the antichrist .
63001008	Watch out that you do not lose what we have worked for , but that you may be rewarded fully .
63001009	Anyone who runs ahead and does not continue in the teaching of Christ does not have God ; whoever continues in the teaching has both the Father and the Son .
63001010	If anyone comes to you and does not bring this teaching , do not take them into your house or welcome them .
63001011	Anyone who welcomes them shares in their wicked work .
63001012	I have much to write to you , but I do not want to use paper and ink . Instead , I hope to visit you and talk with you face to face , so that our joy may be complete .
63001013	The children of your sister , who is chosen by God , send their greetings .
64001001	The elder , To my dear friend Gaius , whom I love in the truth .
64001002	Dear friend , I pray that you may enjoy good health and that all may go well with you , even as your soul is getting along well .
64001003	It gave me great joy when some believers came and testified about your faithfulness to the truth , telling how you continue to walk in it .
64001004	I have no greater joy than to hear that my children are walking in the truth .
64001005	Dear friend , you are faithful in what you are doing for the brothers and sisters , even though they are strangers to you .
64001006	They have told the church about your love . Please send them on their way in a manner that honors God .
64001007	It was for the sake of the Name that they went out , receiving no help from the pagans .
64001008	We ought therefore to show hospitality to such people so that we may work together for the truth .
64001009	I wrote to the church , but Diotrephes , who loves to be first , will not welcome us .
64001010	So when I come , I will call attention to what he is doing , spreading malicious nonsense about us . Not satisfied with that , he even refuses to welcome other believers . He also stops those who want to do so and puts them out of the church .
64001011	Dear friend , do not imitate what is evil but what is good . Anyone who does what is good is from God . Anyone who does what is evil has not seen God .
64001012	Demetrius is well spoken of by everyone — and even by the truth itself . We also speak well of him , and you know that our testimony is true .
64001013	I have much to write you , but I do not want to do so with pen and ink .
64001014	I hope to see you soon , and we will talk face to face . Peace to you . The friends here send their greetings . Greet the friends there by name .

65001001	Jude , a servant of Jesus Christ and a brother of James , To those who have been called , who are loved in God the Father and kept for Jesus Christ :
65001002	Mercy , peace and love be yours in abundance .
65001003	Dear friends , although I was very eager to write to you about the salvation we share , I felt compelled to write and urge you to contend for the faith that was once for all entrusted to God's holy people .
65001004	For certain individuals whose condemnation was written about long ago have secretly slipped in among you . They are ungodly people , who pervert the grace of our God into a license for immorality and deny Jesus Christ our only Sovereign and Lord .
65001005	Though you already know all this , I want to remind you that the Lord at one time delivered his people out of Egypt , but later destroyed those who did not believe .
65001006	And the angels who did not keep their positions of authority but abandoned their proper dwelling — these he has kept in darkness , bound with everlasting chains for judgment on the great Day .
65001007	In a similar way , Sodom and Gomorrah and the surrounding towns gave themselves up to sexual immorality and perversion . They serve as an example of those who suffer the punishment of eternal fire .
65001008	In the very same way , on the strength of their dreams these ungodly people pollute their own bodies , reject authority and heap abuse on celestial beings .
65001009	But even the archangel Michael , when he was disputing with the devil about the body of Moses , did not himself dare to condemn him for slander but said , " The Lord rebuke you ! "
65001010	Yet these people slander whatever they do not understand , and the very things they do understand by instinct — as irrational animals do — will destroy them .
65001011	Woe to them ! They have taken the way of Cain ; they have rushed for profit into Balaam's error ; they have been destroyed in Korah's rebellion .
65001012	These people are blemishes at your love feasts , eating with you without the slightest qualm — shepherds who feed only themselves . They are clouds without rain , blown along by the wind ; autumn trees , without fruit and uprooted — twice dead .
65001013	They are wild waves of the sea , foaming up their shame ; wandering stars , for whom blackest darkness has been reserved forever .
65001014	Enoch , the seventh from Adam , prophesied about them : " See , the Lord is coming with thousands upon thousands of his holy ones
65001015	to judge everyone , and to convict all of them of all the ungodly acts they have committed in their ungodliness , and of all the defiant words ungodly sinners have spoken against him . "
65001016	These people are grumblers and faultfinders ; they follow their own evil desires ; they boast about themselves and flatter others for their own advantage .
65001017	But , dear friends , remember what the apostles of our Lord Jesus Christ foretold .
65001018	They said to you , " In the last times there will be scoffers who will follow their own ungodly desires . "
65001019	These are the people who divide you , who follow mere natural instincts and do not have the Spirit .
65001020	But you , dear friends , by building yourselves up in your most holy faith and praying in the Holy Spirit ,
65001021	keep yourselves in God's love as you wait for the mercy of our Lord Jesus Christ to bring you to eternal life .
65001022	Be merciful to those who doubt ;
65001023	save others by snatching them from the fire ; to others show mercy , mixed with fear — hating even the clothing stained by corrupted flesh .
65001024	To him who is able to keep you from stumbling and to present you before his glorious presence without fault and with great joy —
65001025	to the only God our Savior be glory , majesty , power and authority , through Jesus Christ our Lord , before all ages , now and forevermore ! Amen .
66001001	The revelation from Jesus Christ , which God gave him to show his servants what must soon take place . He made it known by sending his angel to his servant John ,
66001002	who testifies to everything he saw — that is , the word of God and the testimony of Jesus Christ .
66001003	Blessed is the one who reads aloud the words of this prophecy , and blessed are those who hear it and take to heart what is written in it , because the time is near .

66001005	and from Jesus Christ , who is the faithful witness , the firstborn from the dead , and the ruler of the kings of the earth . To him who loves us and has freed us from our sins by his blood ,
66001006	and has made us to be a kingdom and priests to serve his God and Father — to him be glory and power for ever and ever ! Amen .
66001007	" Look , he is coming with the clouds , "
66001008	" I am the Alpha and the Omega , " says the Lord God , " who is , and who was , and who is to come , the Almighty . "
66001009	I , John , your brother and companion in the suffering and kingdom and patient endurance that are ours in Jesus , was on the island of Patmos because of the word of God and the testimony of Jesus .
66001010	On the Lord's Day I was in the Spirit , and I heard behind me a loud voice like a trumpet ,
66001011	which said : " Write on a scroll what you see and send it to the seven churches : to Ephesus , Smyrna , Pergamum , Thyatira , Sardis , Philadelphia and Laodicea . "
66001012	I turned around to see the voice that was speaking to me . And when I turned I saw seven golden lampstands ,
66001013	and among the lampstands was someone like a son of man , dressed in a robe reaching down to his feet and with a golden sash around his chest .
66001014	The hair on his head was white like wool , as white as snow , and his eyes were like blazing fire .
66001015	His feet were like bronze glowing in a furnace , and his voice was like the sound of rushing waters .
66001016	In his right hand he held seven stars , and coming out of his mouth was a sharp , double-edged sword . His face was like the sun shining in all its brilliance .
66001017	When I saw him , I fell at his feet as though dead . Then he placed his right hand on me and said : " Do not be afraid . I am the First and the Last .
66001018	I am the Living One ; I was dead , and now look , I am alive for ever and ever ! And I hold the keys of death and Hades .
66001019	" Write , therefore , what you have seen , what is now and what will take place later .
66001020	The mystery of the seven stars that you saw in my right hand and of the seven golden lampstands is this : The seven stars are the angels of the seven churches , and the seven lampstands are the seven churches .
66002001	" To the angel of the church in Ephesus write : These are the words of him who holds the seven stars in his right hand and walks among the seven golden lampstands .
66002002	I know your deeds , your hard work and your perseverance . I know that you cannot tolerate wicked people , that you have tested those who claim to be apostles but are not , and have found them false .
66002003	You have persevered and have endured hardships for my name , and have not grown weary .
66002004	Yet I hold this against you : You have forsaken the love you had at first .
66002005	Consider how far you have fallen ! Repent and do the things you did at first . If you do not repent , I will come to you and remove your lampstand from its place .
66002006	But you have this in your favor : You hate the practices of the Nicolaitans , which I also hate .
66002007	Whoever has ears , let them hear what the Spirit says to the churches . To the one who is victorious , I will give the right to eat from the tree of life , which is in the paradise of God .
66002008	" To the angel of the church in Smyrna write : These are the words of him who is the First and the Last , who died and came to life again .
66002009	I know your afflictions and your poverty — yet you are rich ! I know about the slander of those who say they are Jews and are not , but are a synagogue of Satan .
66002010	Do not be afraid of what you are about to suffer . I tell you , the devil will put some of you in prison to test you , and you will suffer persecution for ten days . Be faithful , even to the point of death , and I will give you life as your victor's crown .
66002011	Whoever has ears , let them hear what the Spirit says to the churches . The one who is victorious will not be hurt at all by the second death .
66002012	" To the angel of the church in Pergamum write : These are the words of him who has the sharp , double-edged sword .
66002013	I know where you live — where Satan has his throne . Yet you remain true to my name . You did not renounce your faith in me , not even in the days of Antipas , my faithful witness , who was put to death in your city — where Satan lives .
66002014	Nevertheless , I have a few things against you : There are some among you who hold to the teaching of Balaam , who taught Balak to entice the Israelites to sin so that they ate food sacrificed to idols and committed sexual immorality .
66002015	Likewise , you also have those who hold to the teaching of the Nicolaitans .
66002016	Repent therefore ! Otherwise , I will soon come to you and will fight against them with the sword of my mouth .

66002020	Nevertheless , I have this against you : You tolerate that woman Jezebel , who calls herself a prophet . By her teaching she misleads my servants into sexual immorality and the eating of food sacrificed to idols .
66002021	I have given her time to repent of her immorality , but she is unwilling .
66002022	So I will cast her on a bed of suffering , and I will make those who commit adultery with her suffer intensely , unless they repent of her ways .
66002023	I will strike her children dead . Then all the churches will know that I am he who searches hearts and minds , and I will repay each of you according to your deeds .
66002024	Now I say to the rest of you in Thyatira , to you who do not hold to her teaching and have not learned Satan's so-called deep secrets , ' I will not impose any other burden on you ,
66002025	except to hold on to what you have until I come . '

66002027	that one ' will rule them with an iron scepter and will dash them to pieces like pottery ' — just as I have received authority from my Father .
66002028	I will also give that one the morning star .

66003002	Wake up ! Strengthen what remains and is about to die , for I have found your deeds unfinished in the sight of my God .
66003003	Remember , therefore , what you have received and heard ; hold it fast , and repent . But if you do not wake up , I will come like a thief , and you will not know at what time I will come to you .
66003004	Yet you have a few people in Sardis who have not soiled their clothes . They will walk with me , dressed in white , for they are worthy .
66003005	The one who is victorious will , like them , be dressed in white . I will never blot out the name of that person from the book of life , but will acknowledge that name before my Father and his angels .

66003014	" To the angel of the church in Laodicea write : These are the words of the Amen , the faithful and true witness , the ruler of God's creation .
66003015	I know your deeds , that you are neither cold nor hot . I wish you were either one or the other !
66003016	So , because you are lukewarm — neither hot nor cold — I am about to spit you out of my mouth .
66003017	You say , ' I am rich ; I have acquired wealth and do not need a thing . ' But you do not realize that you are wretched , pitiful , poor , blind and naked .
66003018	I counsel you to buy from me gold refined in the fire , so you can become rich ; and white clothes to wear , so you can cover your shameful nakedness ; and salve to put on your eyes , so you can see .

66004001	After this I looked , and there before me was a door standing open in heaven . And the voice I had first heard speaking to me like a trumpet said , " Come up here , and I will show you what must take place after this . "
66004002	At once I was in the Spirit , and there before me was a throne in heaven with someone sitting on it .
66004003	And the one who sat there had the appearance of jasper and ruby . A rainbow that shone like an emerald encircled the throne .
66004004	Surrounding the throne were twenty-four other thrones , and seated on them were twenty-four elders . They were dressed in white and had crowns of gold on their heads .
66004005	From the throne came flashes of lightning , rumblings and peals of thunder . In front of the throne , seven lamps were blazing . These are the seven spirits of God .
66004006	Also in front of the throne there was what looked like a sea of glass , clear as crystal . In the center , around the throne , were four living creatures , and they were covered with eyes , in front and in back .
66004007	The first living creature was like a lion , the second was like an ox , the third had a face like a man , the fourth was like a flying eagle .
66004008	Each of the four living creatures had six wings and was covered with eyes all around , even under its wings . Day and night they never stop saying : " ' Holy , holy , holyis the Lord God Almighty , ' who was , and is , and is to come . "

66004010	the twenty-four elders fall down before him who sits on the throne and worship him who lives for ever and ever . They lay their crowns before the throne and say :
66004011	" You are worthy , our Lord and God ,

66005002	And I saw a mighty angel proclaiming in a loud voice , " Who is worthy to break the seals and open the scroll ? "
66005003	But no one in heaven or on earth or under the earth could open the scroll or even look inside it .
66005004	I wept and wept because no one was found who was worthy to open the scroll or look inside .
66005005	Then one of the elders said to me , " Do not weep ! See , the Lion of the tribe of Judah , the Root of David , has triumphed . He is able to open the scroll and its seven seals . "
66005006	Then I saw a Lamb , looking as if it had been slain , standing at the center of the throne , encircled by the four living creatures and the elders . The Lamb had seven horns and seven eyes , which are the seven spirits of God sent out into all the earth .
66005007	He went and took the scroll from the right hand of him who sat on the throne .
66005008	And when he had taken it , the four living creatures and the twenty-four elders fell down before the Lamb . Each one had a harp and they were holding golden bowls full of incense , which are the prayers of God's people .
66005009	And they sang a new song , saying :
66005011	Then I looked and heard the voice of many angels , numbering thousands upon thousands , and ten thousand times ten thousand . They encircled the throne and the living creatures and the elders .
66005012	In a loud voice they were saying :
66005014	The four living creatures said , " Amen , " and the elders fell down and worshiped .
66006001	I watched as the Lamb opened the first of the seven seals . Then I heard one of the four living creatures say in a voice like thunder , " Come ! "
66006002	I looked , and there before me was a white horse ! Its rider held a bow , and he was given a crown , and he rode out as a conqueror bent on conquest .
66006003	When the Lamb opened the second seal , I heard the second living creature say , " Come ! "
66006004	Then another horse came out , a fiery red one . Its rider was given power to take peace from the earth and to make people kill each other . To him was given a large sword .
66006005	When the Lamb opened the third seal , I heard the third living creature say , " Come ! " I looked , and there before me was a black horse ! Its rider was holding a pair of scales in his hand .
66006006	Then I heard what sounded like a voice among the four living creatures , saying , " Two pounds of wheat for a day's wages , and six pounds of barley for a day's wages , and do not damage the oil and the wine ! "
66006007	When the Lamb opened the fourth seal , I heard the voice of the fourth living creature say , " Come ! "
66006008	I looked , and there before me was a pale horse ! Its rider was named Death , and Hades was following close behind him . They were given power over a fourth of the earth to kill by sword , famine and plague , and by the wild beasts of the earth .
66006009	When he opened the fifth seal , I saw under the altar the souls of those who had been slain because of the word of God and the testimony they had maintained .
66006010	They called out in a loud voice , " How long , Sovereign Lord , holy and true , until you judge the inhabitants of the earth and avenge our blood ? "
66006011	Then each of them was given a white robe , and they were told to wait a little longer , until the full number of their fellow servants , their brothers and sisters , were killed just as they had been .
66006012	I watched as he opened the sixth seal . There was a great earthquake . The sun turned black like sackcloth made of goat hair , the whole moon turned blood red ,
66006013	and the stars in the sky fell to earth , as figs drop from a fig tree when shaken by a strong wind .
66006014	The heavens receded like a scroll being rolled up , and every mountain and island was removed from its place .
66006015	Then the kings of the earth , the princes , the generals , the rich , the mighty , and everyone else , both slave and free , hid in caves and among the rocks of the mountains .
66006016	They called to the mountains and the rocks , " Fall on us and hide us from the face of him who sits on the throne and from the wrath of the Lamb !
66006017	For the great day of their wrath has come , and who can withstand it ? "
66007001	After this I saw four angels standing at the four corners of the earth , holding back the four winds of the earth to prevent any wind from blowing on the land or on the sea or on any tree .
66007002	Then I saw another angel coming up from the east , having the seal of the living God . He called out in a loud voice to the four angels who had been given power to harm the land and the sea :
66007003	" Do not harm the land or the sea or the trees until we put a seal on the foreheads of the servants of our God . "
66007004	Then I heard the number of those who were sealed : 144,000 from all the tribes of Israel .

66008001	When he opened the seventh seal , there was silence in heaven for about half an hour .

66008012	The fourth angel sounded his trumpet , and a third of the sun was struck , a third of the moon , and a third of the stars , so that a third of them turned dark . A third of the day was without light , and also a third of the night .

66009001	The fifth angel sounded his trumpet , and I saw a star that had fallen from the sky to the earth . The star was given the key to the shaft of the Abyss .
66009002	When he opened the Abyss , smoke rose from it like the smoke from a gigantic furnace . The sun and sky were darkened by the smoke from the Abyss .
66009003	And out of the smoke locusts came down on the earth and were given power like that of scorpions of the earth .
66009004	They were told not to harm the grass of the earth or any plant or tree , but only those people who did not have the seal of God on their foreheads .
66009005	They were not allowed to kill them but only to torture them for five months . And the agony they suffered was like that of the sting of a scorpion when it strikes .
66009006	During those days people will seek death but will not find it ; they will long to die , but death will elude them .
66009007	The locusts looked like horses prepared for battle . On their heads they wore something like crowns of gold , and their faces resembled human faces .
66009008	Their hair was like women's hair , and their teeth were like lions' teeth .
66009009	They had breastplates like breastplates of iron , and the sound of their wings was like the thundering of many horses and chariots rushing into battle .
66009010	They had tails with stingers , like scorpions , and in their tails they had power to torment people for five months .
66009011	They had as king over them the angel of the Abyss , whose name in Hebrew is Abaddon and in Greek is Apollyon ( that is , Destroyer ) .
66009012	The first woe is past ; two other woes are yet to come .
66009013	The sixth angel sounded his trumpet , and I heard a voice coming from the four horns of the golden altar that is before God .

66009015	And the four angels who had been kept ready for this very hour and day and month and year were released to kill a third of mankind .
66009016	The number of the mounted troops was twice ten thousand times ten thousand . I heard their number .
66009017	The horses and riders I saw in my vision looked like this : Their breastplates were fiery red , dark blue , and yellow as sulfur . The heads of the horses resembled the heads of lions , and out of their mouths came fire , smoke and sulfur .
66009018	A third of mankind was killed by the three plagues of fire , smoke and sulfur that came out of their mouths .
66009019	The power of the horses was in their mouths and in their tails ; for their tails were like snakes , having heads with which they inflict injury .
66009020	The rest of mankind who were not killed by these plagues still did not repent of the work of their hands ; they did not stop worshiping demons , and idols of gold , silver , bronze , stone and wood — idols that cannot see or hear or walk .
66009021	Nor did they repent of their murders , their magic arts , their sexual immorality or their thefts .
66010001	Then I saw another mighty angel coming down from heaven . He was robed in a cloud , with a rainbow above his head ; his face was like the sun , and his legs were like fiery pillars .

66020013	The sea gave up the dead that were in it , and death and Hades gave up the dead that were in them , and each person was judged according to what they had done .
66020014	Then death and Hades were thrown into the lake of fire . The lake of fire is the second death .
66020015	Anyone whose name was not found written in the book of life was thrown into the lake of fire .
66021001	Then I saw " a new heaven and a new earth , " for the first heaven and the first earth had passed away , and there was no longer any sea .
66021002	I saw the Holy City , the new Jerusalem , coming down out of heaven from God , prepared as a bride beautifully dressed for her husband .
66021003	And I heard a loud voice from the throne saying , " Look ! God's dwelling place is now among the people , and he will dwell with them . They will be his people , and God himself will be with them and be their God .
66021004	' He will wipe every tear from their eyes . There will be no more death ' or mourning or crying or pain , for the old order of things has passed away . "
66021005	He who was seated on the throne said , " I am making everything new ! " Then he said , " Write this down , for these words are trustworthy and true . "
66021006	He said to me : " It is done . I am the Alpha and the Omega , the Beginning and the End . To the thirsty I will give water without cost from the spring of the water of life .
66021007	Those who are victorious will inherit all this , and I will be their God and they will be my children .
66021008	But the cowardly , the unbelieving , the vile , the murderers , the sexually immoral , those who practice magic arts , the idolaters and all liars — they will be consigned to the fiery lake of burning sulfur . This is the second death . "
66021009	One of the seven angels who had the seven bowls full of the seven last plagues came and said to me , " Come , I will show you the bride , the wife of the Lamb . "
66021010	And he carried me away in the Spirit to a mountain great and high , and showed me the Holy City , Jerusalem , coming down out of heaven from God .
66021011	It shone with the glory of God , and its brilliance was like that of a very precious jewel , like a jasper , clear as crystal .
66021012	It had a great , high wall with twelve gates , and with twelve angels at the gates . On the gates were written the names of the twelve tribes of Israel .
66021013	There were three gates on the east , three on the north , three on the south and three on the west .
66021014	The wall of the city had twelve foundations , and on them were the names of the twelve apostles of the Lamb .
66021015	The angel who talked with me had a measuring rod of gold to measure the city , its gates and its walls .
66021016	The city was laid out like a square , as long as it was wide . He measured the city with the rod and found it to be 12,000 stadia in length , and as wide and high as it is long .
66021017	The angel measured the wall using human measurement , and it was 144 cubits thick .
66021018	The wall was made of jasper , and the city of pure gold , as pure as glass .
66021019	The foundations of the city walls were decorated with every kind of precious stone . The first foundation was jasper , the second sapphire , the third agate , the fourth emerald ,
66021020	the fifth onyx , the sixth ruby , the seventh chrysolite , the eighth beryl , the ninth topaz , the tenth turquoise , the eleventh jacinth , and the twelfth amethyst .
66021021	The twelve gates were twelve pearls , each gate made of a single pearl . The great street of the city was of gold , as pure as transparent glass .
66021022	I did not see a temple in the city , because the Lord God Almighty and the Lamb are its temple .
66021023	The city does not need the sun or the moon to shine on it , for the glory of God gives it light , and the Lamb is its lamp .
66021024	The nations will walk by its light , and the kings of the earth will bring their splendor into it .
66021025	On no day will its gates ever be shut , for there will be no night there .
66021026	The glory and honor of the nations will be brought into it .
66021027	Nothing impure will ever enter it , nor will anyone who does what is shameful or deceitful , but only those whose names are written in the Lamb's book of life .
66022001	Then the angel showed me the river of the water of life , as clear as crystal , flowing from the throne of God and of the Lamb
66022002	down the middle of the great street of the city . On each side of the river stood the tree of life , bearing twelve crops of fruit , yielding its fruit every month . And the leaves of the tree are for the healing of the nations .
66022003	No longer will there be any curse . The throne of God and of the Lamb will be in the city , and his servants will serve him .
66022004	They will see his face , and his name will be on their foreheads .
66022005	There will be no more night . They will not need the light of a lamp or the light of the sun , for the Lord God will give them light . And they will reign for ever and ever .
66022006	The angel said to me , " These words are trustworthy and true . The Lord , the God who inspires the prophets , sent his angel to show his servants the things that must soon take place . "
66022007	" Look , I am coming soon ! Blessed is the one who keeps the words of the prophecy written in this scroll . "
66022008	I , John , am the one who heard and saw these things . And when I had heard and seen them , I fell down to worship at the feet of the angel who had been showing them to me .
66022009	But he said to me , " Don't do that ! I am a fellow servant with you and with your fellow prophets and with all who keep the words of this scroll . Worship God ! "
66022010	Then he told me , " Do not seal up the words of the prophecy of this scroll , because the time is near .
66022011	Let the one who does wrong continue to do wrong ; let the vile person continue to be vile ; let the one who does right continue to do right ; and let the holy person continue to be holy . "
66022012	" Look , I am coming soon ! My reward is with me , and I will give to each person according to what they have done .
66022013	I am the Alpha and the Omega , the First and the Last , the Beginning and the End .
66022014	" Blessed are those who wash their robes , that they may have the right to the tree of life and may go through the gates into the city .
66022015	Outside are the dogs , those who practice magic arts , the sexually immoral , the murderers , the idolaters and everyone who loves and practices falsehood .
66022016	" I , Jesus , have sent my angel to give you this testimony for the churches . I am the Root and the Offspring of David , and the bright Morning Star . "
66022017	The Spirit and the bride say , " Come ! " And let the one who hears say , " Come ! " Let the one who is thirsty come ; and let the one who wishes take the free gift of the water of life .
66022018	I warn everyone who hears the words of the prophecy of this scroll : If anyone adds anything to them , God will add to that person the plagues described in this scroll .
66022019	And if anyone takes words away from this scroll of prophecy , God will take away from that person any share in the tree of life and in the Holy City , which are described in this scroll .
66022020	He who testifies to these things says , " Yes , I am coming soon . " Amen . Come , Lord Jesus .
66022021	The grace of the Lord Jesus be with God's people . Amen .
